 
ben̪ami d̪bara b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ ibuk

ei ibukti d͡zekোn̪o d͡ʑae̯ɡae̯ bin̪a kʰɔrɔt͡ɕe ebɔŋ s̪at̪ʰe d͡ze karো bd͡zɔbɔharer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
prae̯ kɔোn̪ɔ bid̪̤in̪iʂed̪̤ n̪ei। apn̪i eti on̪ul̪ipi eti d̪ure d̪it̪e paren̪ ba
prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ l̪ais̪en̪s̪er ɕɔrt̪abl̪ir od̪̤in̪e eti pun̪rae̯ bd͡zɔbɔhar kɔrun̪ on̪t̪ɔrb̤ukt̪ɔ
ei ibuk s̪ɔhɔ ba on̪l̪ain̪ e


ɕirোn̪am b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɡit̪a

l̪ekʰɔkɔ ben̪ami

on̪ubad̪ɔkɔ s̪d͡zar eduin̪ arn̪ɔl̪dɔ

pɔোs̪tiŋ t̪arikʰ d͡ʑun̪ ibuk #
prɔkaɕer t̪arikʰ n̪ɔb̤embɔrɔ 
prɔt̪ʰɔmɔ pɔোs̪tɔ d͡ʑan̪ue̯ari 

b̤aʂa iŋred͡ʑi

okʂɔrɔ s̪et en̪ɔkɔোdiŋ ei prɔkɔl̪per ɕuru ɡuten̪barɡɔ b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɡit̪a ibuk ***




prɔd͡zɔোd͡ʑɔn̪a kɔret͡ɕʰen̪ d͡ʑes̪i bae̯ars̪ɔ। al̪ hain̪es̪er eit͡ɕtiemel̪ s̪ɔŋs̪kɔrɔnɔ।










d̪d͡zɔ
ɡan̪ s̪el̪es̪tie̯al̪।
ba
b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪a
mɔhab̤arɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰeke
ord͡ʑun̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze ekti bɔkt̪ɽit̪a hɔt͡ɕt͡ɕʰe
b̤art̪er d͡zubrad͡ʑ ebɔŋ pɔrɔmɔ s̪ɔt̪t̪a
kɽiʂner ruper n̪it͡ɕe


s̪ɔŋs̪kɽit̪ patʰ t̪ʰeke on̪ud̪it̪
d̪bara
s̪d͡zar eduin̪ arn̪ɔl̪dɔ
eme kes̪iaii s̪ies̪ai
n̪iuie̯ɔrkɔ
trus̪l̪ɔোb̤ɔ hd͡zan̪ɔs̪ɔn̪ɔ o্d͡zan̪dɔ kɔmba l̪imited
 pɔnt͡ɕɔmɔ eb̤in̪iu




ut̪ɔs̪ɔrɡɔ

b̤art̪e

t̪ai ki ami ei t͡ɕɔmɔt̪ɔkar ebɔŋ at̪marোmant͡ɕɔkɔrɔ b̤aʂɔnɔti pɔɽet͡ɕʰi
kɽiʂnɔ ebɔŋ rad͡ʑkumar ord͡ʑun̪ d̪̤ɔre rekʰet͡ɕʰen̪ prɔt̪d͡zeker s̪at̪ʰe bɔkt̪ɽit̪a kɔrɔt͡ɕʰen̪
t̪ai ki ami ekʰan̪e er prɔd͡ʑna l̪ikʰet͡ɕʰi er l̪ukan̪ো rɔhɔs̪d͡zɔ
iŋl̪d͡zan̪der d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ he amad̪er b̤arɔt̪ɔ amar kat͡ɕʰe s̪e d͡zɔt̪ɔta prie̯

eduin̪ arn̪ɔl̪dɔ





mukʰɔbɔn̪d̪̤ɔ
ei bikʰd͡zat̪ ebɔŋ aɕt͡ɕɔrd͡zɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ s̪ɔŋs̪kɽit̪ kɔbit̪ati mɔhab̤art̪er ekti pɔrbɔ his̪abe mɔhan̪ hin̪d̪u mɔhakabd͡zer ʂɔʂtʰɔ ba b̤iʂmɔpɔrbe ̤ɡ̤ɔte। eti b̤art̪e bd͡zapɔkɔ d͡ʑɔn̪ɔprie̯t̪a ebɔŋ kɔrt̪ɽit̪bɔ upɔb̤ɔোɡɔ kɔre d͡zekʰan̪e eti d̪ebn̪aɡiri s̪ahit̪d͡zer pɔ̃t͡ɕɔ rɔt̪n̪ɔpɔnt͡ɕɔrɔt̪ɔn̪an̪ier mɔd̪̤d͡ze ekti his̪abe ɡɔnd͡zɔ he̯ɔ। s̪ɔrɔl̪ɔ kin̪t̪u mɔhɔt̪ɔ b̤aʂae̯ eti ekti d̪arɕɔn̪ik bd͡zɔbɔs̪t̪ʰa un̪mɔোt͡ɕɔn̪ɔ kɔre d͡za ad͡ʑo bid̪d͡zɔman̪ brahmɔnd͡zɔbad̪i। biɕbas̪ eti kɔpil̪a pɔt̪ɔnd͡ʑɔl̪i ebɔŋ bed̪er mɔt̪ɔbad̪er mɔt̪ɔ miɕrit̪ kɔre। er on̪ek ̤ɡ̤ɔোʂɔna et̪i ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔ er ut͡ɕt͡ɕakaŋkʂake et̪i mɔhɔt̪ɔ et̪ biɕud̪d̪̤ɔ ebɔŋ kɔোmɔl̪ɔ er d̪̤armikt̪a d͡ze ɕl̪eɡel̪ kɔbit̪ati od̪̤d͡ze̯ɔn̪er pɔre bib̤ɔkt̪ɔ he̯ɔ t̪ar od͡ʑan̪a l̪ekʰker prɔt̪i an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ o prɔɕɔŋs̪ar ei bis̪ɸɔোrɔnɔ md͡zad͡ʑis̪trɔোram reb̤aren̪tie̯a e brd͡zakɔmd͡zan̪is̪ in̪tar s̪d͡zaktis̪ima pitatis̪ oɸis̪ie̯a reɸaretar। t̪ai praimɔmɔ b̤d͡zatɔs̪ɔ pɔbit̪rɔt̪a n̪umin̪ɔs̪kɔ haipোɸeta ei t͡ɕɔmɔt̪kar ɕrɔd̪d̪̤ar prɔt̪id̪̤bɔn̪i kɔre ebɔŋ prɔkɽit̪ɔpɔkʂe ekʰan̪e kit͡ɕʰu n̪ojt̪ikt̪a et̪tai akɔrʂɔnie̯ ebɔŋ s̪ɔman̪t̪ɔral̪t̪ake et̪tai bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre d̪ee̯ prae̯ɕi prɔkɽit̪ɔpɔkʂe mɔৌkʰik er ɕikʂa ebɔŋ n̪iu tes̪tamen̪ter mɔd̪̤d͡ze d͡ze pɔndit̪ ebɔŋ d̪̤ɔrmɔprɔt͡ɕarɔkɔd̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze ekti bit̪ɔrkɔ d̪ekʰa d̪ie̯et͡ɕʰe l̪ekʰɔkɔ kʰris̪tan̪ ut̪s̪ɔ t̪ʰeke d̪̤ar kɔret͡ɕʰen̪ kin̪a ba t̪ɔ̃rɔ kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke ib̤and͡ʑel̪is̪tɔ ebɔŋ prerit̪d̪er kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke n̪eoe̯a he̯et͡ɕʰe kin̪a t̪a n̪ie̯e।

eti t̪ar t̪arikʰer prɔɕn̪ɔ ut̪t̪ʰapɔn̪ɔ kɔre d͡za it̪ibat͡ɕɔkɔb̤abe n̪iʂpɔt̪t̪i kɔra d͡zae̯ n̪a। eti obɔɕd͡zi prat͡ɕin̪ mɔhakabd͡zer mɔd̪̤d͡ze mul̪ mɔhab̤art̪er t͡ɕee̯e pɔrɔbɔrt̪i s̪ɔme̯e on̪t̪ɔrb̤ukt̪ɔ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe t̪ɔbe miɦ kas̪in̪at̪ʰ t̪el̪aŋ etike kʰris̪tie̯ d͡zuɡer purbɔbɔrt̪i prɔman kɔrar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kit͡ɕʰu n̪d͡zad͡zd͡zɔ d͡zukt̪i upɔs̪t̪ʰapɔn̪ɔ kɔret͡ɕʰen̪। prɔmaner od͡ʑɔn̪ɔ t̪ɔbe kʰris̪ter pɔre prae̯ t̪ɽit̪ie̯ ɕɔt̪abd̪it̪e er rɔt͡ɕɔn̪ake s̪t̪ʰan̪ d̪ee̯ ebɔŋ s̪ɔmb̤ɔbɔt̪ɔ ei brahmɔnd͡zɔ kɔbit̪ae̯ ɡɔd͡zal̪il̪er patʰ ebɔŋ s̪irie̯ar obt̪arer prɔt̪id̪̤bɔn̪i re̯et͡ɕʰe।

er d̪ɽiɕd͡zɔ hɔl̪ɔ d͡ʑumn̪a o s̪ɔrɔs̪ut̪i n̪ɔd̪ir mɔd̪̤d͡zɔbɔrt̪i s̪ɔmɔt̪ɔl̪ɔ d̪eɕ ekʰɔn̪ɔ kurn̪ul̪ o d͡ʑ̤in̪d̪ɔ। er s̪ɔrɔl̪ɔ pl̪ɔtɔtit̪e rad͡ʑa d͡zud̪̤iʂtʰirer b̤ai d͡zubrad͡ʑ ord͡ʑun̪er s̪ɔŋl̪ap re̯et͡ɕʰe d͡zin̪i ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ s̪art̪ʰir t͡ɕʰɔd̪mɔbeɕe pɔrɔmɔ d̪ebt̪a kɽiʂner s̪at̪ʰe। kɔৌrɔbɔ ebɔŋ pandɔbɔd̪er s̪en̪abahin̪ir mɔd̪̤d͡ze ekti mɔhan̪ d͡zud̪d̪̤ɔ as̪ɔn̪n̪ɔ ebɔŋ ei kɔt̪ʰɔোpɔkɔt̪ʰɔn̪ɔti birোd̪̤i d̪ɔl̪ɔɡul̪ir mɔd̪̤d͡ze ekti d͡zud̪d̪̤ɔrɔt̪ʰe t̪ojri kɔra he̯ɔ।

kɔbit̪atike barn̪uɸ d̪bara ɸɔras̪i b̤aʂae̯ l̪d͡zas̪en̪er d̪bara l̪d͡zatin̪e s̪tan̪is̪l̪ab̤ ɡattir d̪bara it̪al̪ie̯ b̤aʂae̯ ɡɔd͡zal̪an̪োs̪er d̪bara ɡɔrik b̤aʂae̯ ebɔŋ mis̪tar t̪ʰɔmɔs̪ɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ mis̪tar deb̤is̪ d̪bara iŋred͡ʑit̪e rupan̪t̪ɔrit̪ he̯et͡ɕʰe ɕeʂ n̪amtir ɡɔd̪d͡zɔ prɔt̪il̪ipi s̪ɔt̪d͡zii prɔɕɔŋs̪ar baire। er biɕbɔs̪t̪ɔt̪a ebɔŋ s̪pɔʂtɔt̪a। miɦ t̪el̪aŋ bɔোmbet̪e kɔt̪ʰd͡zɔ t͡ɕʰɔn̪d̪e ekti s̪ɔŋs̪kɔrɔno prɔkaɕ kɔret͡ɕʰen̪ d͡za biɕiʂtɔb̤abe ɕekʰa ebɔŋ bud̪d̪̤iman̪ kin̪t̪u as̪ɔl̪ɔtir mɔrd͡zad̪a ba on̪uɡɔrɔhɔ prɔkaɕ kɔren̪i। ami d͡zɔd̪i et̪ ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪ɔrɔ pɔndit̪d̪er pɔre ekti bis̪me̯ɔkɔrɔ kɔbit̪ar on̪ubad̪ d̪eoe̯ar ud̪d͡zɔোɡɔ kɔri t̪ɔbe eti t̪ad̪er ɕrɔmɔ t̪ʰeke prapt̪ɔ s̪ahad͡zd͡zer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kɽit̪ɔd͡ʑnɔt̪ar s̪bikɽit̪is̪bɔrup ebɔŋ karɔnɔ d͡ʑɔn̪ɔprie̯ akare ekti kabd͡zik ebɔŋ d̪arɕɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ n̪a t̪ʰakl̪e iŋred͡ʑi s̪ahit̪d͡zɔ obɔɕd͡zi os̪ɔmpurnɔ hɔbe। b̤art̪er kat͡ɕʰe।

s̪el̪es̪tie̯al̪ ɡan̪ n̪id͡ʑer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ bd͡zakʰd͡za kɔre n̪a emɔn̪ɔ bɔl̪ar mɔt̪ɔো ar kit͡ɕʰu n̪ei। s̪ɔŋs̪kɽit̪ mul̪ti on̪uʂtub̤ mitare l̪ekʰa d͡za pɔɕt͡ɕima kan̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ s̪ɔɸɔl̪ɔb̤abe pun̪rut̪pad̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔra d͡zae̯ n̪a। t̪ai ami etike amad̪er n̪ɔmɔn̪ie̯ ɸɔ̃ka ɕl̪ɔোke n̪ikʂep kɔret͡ɕʰi l̪irikal̪ pɔrimape pɔribɔrt̪it̪ d͡zekʰan̪e patʰd͡zɔti ekib̤abe b̤eŋe d͡zae̯। beɕirb̤aɡ oŋɕer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ami biɕbas̪ kɔri d͡ze ort̪ʰɔti biɕbɔs̪t̪ɔb̤abe n̪imn̪ɔl̪ikʰit̪ pɽiʂtʰaɡul̪it̪e s̪ɔŋrɔkʂit̪ hɔbe kin̪t̪u ɕl̪eɡel̪ke n̪id͡ʑei bɔl̪ɔt̪e he̯et͡ɕʰil̪ in̪ kɔn̪ɔditioribas̪ mi s̪empar pɔোe̯etaɸোs̪tar men̪tem rektɔ dib̤in̪as̪e o্d͡zaɸimare o as̪im। d͡zara kɔbit̪atir d̪ɔrɕɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔmpɔrke aro pɔɽɔt̪e t͡ɕan̪ t̪ara mes̪ars̪ɔ trubn̪ar o্d͡zan̪dɔ kɔোŋ d̪bara mud̪rit̪ mis̪tar deb̤is̪er b̤ɔl̪iume ekti prɔɕɔŋs̪ɔn̪ie̯ b̤umika pet̪e paren̪।

eduin̪ arn̪ɔl̪dɔ s̪ies̪ai

od̪̤d͡zae̯

kurukʂet̪re bɔl̪ɔ s̪ɔnd͡ʑe̯ɔ bɔl̪ɔ

rad͡ʑa d̪urd͡zɔোd̪̤ɔn̪ɔ d̪rɔোner kat͡ɕʰe ãkəlen

pan̪du d͡zɔোd̪d̪̤ad̪er kɔt̪ɔ biɕal̪
d̪rupɔd̪ɔ put̪rer d̪bara d͡zud̪d̪̤e l̪ipt̪ɔ

d̪̤ɽiʂtɔket̪ t͡ɕekit̪an̪ kaɕir ɕɔkt̪ɔ prɔb̤u
purud͡ʑit̪ kun̪t̪ib̤োd͡ʑɔ o ɕojbd͡zɔ

s̪ahɔs̪i ebɔŋ t͡ɕeʂta ei d̪in̪ mɽit̪d͡zur d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ prɔs̪t̪ut̪

matʰe prɔt̪d͡zekei d̪ɔkʂɔ। d̪urbɔl̪ɔt̪ɔmɔmes̪imɔs̪ɔ

bl̪ee̯ar d̪ie̯e d͡ʑaɡie̯e t̪ul̪t͡ɕʰe rɔkt̪ɔ ̤ɡ̤ure beɽat͡ɕt͡ɕʰe
s̪iŋher ɡɔrd͡ʑɔn̪er mɔt̪ɔো trampetarer mɔt̪ɔো

akɔs̪mik kɔোl̪ahɔl̪e ɸete pɔɽa bis̪ɸɔোrɔnɔ his̪abe
d̤il̪ed̤al̪a t̪uɸan̪ emɔn̪ɔ t̪ɔোl̪ɔpaɽ mɔn̪e hɔl̪ɔো
t̪arɔpɔrɔ d̪ekʰa d͡zabe t̪ad̪er s̪ɔোn̪ar ɡaɽir opɔrɔ
s̪ad̪a ̤ɡ̤ɔোɽar d͡ʑɔোe̯al̪e d͡ʑɔɽan̪ো t̪ad̪er d͡zud̪d̪̤er ɕel̪ uɽie̯e
kɽiʂnɔ b̤ɔɡɔban̪ ord͡ʑun̪ t̪ar paɕe
kɽiʂnɔ ɡĩtəd͡ʒukə্tə t̪al̪a s̪ɔhɔ t̪ɔ̃rɔ d̪urd̪an̪t̪ɔ ɕɔŋkʰɔ bad͡ʑal̪en̪
d̪ojt̪d͡zer haɽ kʰɔোd̪ai kɔra ord͡ʑun̪ uɽie̯e d̪il̪en̪
in̪d̪rer d͡ʑɔোre d̪an̪ b̤e̯ɔŋkɔrɔ b̤im
n̪ekɽepetoe̯al̪a b̤imekti l̪ɔmba ɕɔŋkʰɔ bad͡ʑal̪en̪

ar n̪ɔkul̪ t̪ar ɕɔŋkʰer upɔrɔ ɸũkə d̪il̪
n̪am d̪ie̯et͡ɕʰen̪ ‘mɔd̪̤ur d̪̤bɔn̪i s̪ɔhɔd̪eb t̪ar opɔrɔ
d͡zake mɔniɕɔd͡zd͡zabiɕiʂtɔ bɔl̪a he̯ɔ ebɔŋ t̪ar upɔrɔ kas̪ir rad͡ʑkumar।
ɕikʰɔndi t̪ar ɡaɽit̪e d̪̤ɽiʂtɔd̪d͡zumn̪ɔ
birat s̪at̪d͡zɔki on̪abɽit̪
d̪rupɔd̪ɔ t̪ar put̪rɔd̪er s̪at̪ʰe he pɽit̪ʰibir prɔb̤u
d̪ir̤ɡ̤ɔ s̪ɔɕɔs̪t̪rɔ s̪ub̤ɔd̪rar ɕiɕura s̪ɔbai d͡ʑɔোre ɸũ d̪il̪ো
d͡zat̪e d͡ʑ̤ɔn̪ɔd͡ʑ̤ɔn̪ɔ ɕɔbd̪ɔ t̪ad̪er ɕɔt̪rud̪er hɽid̪e̯ɔke n̪aɽa d̪ee̯
kɔ̃pan̪ো pɽit̪ʰibi ebɔŋ akaɕer bɔd͡ʑrer s̪at̪ʰe।
t̪arɔpɔre
d̪̤ɽit̪iraʂtrer d͡zud̪d̪̤er s̪et d̪ekʰt͡ɕʰi
os̪t̪rɔ mukt̪ɔ d̪̤ɔn̪uk tan̪a d͡zud̪d̪̤ɔ
t̪ɔt̪ɔkʂɔnat̪ b̤aŋaord͡ʑun̪ d͡zar pɔt̪akabd͡zad͡ʑ

kɽiʂner kat͡ɕʰe t̪ɔ̃rɔ s̪art̪ʰi
draib̤ n̪irb̤ik ek kʰɔোl̪a matʰer d̪ike
s̪en̪abahin̪ir mɔd̪̤d͡ze ami arো kat͡ɕʰakat͡ɕʰi d̪ekʰt̪e hɔbe
d͡zara amad̪er s̪at̪ʰe d͡zud̪d̪̤ɔ kɔrɔbe t̪ad̪er hɔt̪d͡za kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe
ad͡ʑ d͡zud̪d̪̤er s̪al̪iɕe d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ n̪iɕt͡ɕit̪
ei s̪ɔmɔt̪ɔl̪e d͡zara b̤iɽ kɔre t̪ara s̪ɔbai rɔkt̪ɔpat̪er d̪ike d͡ʑ̤ũkət͡ʃʰe
d̪̤ɽit̪iraʂtrer papi put̪rer an̪uɡɔt̪d͡zɔ kɔra।
eib̤abe ord͡ʑun̪ prart̪ʰɔn̪a kɔrɔl̪en̪ he b̤ɔrɔt̪ɔ
s̪bɔrɡie̯ s̪art̪ʰi hɔোs̪tɔd̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze
ud͡ʑd͡ʑbɔl̪ɔ ɡaɽiti t͡ɕal̪an̪ t̪ar d̪ud̪̤s̪ad̪a s̪tidɡul̪ike l̪aɡan̪
d͡zekʰan̪e b̤iʂmɔ d̪rɔোnɔ ebɔŋ t̪ad̪er prɔb̤ura n̪et̪ɽit̪bɔ d̪ie̯et͡ɕʰil̪en̪।
d̪ekʰa t̪in̪i ord͡ʑun̪ke bɔl̪ɔl̪en̪ t̪ara d͡zekʰan̪e d̪ɔ̃ɽie̯e at͡ɕʰe
t̪ɔোmar kurud̪er at̪mie̯ ebɔŋ rad͡ʑkumar
prɔt̪iti hat̪e t̪ar baɽir at̪mie̯d̪er t͡ɕihn̪it̪ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe
n̪at̪i ebɔŋ b̤ai t͡ɕat͡ɕa ebɔŋ b̤ai ebɔŋ t͡ɕʰel̪e
t͡ɕat͡ɕat̪ো b̤ai o d͡ʑamai o b̤aɡn̪e mil̪e miɕe ɡet͡ɕʰe
bɔn̪d̪̤u ebɔŋ s̪ɔmman̪it̪ prɔbind̪er s̪at̪ʰe keu keu ei d̪ike
s̪ei pɔkʂer kit͡ɕʰu l̪ɔোkɔ t͡ɕʰil̪ ebɔŋ d͡zara birোd̪̤it̪a kɔrɔt͡ɕʰe t̪ad̪er d̪ekʰe
emɔn̪ɔ kit̪ʰ beɽet͡ɕʰe ɕɔt̪ruord͡ʑun̪er hɽid̪e̯ɔ
kɔrunae̯ ɡɔl̪e ɡel̪en̪ d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ t̪in̪i ei kɔt̪ʰati ut͡ɕt͡ɕarɔnɔ kɔrɔl̪en̪
ord͡ʑun̪।
kɽiʂnɔ ami d̪ekʰt͡ɕʰi ekʰan̪e ɕed kɔrɔt̪e as̪a
t̪ad̪er s̪ad̪̤arɔnɔ rɔkt̪ɔ amad̪er at̪mie̯d̪er s̪ɔmɔbet̪
amar s̪ɔd̪ɔs̪d͡zɔra bd͡zɔrt̪ʰɔ he̯ɔ amar d͡ʑib̤ amar mukʰe ɕukie̯e d͡zae̯
ekti kɔ̃pun̪i amar ɕɔrir ebɔŋ amar t͡ɕul̪ rɔোmant͡ɕit̪
b̤it̪i s̪ɔŋɡe amar d̪urbɔl̪ɔ hat̪er s̪l̪ip t̪ʰeke
ɡan̪d̪̤ib b̤al̪b̤abe n̪ɔmɔ d͡ʑbɔrɔ d͡ʑbɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰe
amar t̪bɔkɔ ɕukie̯e d͡zaoe̯a kʰub kɔmi ami d̪ɔ̃ɽat̪e pari
amar mɔd̪̤d͡ze d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔ̃t̪ar kata ebɔŋ od͡ʑnan̪ mɔn̪e he̯ɔ
aɸɔs̪ɔোs̪ɔ ar hahakar t͡ɕʰaɽa ami kit͡ɕʰui b̤abi n̪a
eta b̤al̪ n̪e̯ɔ he keɕɔbɔ b̤al̪ো kit͡ɕʰu n̪a
parɔs̪pɔrik bɔd̪̤ɔ t̪ʰeke bɔs̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ hɔt̪e pare d̪ekʰ ami ̤ɡ̤ɽina kɔri
bid͡ʑe̯ɔ ebɔŋ ad̪̤ipɔt̪d͡zɔ s̪ɔmpɔd̪ɔ ebɔŋ s̪bat͡ɕt͡ɕʰɔn̪d̪d͡zɔ
eb̤abei d̪uঃkʰer d͡ʑe̯ɔ ahɔো ki bid͡ʑe̯ɔ
an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ an̪t̪e pare ɡɔোbin̪d̪ɔ ki d̪̤ɔn̪i l̪untʰɔn̪ɔ
l̪ab̤ kɔrɔt̪e pare ki n̪ie̯ɔmɔ prɔt̪id̪an̪ ki s̪pd͡zan̪
n̪id͡ʑer d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔke miʂti mɔn̪e he̯ɔ emɔn̪ɔ rɔkt̪ɔ ​​d̪ie̯e ken̪a
d̪ekʰe d͡ze t̪ara ekʰan̪e d̪ɔ̃ɽie̯e at͡ɕʰe mɔrɔt̪e prɔs̪t̪ut̪
d͡zar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕʰil̪ n̪d͡zad͡zd͡zɔ ebɔŋ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ kʰuɕi
ebɔŋ kʂɔmɔt̪a mul̪d͡zɔban̪ he̯e utʰɔl̪ɔn̪an̪i s̪d͡zar ebɔŋ put̪rɔ
b̤ai ebɔŋ ɕbɔɕur ebɔŋ d͡ʑamai
prɔbin ebɔŋ bɔn̪d̪̤ura ami ki es̪ber upɔrɔ mɽit̪d͡zu mɔোkabel̪a kɔrɔbɔ
d͡zɔd̪io t̪ara amad̪er hɔt̪d͡za kɔrɔt̪e t͡ɕae̯ ek d̪̤akka n̪e̯ɔ
he mɔd̪̤us̪ud̪ɔn̪ɔ ami l̪ab̤er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ a̤ɡ̤at̪ kɔrɔbɔ
t̪in̪ti biɕber n̪ie̯ɔmɔ t̪ahɔl̪e kɔt̪ɔ kɔmɔ
part̪ʰib rad͡ʑd͡zɔ d̪ɔkʰɔl̪ɔ kɔrɔt̪e es̪ɔbɔ hɔt̪d͡za
prɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe kin̪t̪u d͡zɔn̪t̪rɔna kɽiʂnɔ d͡zɔd̪i t̪ara he̯ɔ
d̪ɔোʂi t̪ad̪er mɽit̪d͡zut̪e amra d̪ɔোʂi hɔbɔ

d̪̤ɽit̪raʂtrer s̪ei t͡ɕʰel̪era ebɔŋ amad̪er at̪mie̯ra
t̪at̪e ki ɕan̪t̪i as̪be he mad̪̤ɔbɔ
karɔnɔ d͡zɔd̪i s̪ɔt̪d͡zii l̪al̪s̪a o krɔোd̪̤e on̪d̪̤ɔ he̯e d͡zae̯
era pap d̪ekʰt̪e pae̯ n̪a ba d̪ekʰt̪e pabe n̪a
bad̪ɕahi o at̪mie̯ɔs̪bɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ n̪ihɔt̪ɔd̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze
amra d͡zara d̪ekʰt͡ɕʰi emɔn̪ɔ oprad̪̤ eɽie̯e t͡ɕɔl̪a ut͡ɕit̪ n̪e̯ɔ kib̤abe
amra d͡zara oprad̪̤ upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤i kɔri ebɔŋ l̪ɔd͡ʑd͡ʑa on̪ub̤ɔbɔ kɔri
he d͡ʑɔn̪ard̪ɔn̪ɔ he puruʂer an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ
baɽi̤ɡ̤ɔrɔ ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ kɔre d̪̤bɔŋs̪ɔ he̯e d͡zae̯
t̪ad̪er miʂti krɔmaɡɔt̪ɔ paribarik d̪̤armikt̪a
ebŋat͡ɕaron̪uʂtʰan̪ obɔhel̪it̪ t̪akoe̯a bil̪upt̪ɔ
s̪ei ɡɽiher upɔrɔ oɕl̪il̪t̪a prɔbeɕ kɔre
er n̪arira n̪arihin̪b̤abe beɽe otʰe d͡zekʰan̪ t̪ʰeke bɔs̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ he̯ɔ
un̪mad̪ abeɡ ebɔŋ bɔrner mil̪ɔn̪ɔ
ekti hel̪oe̯ardɔ ras̪t̪a patʰan̪ো hɔt͡ɕt͡ɕʰe d͡ze pɔribar
ebɔŋ d͡ze t̪ar kʂɔোb̤er d̪bara t̪ar s̪ɔrbɔn̪aɕ ̤ɡ̤ɔtie̯et͡ɕʰe।
n̪a ebɔŋ s̪ɔmman̪it̪ purbɔpuruʂd̪er at̪ma
t̪ad̪er ɕan̪t̪ir d͡ʑae̯ɡa t̪ʰeke t͡ɕʰitke pɔɽun̪
on̪t̪d͡zeʂtikrie̯akek ebɔŋ oe̯an̪ det̪ʰ oe̯atar।#
t̪ai amad̪er pɔbit̪rɔ s̪t̪ɔোt̪rɔ ɕekʰan̪। eib̤abe d͡zɔd̪i amra hɔt̪d͡za
part̪ʰib ɕɔkt̪ir b̤al̪bas̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ at̪mie̯ ebɔŋ bɔn̪d̪̤ura
ahɔোb̤at̪ eta ki ekti kʰarap d̪ɔোʂɔ t͡ɕʰil̪
amar at̪mie̯ɔs̪bɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔra a̤ɡ̤at̪ kɔrɔl̪ei b̤al̪ো mɔn̪e he̯ɔ
os̪t̪rɔhin̪ t̪ad̪er mɔোkabel̪a kɔrɔt̪e ebɔŋ amar s̪t̪ɔn̪ɔ kʰal̪i kɔrɔt̪e

ekʰan̪e b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar prɔt̪ʰɔmɔ od̪̤d͡zae̯ ɕeʂ kɔrɔt͡ɕʰi

s̪ɔnd͡ʑe̯ɔ।
t̪in̪i emɔn̪ɔ kɔruna ebɔŋ emɔn̪ɔ d̪uঃkʰe b̤ɔra
t͡ɕɔোkʰɔ oɕruos̪pɔʂtɔ hɔt̪aɕaɡɔrɔs̪t̪ɔ kɔɽa kɔt̪ʰae̯
draib̤ar mɔd̪̤us̪ud̪ɔn̪ɔ eb̤abe s̪ɔmbɔোd̪̤ɔn̪ɔ kɔrɔl̪en̪
kɽiʂnɔ।
ei d̪urbɔl̪ɔt̪a apn̪ake kib̤abe n̪ie̯et͡ɕʰe d͡zekʰan̪ t̪ʰeke d͡ʑ̤ɔrna
l̪ɔd͡ʑd͡ʑad͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ kɔʂtɔ s̪ahɔs̪id̪er kat͡ɕʰe l̪ɔd͡ʑd͡ʑad͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ
pund͡zer pɔt̪ʰe bad̪̤a n̪a ord͡ʑun̪
n̪id͡ʑeke d̪urbɔl̪ɔt̪a barɔnɔ eta mɔŋɡɔl̪ɔ
t̪ɔোmar d͡zɔোd̪d̪̤an̪am kapuruʂɸit bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ n̪ikʂep
d͡ʑaɡো n̪id͡ʑeke ho otʰো t̪ɔোmar ɕɔt̪rud̪er ɕas̪t̪i
ord͡ʑun̪।
kib̤abe ami d͡zud̪d̪̤e kʰad̪ d̪ie̯e ɡul̪i kɔrɔt̪e pari
b̤iʂmer upɔrɔ n̪a d̪rɔোner upre he t̪umi prɔd̪̤an̪
ub̤e̯ɔ pud͡ʑn̪ie̯ ub̤e̯ɔ s̪ɔmman̪it̪ puruʂ
b̤ikʰarir rutit̪e bẽt͡ʃe t̪ʰakai b̤al̪ো
d͡zad̪erke amra d͡ʑibit̪ b̤al̪োbas̪i
s̪ɔmɽid̪d̪̤ɔ ut̪ɔs̪ɔbe t̪ad̪er rɔkt̪er s̪bad̪ n̪eoe̯ar t͡ɕee̯e
ar oprad̪̤ɔbɔোd̪̤e bẽt͡ʃe t̪ʰaka
ahɔ eta kʰarap t͡ɕʰil̪ke d͡ʑan̪ehɔbe
ekʰan̪e bid͡ʑe̯i ba pɔrad͡ʑit̪
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ t̪ara raɡ kɔre amad̪er mukʰোmukʰi he̯ɔ
kar mɽit̪d͡zu d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔke b̤e̯ɔŋkɔrɔ t͡ɕʰeɽe d̪ee̯
mɔmɔt̪ae̯ harie̯e s̪ɔn̪d̪ehɔ t͡ɕʰuɽe ɸel̪e
amar t͡ɕin̪t̪abikʂipt̪ɔ pal̪a
apn̪ar kat͡ɕʰe ɡaid d͡zake ami s̪ɔbɔt͡ɕee̯e beɕi ɕrɔd̪d̪̤a kɔri
d͡zat̪e ami ɕikʰt̪e pari
ami d͡ʑan̪i n̪a ki d̪uঃkʰɔ n̪irame̯ɔ hɔbe
at̪ma ebɔŋ in̪d̪rie̯e puɽe ɡet͡ɕʰe
ami d͡zɔd̪i pɽit̪ʰibir oprɔt̪id̪bɔn̪d̪bi prɔd̪̤an̪ hɔt̪am
ekti d̪ebt̪a ebɔŋ eiɡul̪i s̪ekʰan̪ t̪ʰeke t͡ɕɔl̪e ɡet͡ɕʰe
s̪ɔnd͡ʑe̯ɔ।
t̪ai ord͡ʑun̪ hɽid̪e̯er prɔb̤uke bɔl̪ɔl̪en̪
ebɔŋ d̪ir̤ɡ̤ɔɕbas̪ ɸel̪e ami d͡zud̪d̪̤ɔ kɔrɔbɔ n̪a t̪ɔkʰɔn̪ɔ n̪irɔbɔt̪a pal̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔren̪।
d͡zar prɔt̪i kɔোmɔl̪ɔ has̪i d̪ie̯e he b̤ɔrɔt̪ɔ
d͡zubrad͡ʑ d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ hɔt̪aɕaɡɔrɔs̪t̪ɔ he̯e kẽdet͡ʃʰilen oi hɔোs̪tɔd̪er tuiks̪ɔdɔ
kɽiʂnɔ d̪ibd͡zɔ ɕl̪ɔোke ut̪t̪ɔrɔ d̪ie̯et͡ɕʰen̪
kɽiʂnɔ।
apn̪i d̪uঃkʰit̪ d͡zekʰan̪e kɔোn̪ɔ d̪uঃkʰɔ t̪ʰaka ut͡ɕit̪ n̪e̯ɔ t̪umi kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪ɔ
kɔt̪ʰae̯ d͡ʑnan̪er ob̤ab on̪t̪ɔre d͡ʑnan̪id̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
d͡zara bẽt͡ʃe t̪ʰake t̪ad̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ɕɔোkɔ kɔrɔো n̪a ebɔŋ d͡zara mara d͡zae̯ t̪ad̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ɕɔোkɔ kɔrɔো n̪a।
n̪a ami n̪a t̪umi n̪a ed̪er keui
kɔkʰɔn̪ɔো t͡ɕʰil̪ n̪a kɔkʰɔn̪ɔো hɔbe n̪a
t͡ɕirkal̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ebɔŋ on̪ɔn̪t̪ɔkal̪ pɔre।
s̪ɔbɔ d͡ze bẽt͡ʃe t̪ʰake s̪ɔbɔs̪ɔme̯ɔ bẽt͡ʃe t̪ʰake man̪uʂer ɸreme
ɕojɕɔbɔ ebɔŋ d͡zɔৌbɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ be̯ɔs̪ɔ as̪e
t̪ai s̪ekʰan̪e raid͡ʑiŋap ebɔŋ l̪ee̯iŋdaun̪ kɔrun̪
on̪d͡zan̪d͡zɔ ebɔŋ on̪d͡zan̪d͡zɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔbas̪er
d͡za d͡ʑnan̪ira d͡ʑan̪e ebɔŋ b̤e̯ɔ pae̯ n̪a। eta d͡ze birɔkt̪ɔ kɔre
t̪ɔোmar in̪d̪rie̯d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ upad̪an̪e rɔোmant͡ɕɔkɔrɔ
apn̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ t̪ap ebɔŋ tʰan̪da d̪uঃkʰɔ ebɔŋ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ n̪ie̯e as̪e
eti s̪ɔŋkʂipt̪ɔ ebɔŋ pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪ɔd͡zɔোɡɔd͡zɔ eta s̪ɔhd͡zɔ kɔrun̪ rad͡ʑkumar
d͡ʑnan̪i b̤al̪uk his̪abe d͡ze at̪ma s̪ɔre n̪a
at̪ma d͡ze ekti ɕɔkt̪iɕal̪i ebɔŋ d̪̤rubɔkɔ ɕan̪t̪ɔ s̪ɔŋɡe
d̪uঃkʰɔ n̪ee̯ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ n̪ee̯ ud̪as̪in̪b̤abe
omɽit̪ d͡ʑibn̪e bẽt͡ʃe t̪ʰake d͡ze d͡za
kɔkʰɔn̪i t̪ʰamt̪e pare n̪a d͡za n̪e̯ɔ
t̪ʰakbe n̪a। d̪ud͡ʑn̪er ei s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ d̪ekʰt̪e
t̪ad̪er ki d̪ur̤ɡ̤ɔtɔn̪a t̪ʰeke s̪araŋɕɔ oŋɕɔ
t͡ɕʰae̯a t̪ʰeke pɔd̪art̪ʰɔ। obin̪ɔɕbɔrɔ
apn̪i ɕikʰun̪ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ hɔl̪ɔ s̪ɔbar mɔd̪̤d͡ze d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕʰɔɽie̯e d̪eoe̯a
eta kɔোt̪ʰao kɔোn̪ɔোb̤abei
d͡zahai huk kɔmɔ t̪ʰaki ba pɔribɔrt̪it̪ ho।
kin̪t̪u ei kʂɔnɔs̪t̪ʰae̯i ɸremer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ d͡za eti d͡ʑan̪ae̯
at̪mar s̪at̪ʰe mɽit̪d͡zuhin̪ on̪t̪ɔhin̪ os̪im
t̪ara bin̪ɔʂtɔ he̯ɔ। t̪ad̪er d̪̤bɔŋs̪ɔ hɔোkɔ rad͡ʑkumar ebɔŋ d͡zud̪d̪̤ɔ
d͡ze bɔl̪ɔbe ami ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔke hɔt̪d͡za kɔret͡ɕʰi
d͡ze mɔn̪e kɔrɔbe d̪ekʰ ami n̪ihɔt̪ɔ d͡zara ub̤e̯ɔ
kit͡ɕʰui d͡ʑan̪i n̪a d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔke hɔt̪d͡za kɔra d͡zae̯ n̪a। d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ bɔd̪̤ɔ n̪e̯ɔ
at̪mar d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ he̯ɔ n̪i at̪ma kɔkʰɔn̪o hɔt̪e bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ hɔbe
s̪ɔme̯ɔ t͡ɕʰil̪ n̪a eta t͡ɕʰil̪ n̪a ɕeʂ ebɔŋ ɕuru s̪bɔpn̪ɔ
d͡ʑɔn̪mɔhin̪ ebɔŋ mɽit̪d͡zuhin̪ ebɔŋ pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪ɔhin̪ at̪ma t͡ɕirkal̪ t̪ʰake
mɽit̪d͡zu s̪pɔrɕɔ kɔren̪i ektuo mɔre ɡel̪eo mɔn̪e he̯ɔ ̤ɡ̤ɔrɔ
ke d͡ʑan̪e kl̪an̪t̪ihin̪ s̪babɔl̪ɔmbi
omɔrɔ obin̪ɔɕbɔrɔ emɔn̪ɔ hɔbe
bɔl̪un̪ ami ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔke hɔt̪d͡za kɔret͡ɕʰi n̪aki hɔt̪d͡za kɔret͡ɕʰi
n̪a kin̪t̪u d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ keu ɕue̯e t̪ʰake
t̪ar d͡ʑirnɔ pɔোɕak d̪ure
ebɔŋ n̪ɔt̪un̪ ɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔre bɔl̪e
eɡul̪ো ami ad͡ʑ pɔrɔbɔ
t̪ai at̪ma d̪bara 
hal̪ka t̪ar maŋs̪er pɔোɕak
ebɔŋ ut̪t̪ɔrad̪̤ikar s̪ut̪re t͡ɕɔl̪e d͡zae̯
n̪ɔt̪un̪ kɔre ekti bas̪ɔs̪t̪ʰan̪।
ami t̪ɔোmake bɔl̪i os̪t̪rɔ d͡ʑibn̪er kat͡ɕʰe pɔৌ̃t͡ʃʰaj n̪a
ɕikʰa t̪a pɔোɽae̯ n̪a d͡ʑɔl̪ɔ d͡ʑbɔl̪ɔt̪e pare n̪a
ɕukɔn̪ɔো bat̪as̪o t̪a ɕukie̯e d͡zae̯ n̪a। d̪urb̤ed̪d͡zɔ
oprɔbeɕit̪ n̪irɔs̪t̪rɔ okʂɔt̪ɔ os̪pɔrɕit̪
omɔrɔ s̪ɔrbat̪mɔkɔ s̪t̪ʰit̪iɕil̪ n̪iɕt͡ɕit̪
od̪ɽiɕd͡zɔ okʂɔmɔ ɕɔbd̪ɔ d̪bara
ebɔŋ os̪ɔŋl̪ɔɡɔn̪ɔ b̤aben̪ s̪ɔrbɔd̪a n̪id͡ʑei
eb̤abe at̪ma ̤ɡ̤ɔোʂɔna kɔra he̯ɔ t̪ahɔl̪e t̪umi kemɔn̪ɔ hɔbe
eta d͡ʑen̪eo d̪uঃkʰɔ kɔrɔো kɔkʰɔn̪ɔ t̪ɔোmar d̪uঃkʰɔ kɔra ut͡ɕit̪ n̪e̯ɔ
kib̤abe d͡zɔd̪i apn̪i ɕun̪t̪e pan̪ d͡ze l̪ɔোkɔti n̪ɔt̪un̪mɽit̪
ki s̪ɔd̪d͡zɔ d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ n̪eoe̯a man̪uʂer mɔt̪ɔো ekʰn̪o d͡ʑibit̪ man̪uʂ
eki bid̪d͡zɔman̪ at̪ma t̪umi ki kɔ̃d̪ɔbe
d͡ʑɔn̪mer ɕeʂ mɽit̪d͡zu mɽit̪d͡zur ɕeʂ

d͡za on̪d͡zɔt̪ʰae̯ ̤ɡ̤ɔtɔt̪e pare n̪a d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ
d͡ʑibɔn̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪er ot͡ɕet̪ɔn̪ɔ as̪e mɽit̪d͡zu

bis̪me̯ɔkɔrɔ bis̪me̯ɔkɔrɔ t͡ɕin̪t̪a kɔra

d͡zar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kɔʂtɔ kɔra d͡zae̯ n̪a। apn̪ar oŋɕɔ kɔrun̪
apn̪ar n̪am mɔn̪e rakʰben̪ ebɔŋ kɔ̃pɔben̪ n̪a

bojd̪̤ d͡zud̪d̪̤er t͡ɕee̯e d͡zɔোd̪d̪̤a kʰuɕi
kar kat͡ɕʰe d͡zud̪d̪̤er an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ as̪eas̪e ekʰɔn̪ɔkar mɔt̪ɔো
ɡɔৌrɔbɔme̯ɔ ebɔŋ n̪d͡zad͡zd͡zɔ oprɔt̪d͡zaɕit̪ t̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kʰɔোl̪a

kɔrt̪ɔbd͡zɔ ar kad͡ʑ t͡ɕɔl̪es̪e pap hɔbe
ar d͡zara as̪be t̪ara t̪ɔোmake opman̪ɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪ɔbe

rɔkt̪er man̪uʂd̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ mɽit̪d͡zur t͡ɕee̯e s̪ɔhd͡zɔ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe

t̪ɔোmake n̪ie̯e t̪ikt̪ɔ kɔt̪ʰabart̪a t͡ɕʰɔɽabe upɔhas̪ kɔrɔt̪e
t̪ɔোmar d͡ze birɔt̪bɔ t͡ɕʰil̪ ki b̤aɡɔd͡zɔ pɔt̪ɔn̪ɔ hɔt̪e pare

ot̪eb otʰ he kun̪t̪iput̪rɔ bɔn̪d̪̤ɔn̪i

d͡zemɔn̪ɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪ apn̪ar kat͡ɕʰe eki rɔkɔmɔ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ ba bed̪n̪a

d͡zɔd̪io s̪ɔmpɔd̪ɔ ebɔŋ kʂɔmɔt̪a ke s̪ɔbɔt͡ɕee̯e beɕi kamn̪a kɔre
at̪mar n̪d͡zun̪ɔt̪ɔmɔ s̪t̪ʰirt̪a emɔn̪ɔ n̪d͡zun̪ɔt̪ɔmɔ d̪̤ɔre rakʰun̪

d̪ekʰো d͡zemɔn̪ɔ ekti td͡zaŋkɔ d͡ʑɔl̪ɔ d̤el̪e d̪ee̯

pɔbit̪rɔ l̪ekʰar td͡zaŋkɔ t̪ʰeke s̪ɔkɔl̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ patʰd͡zɔ।

dan̪e dan̪e kad͡ʑ kɔrar s̪ɔtʰik kad͡ʑ hɔোkɔ

t̪ɔোmar d̪̤armikt̪a s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ n̪id͡ʑeke ekpaɕe ɸel̪e
l̪ab̤ ebɔŋ d͡zɔোɡɔd͡zɔt̪ake ̤ɡ̤ɽina kɔra s̪ɔman̪
b̤al̪ ba mɔn̪d̪ɔ s̪amd͡zɔt̪a
d͡zɔোɡɔ he̯ɔ t̪akoe̯a he̯ɔ
t̪ɔbuo s̪ɔtʰik kad͡ʑ
kɔmɔ on̪ek kɔmɔ s̪ɔtʰik t͡ɕin̪t̪aɕil̪ mɔn̪er t͡ɕee̯e।
t̪ɔোmar at̪mae̯ aɕre̯ɔ t͡ɕao s̪ekʰan̪e t̪ɔোmar s̪bɔrɡɔ at͡ɕʰe
t̪ar upɔhar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ pund͡zɔ on̪us̪ɔrɔnɔ d͡zara t̪ad̪er t̪irɔs̪kar
biɕud̪d̪̤ɔ b̤ɔkt̪ir mɔn̪ekʰan̪eo
b̤al̪োmɔn̪d̪ɔke s̪ɔman̪b̤abe d̪ure rakʰe
t̪ad̪er upɔrɔ d̪ie̯e d͡zaoe̯a। biɕud̪d̪̤ɔ b̤ɔkt̪ir d̪ike
n̪id͡ʑeke ut̪s̪ɔrɡɔ kɔrun̪ n̪ikʰũtə d̪̤d͡zan̪er s̪at̪ʰe
as̪e n̪ikʰũtə kad͡ʑ ebɔŋ s̪ɔtʰik hɽid̪e̯er ut̪t̪ʰan̪
arো n̪iɕt͡ɕit̪ karɔnɔ t̪ara kɔোn̪ɔ l̪ab̤ t͡ɕae̯ n̪a
ɕɔrirer bd͡zan̪dɔ t̪ʰeke d̪̤ape d̪̤ape
an̪ɔn̪d̪er s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ as̪n̪e। d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ t̪ɔোmar d̪ɽiɽ̤ at̪ma
d͡ʑ̤eɽe ɸel̪et͡ɕʰe s̪ei d͡ʑɔtɔbɔd̪d̪̤ɔ orakɔl̪ɔ
d͡za od͡ʑnɔt̪ae̯ pɔt̪ʰɔ d̪ekʰabe t̪ɔkʰɔn̪ɔ t̪a uɽbe
d͡za os̪bikar kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe ba bɔl̪a he̯et͡ɕʰe t̪ar prɔt̪i ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔ obɔhel̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
ei b̤abe ba s̪ei b̤abe mɔt̪ɔbad̪er rite।
purোhit̪er bid̪d͡zae̯ ar kɔʂtɔ he̯ɔ n̪a
n̪irapd̪e bɔ̃t͡ɕɔbe ebɔŋ n̪iɕt͡ɕit̪ obit͡ɕl̪it̪ɔb̤abe n̪ɔmit̪
d̪̤d͡zan̪er upɔrɔ। ei d͡zɔোɡɔ ebɔŋ ɕan̪t̪i
ord͡ʑun̪।
d͡ze otɔl̪ɔ hɽid̪e̯ɔ at͡ɕʰe t̪ar t͡ɕihn̪ɔ ki
pɔbit̪rɔ d̪̤d͡zan̪e n̪iɕt͡ɕit̪ kib̤abe
keɕɔbɔ amra t̪ar bɔkt̪ɽit̪a d͡ʑan̪i s̪e bɔs̪e s̪e n̪ɔɽe
on̪d͡zan̪d͡zɔ puruʂd̪er mɔt̪ɔ
kɽiʂnɔ।
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ ek he pɽit̪ʰar put̪rɔ
akaŋkʂa t̪d͡zaɡ kɔra d͡za mɔn̪ɔke n̪aɽa d̪ee̯
t̪ar at̪mar mɔd̪̤d͡ze t̪ar at̪mar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ purnɔ s̪an̪t̪bɔn̪a kʰũd͡ʒe pae̯
t̪in̪i d͡zɔোɡɔ l̪ab̤ kɔret͡ɕʰen̪s̪ei man̪uʂ
d̪uঃkʰe n̪iraɕ he̯ɔ n̪a ebɔŋ an̪ɔn̪d̪e
an̪ɔn̪d̪it̪ n̪a t͡ɕaper baire bas̪ kɔra
abeɡ b̤e̯ɔ ebɔŋ raɡ ɕan̪t̪ɔ obɔs̪t̪ʰae̯ s̪t̪ʰir
ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪ɔrɔ mɔn̪ɔn̪emɔn̪ɔ ekti
ki mun̪i ki ɽiʂi s̪ɔt̪d͡zikarer obɔs̪ɔrɔ
t̪in̪i d͡ze keu n̪a ebɔŋ kɔোt̪ʰao 
maŋs̪er bɔn̪d̪̤ɔn̪ɔ d̪bara kʰarap d͡ʑin̪is̪ ebɔŋ b̤al̪ ɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔre
hɔt̪aɕad͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ ba ul̪l̪as̪it̪ n̪e̯ɔ d͡zemɔn̪ɔ
prɔd͡ʑnar s̪ɔrɔl̪ɔ t͡ɕihn̪ɔ bɔhɔn̪ɔ kɔre d͡zin̪i ãkəben
d͡ʑnan̪i kɔt͡ɕt͡ɕʰɔpɔ d͡zemɔn̪ɔ t̪ar t͡ɕar pa n̪irapd̪e tan̪e
er d̤al̪er n̪it͡ɕe t̪ar pɔ̃t͡ɕɔti d̪urbɔl̪ɔ in̪d̪rie̯ ɸire as̪e
biɕbɔ t̪ʰeke at̪mar bakl̪er od̪̤in̪e
ar kɔোn̪ɔta t̪ad̪er l̪ant͡ɕʰit̪ kɔre emɔn̪ɔ ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ amar rad͡ʑkumar
d͡ʑnan̪er t͡ɕihn̪ɔ at͡ɕʰe d͡ʑin̪is̪ d͡ze in̪d̪rie̯ t͡ɕaoe̯a
s̪bɔɕas̪it̪ t̪ʰeke bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ rakʰa n̪a as̪e
t̪ar kʂud̪̤a opare d͡ze t̪ʰake
prɔs̪t̪ʰan̪ ar d͡ʑaɡan̪ো n̪a t̪ɔbuo s̪ud͡zোɡɔ hɔt̪e pare
he kun̪t̪iput̪rɔ d͡ze ekti n̪ie̯ɔn̪t̪rit̪ mɔn̪ɔ
kit͡ɕʰu s̪ɔme̯ɔ on̪ub̤ɔbɔ kɔrɔbe in̪d̪rie̯ɔd͡ʑ̤ɔɽɔ d͡ʑ̤aɽu ar kus̪t̪i
ɕikɔɽɔ d̪bara d̪ɽiɽ̤ at̪mɔn̪ie̯ɔn̪t̪rɔnɔ t̪ake ɸire pet̪e d̪in̪
t̪ar rad͡ʑd͡zɔ t̪ake eti d͡ʑe̯ɔ kɔrɔt̪e d̪in̪ ebɔŋ bɔs̪ɔt̪e d̪in̪
amar ob̤iprae̯ upɔrɔ ekmat̪rɔ s̪ei man̪uʂtii d͡ʑnan̪i
n̪id͡ʑer ae̯ɔt̪t̪ɔ ke rakʰe d͡zɔd̪i ekti
in̪d̪rie̯ bɔs̪t̪ur upɔrɔ t͡ɕin̪t̪a s̪ekʰan̪e s̪priŋs̪ɔ
akɔrʂɔnɔ akɔrʂɔnɔ t̪ʰeke it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa d͡ʑɔn̪mae̯
akaŋkʂar ɕikʰa prɔt͡ɕɔndɔ abeɡ abeɡ bɔŋɕɔbɽid̪d̪̤i kɔre
bepɔrɔোe̯at̪a t̪arɔpɔrɔ s̪mɽit̪is̪ɔbɔ biɕbas̪ɔ̤ɡ̤at̪ɔkɔt̪a
mɔhɔt̪ɔ ud̪d̪eɕd͡zɔ d͡zet̪e d̪in̪ ebɔŋ mɔn̪ɔke s̪ɔn̪t̪uʂtɔ kɔrun̪
ud̪d̪eɕd͡zɔ mɔn̪ɔ man̪uʂ s̪ɔbi purbabɔs̪t̪ʰae̯।
kin̪t̪u d͡zɔd̪i keu in̪d̪rie̯er bɔs̪t̪u n̪ie̯e kad͡ʑ kɔre
prem n̪e̯ɔ ebɔŋ ̤ɡ̤ɽina n̪e̯ɔ t̪ad̪er t̪ojri kɔra
t̪ɔ̃rɔ mukt̪ɔ at̪make s̪eba kɔrun̪ d͡za prɔb̤uke ɕan̪t̪ɔb̤abe biɕram d̪ee̯
l̪ɔো d͡zemɔn̪ɔ ekti man̪uʂ prɔɕan̪t̪i as̪e
ebɔŋ s̪ei prɔɕan̪t̪i t̪ʰeke utʰbe
t̪ar part̪ʰib d͡zɔn̪t̪rɔnar s̪ɔmapt̪i ebɔŋ n̪irame̯ɔ
d͡zehet̪u it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa ɕas̪it̪ at̪make ɕan̪t̪i d̪ee̯।
oɕas̪n̪er at̪ma t̪ar n̪e̯ɔ
t̪ar n̪id͡ʑer s̪ɔmpɔrkeo d͡ʑnan̪ n̪ei। d͡zar ob̤ab t͡ɕʰil̪
kib̤abe prɔɕan̪t̪i bɽid̪d̪̤i ebɔŋ eta t͡ɕai
kɔোt̪ʰa t̪ʰeke s̪e s̪ukʰer aɕa kɔrɔbe
mɔn̪ɔ
d͡ze n̪id͡ʑeke in̪d̪rie̯ prɔd̪ɔrɕɔn̪ɔ on̪us̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔrɔt̪e d̪ee̯
t̪ar prɔd͡ʑnar ɕirɔd̪ɔ̃ɽa t͡ɕʰĩɽe d͡zat͡ɕt͡ɕʰe
ebɔŋ ̤ɡ̤urnid͡ʑ̤ɽer t̪ɔrɔŋɡer mɔd̪̤d͡ze ekti d͡ʑahad͡ʑer mɔt̪ɔো t͡ɕal̪n̪a kɔre
d̪̤bɔŋs̪ɔ ebɔŋ mɽit̪d͡zur d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ɕud̪̤u t̪ar s̪at̪ʰe mɔhan̪ d͡zubrad͡ʑ
d͡zar in̪d̪rie̯ in̪d̪rie̯er d͡ʑin̪is̪ d̪bara prɔb̤abit̪ he̯ɔ n̪a
ɕud̪̤umat̪rɔ t̪ar s̪at̪ʰe d͡ze t̪ar prɔb̤ut̪bɔ d̪̤ɔre rakʰe
prɔd͡ʑna n̪ikʰũtə d̪ekʰae̯। mad͡ʑ̤rat̪riɡɔl̪ɔোmɔ ki
al̪োkɔhin̪ at̪mar kat͡ɕʰe d͡ʑaɡɔrɔt̪ɔ d̪in̪ d͡ʑbɔl̪e
t̪ar s̪pɔʂtɔ d̪ɽiʂtit̪e ki d͡ʑaɡɔrɔt̪ɔ d̪in̪ his̪abe mɔn̪e he̯ɔ
rat̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ pɔrit͡ɕit̪ od͡ʑnɔt̪ar ̤ɡ̤ɔn̪ɔ rat̪
t̪ar s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔd̪ɔrɕɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕɔোkʰer kat͡ɕʰe। emɔn̪ɔ s̪ad̪̤u
ar s̪aɡrer mɔt̪ɔো d̪in̪e d̪in̪e prapt̪i
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ b̤umi t̪ʰeke bɔn̪d͡za d͡za kɔkʰɔn̪o upt͡ɕe pɔɽe n̪a
er s̪imarekʰa l̪aɸat͡ɕt͡ɕʰe n̪a t͡ɕʰaɽbe n̪a
n̪ɔd̪i d̪bara kʰaoe̯an̪ো kin̪t̪u t̪ad̪er d̪bara os̪ɸit̪
t̪ai n̪ikʰũtə ek t̪ar at̪mar s̪ɔmud̪re
in̪d̪rie̯ d͡ʑɔɡɔt̪e d͡ʑad̪ubid̪d͡zar s̪rɔোt̪ɔ d̤el̪e d̪ee̯
t̪ara t̪ake d͡zemɔn̪ɔ kʰũd͡ʒe pae̯ t̪emɔn̪ɔ kɔোn̪ɔো hɔttɔɡɔোl̪ɔ t͡ɕʰaɽai t͡ɕʰeɽe d̪ee̯
t̪ad̪er ɕrɔd̪d̪̤a n̪ibed̪ɔn̪ɔ kin̪t̪u baki s̪aɡɔrɔ
hd͡zɔ̃ d͡zara maŋs̪er d͡ʑɔোe̯al̪ d͡ʑ̤ɔ̃kat͡ɕt͡ɕʰe
prɔb̤u b̤ɽit̪d͡zɔ n̪e̯ɔ t̪ar kamn̪a bas̪ kɔre mukt̪ɔ kɔra
ohɔŋkar t̪ʰeke abeɡ t̪ʰeke n̪id͡ʑer pap t̪ʰeke
prɔɕan̪t̪ir t͡ɕʰɔো̃ja he pɽit̪ʰar put̪rɔ
d͡ze brɔhmer obɔs̪t̪ʰa kɔোn̪ɔো b̤e̯ɔ n̪ei
kɔkʰɔn̪ɔ d͡ze ɕeʂ d̪̤ape pɔৌt͡ɕʰe d͡zae̯ s̪e d͡zekʰan̪e it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa bas̪ kɔrɔbe
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ s̪e pare t̪ɔkʰɔn̪i mɽit̪d͡zubɔrɔnɔ kɔrɔ emɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔbɔ pl̪ein̪iŋ t̪ʰeke t͡ɕɔl̪e d͡zae̯
n̪irbanke aɕirbad̪ kɔra d̪ebt̪ad̪er s̪at̪ʰe prapt̪i।
ekʰan̪e d̪bit̪ie̯ od̪̤d͡zae̯ ɕeʂ kɔrun̪। b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar
ɕirোn̪am s̪aŋkʰd͡zɔd͡zɔোɡɔ
ot̪ʰba mɔt̪ɔbad̪er bi।




od̪̤d͡zae̯ 
ord͡ʑun̪।
t̪umi d͡zɔ̃rɔ s̪t̪ɔbɔ s̪ɔkɔl̪ɔ mɔrɔnɔɕil̪ d͡ʑɔn̪ard̪ɔn̪ɔ
d̪̤d͡zan̪ ekti d͡ʑin̪is̪ d͡zɔd̪i
kɔrmer t͡ɕee̯e t̪ail̪e mɔha keɕɔbɔ
t̪umi ki amake ei b̤e̯ɔŋkɔrɔ l̪ɔɽaie̯e prɔrɔোt͡ɕit̪ kɔrɔ
ekʰɔn̪ɔ ki t̪ɔোmar s̪ɔn̪d̪ehɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ kɔt̪ʰabart̪ae̯ ami birɔkt̪ɔ
amake ekti kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪un̪ ebɔŋ amake obɔɕd͡zi bɔl̪un̪
kɔোn̪ɔ ras̪t̪a d̪ie̯e ami b̤al̪ ɕeʂ kʰũd͡ʒe pab
kɽiʂnɔ।
ami t̪ɔোmae̯ bɔl̪et͡ɕʰil̪am he n̪ird̪ɔোʂɔ prɔb̤u d̪uti pɔt̪ʰɔ at͡ɕʰe
ei biɕbɔke d̪ekʰan̪ো he̯et͡ɕʰe d͡ʑnan̪er d̪uti s̪kul̪।
prɔt̪ʰɔmɔ
s̪aŋkʰd͡zer d͡za kad͡ʑer upae̯e s̪ɔŋrɔkʂɔnɔ kɔre
karɔnɔ d̪bara n̪ird̪̤arit̪ pɔrɔbɔrt̪i d͡zɔোɡɔ d͡za bid
d̪̤d͡zan̪ d̪bara ord͡ʑɔn̪ɔ ad̪̤d͡zat̪mikb̤abe
t̪ɔbuo era ek kɔোn̪ɔো man̪uʂ kad͡ʑ t̪ʰeke rehai pabe n̪a
kɔrmɔ pɔrihar kɔre n̪a ebɔŋ keu as̪be n̪a
n̪it͡ɕʰɔkɔ pɔripurnɔt̪ar kat͡ɕʰe bis̪ɔrd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ d̪ie̯e।
n̪a ebɔŋ s̪ɔme̯er kɔোn̪ɔ s̪ɔŋkʂepe d͡ze kɔোn̪ɔ s̪ɔme̯ɔ
kɔোn̪ɔ kɔrmɔhin̪ biɕram t̪ar prɔkɽit̪ir n̪ie̯ɔmɔ
t̪ake bad̪̤d͡zɔ kɔre emɔn̪ɔki on̪it͡ɕt͡ɕʰae̯o kad͡ʑ kɔrɔt̪e
t͡ɕin̪t̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ob̤in̪ɔbɔ kad͡ʑ he̯ɔ। d͡zin̪i bɔs̪e at͡ɕʰen̪
maŋs̪er s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d͡zɔn̪t̪rɔke d̪ɔmɔn̪ɔ kɔre
t̪ɔbuo ol̪ɔs̪ɔ hɽid̪e̯e t̪ad̪er kɔt̪ʰa b̤abt͡ɕʰe
od͡zোɡɔd͡zɔ ebɔŋ d̪ɔোʂi b̤ɔn̪der b̤umika pal̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔre
kin̪t̪u d͡ze d̪ɽiɽ̤ d̪eher s̪ebae̯ mɔn̪ɔ d̪ie̯e
d͡zɔোɡɔd͡zɔ kad͡ʑer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ t̪ar n̪ɔɕbɔrɔ kʂɔmɔt̪a t͡ɕʰeɽe d̪ee̯
l̪ab̤ t͡ɕai n̪a ord͡ʑun̪ d͡zemɔn̪ɔ ekti
s̪ɔmman̪ɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ। t̪ɔোmar bɔrad̪d̪ɔ tas̪kɔ kɔrɔো
kɔrmɔ ol̪ɔs̪ɔt̪ar t͡ɕee̯e ut̪t̪ɔmɔ
d̪eher d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕɔl̪e n̪a kad͡ʑer ob̤ab।
pɔbit̪rɔt̪ar ekta kad͡ʑ at͡ɕʰe
biɕbabɔd̪d̪̤ɔ pɔriɕrɔmer biprit̪e d͡za bɔ̃d̪̤e n̪a
biɕbɔs̪t̪ɔ at̪ma d͡zemɔn̪ɔ part̪ʰib kɔrt̪ɔbd͡zɔ kɔri
it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa t̪ʰeke mukt̪ɔ ebɔŋ apn̪i b̤al̪ s̪ɔnt͡ɕal̪ɔn̪ɔ hɔbe
t̪ɔোmar s̪bɔrɡie̯ ud̪d̪eɕd͡zɔ। kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪un̪ prɔd͡ʑapt̪i
ɕurut̪e d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ man̪uʂ t̪ojri he̯et͡ɕʰil̪
ebɔŋ man̪ɔbɔd͡ʑat̪ir s̪at̪ʰe t̪d͡zaɡ eti kɔrun̪
kad͡ʑ bɔl̪id̪an̪ bɽid̪d̪̤i ebɔŋ ɡun̪
t̪d͡zaɡ s̪ɔhɔ ei hɔbe kamd̪uk
apn̪ar prɔt͡ɕur ɡab̤i t̪ar d̪ud̪̤ ɸirie̯e d̪it͡ɕt͡ɕʰe
s̪ɔbɔ prat͡ɕurd͡zɔ er d̪bara d̪ebt̪ad̪er pud͡ʑa kɔra
d̪ebt̪ara apn̪ake kɽipa d̪eben̪। d͡ze maŋs̪ɔ apn̪i akaŋkʂa
d̪ebt̪ara ɕrɔmɔke mɔnd͡ʑur kɔrɔben̪ d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ eti ort̪ʰɔ prɔd̪an̪ kɔrɔbe
bed̪iɕikʰae̯ d̪ɔɕɔmaŋɕɔ। kin̪t̪u d͡zɔd̪i keu kʰae̯
pɽit̪ʰibir ɸɔl̪ɔ d̪e̯ame̯ɔ s̪bɔrɡer prɔt̪id̪an̪
pɔriɕrɔmer upɔhar n̪e̯ɔ d͡ze t͡ɕɔোrɔ t̪ar pɽit̪ʰibi t̪ʰeke t͡ɕuri kɔre।
d͡zara t̪ad̪er kɔোrɔban̪ir pɔrɔ kʰabar kʰae̯
d̪ɔোʂɔ t̪ʰeke prɔs̪t̪ʰan̪ kɔrun̪ kin̪t̪u ekti b̤ɔোd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕʰɔɽie̯e d͡zara
s̪ɔbɔ n̪id͡ʑer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ pap kʰae̯ ebɔŋ pap pan̪ kɔre।
kʰad̪d͡zɔ d̪bara d͡ʑibit̪ he̯ɔ bɽiʂti as̪e kʰabar
ebɔŋ bɽiʂti as̪e pɔbit̪rɔ t̪d͡zaɡer d̪bara
ebɔŋ bɔl̪id̪an̪ kɔra he̯ɔ pɔriɕrɔmer d̪ɔɕɔmaŋɕɔ d̪ie̯e
eib̤abe kɔrmɔ brɔhmar d͡zin̪i ek
ekmat̪rɔ s̪ɔrbɔbd͡zapi s̪ɔbɔ s̪ɔme̯e
t̪d͡zaɡe upɔs̪t̪ʰit̪। s̪e d͡ze birɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰake
ei mɔhan̪ biɕber ̤ɡ̤urnae̯man̪ t͡ɕaka s̪ahad͡zd͡zɔ kɔrar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
n̪id͡ʑer ol̪ɔs̪ɔ bɔোd̪̤ɔke at͡ɕt͡ɕʰɔn̪n̪ɔ kɔre harie̯e d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ d͡zapɔn̪ɔ kɔre
l̪ɔd͡ʑd͡ʑad͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ ebɔŋ n̪irɔrt̪ʰɔkɔ। n̪id͡ʑer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ bid̪d͡zɔman̪
at̪mɔken̪d̪rik eka n̪id͡ʑeke s̪eba kɔra
t̪ar kɔোn̪ɔ oŋɕɔ n̪ei kit͡ɕʰui ord͡ʑit̪ he̯ɔn̪i
kɔোn̪ɔ kit͡ɕʰu t̪ojri ba okatd͡zɔ t̪ake s̪pɔrɕɔ kɔre n̪a aɕa n̪ei
pɽit̪ʰibir s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ s̪ahad͡zd͡zɔ
t̪ar upɔrɔ n̪irb̤ɔrɔ kɔre।# ot̪eb apn̪ar kad͡ʑ n̪ird̪̤arit̪
at̪mar s̪at̪ʰe os̪ɔŋl̪ɔɡɔn̪ɔ an̪ɔn̪d̪er s̪at̪ʰe s̪ɔmpad̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔrun̪
d͡zehet̪u pl̪ein̪ diuti ​​md͡zan̪ parɔɸɔrɔmd͡zan̪s̪e
t̪ar s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ an̪ɔn̪d̪er maun̪tɔ eka kad͡ʑ kɔre
d͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ o prat͡ɕin̪ s̪ad̪̤ɔkɔɡɔnɔ aɕirbad̪ɔprapt̪ɔ hɔn̪ɔ
t̪ɔd̪upri apn̪ar d̪̤ɔrɔner s̪ɔmɔrt̪ʰɔn̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
o্d͡zakɔɕɔn̪ɔ apn̪ar al̪iŋɡɔn̪ɔ kɔra ut͡ɕit̪ d͡ʑnan̪ira ki bet͡ɕʰe n̪ee̯
murkʰɔ l̪ɔোkera n̪ee̯ s̪era puruʂd̪er ki
d͡ʑɔn̪ɔt̪a on̪us̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔrɔbe। amar d̪ike t̪akao
t̪umi pɽit̪ʰar put̪rɔ t̪in̪ti bis̪t̪ɽit̪ biɕbe
ami kɔোn̪ɔ pɔriɕrɔme abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ n̪i kɔোn̪ɔ ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪ae̯ abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ n̪i
s̪kel̪ kɔrar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ opekʂa kɔrɔt͡ɕʰe kɔোn̪ɔ upɔhar paoe̯ar baki n̪ei
t̪ɔbuo ami ekʰan̪e ob̤in̪e̯ɔ kɔri ebɔŋ d͡zɔd̪i ami ob̤in̪e̯ɔ n̪a kɔri
an̪t̪ɔrik ebɔŋ s̪ɔt̪ɔrkɔ d͡zara amar d̪ike t̪akae̯
n̪ird̪eɕn̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ abar al̪ɔs̪d͡ze dube d͡zaoe̯a
karɔnɔ ami ̤ɡ̤umie̯et͡ɕʰil̪am b̤al̪ t̪ʰeke prɔt̪d͡zakʰd͡zan̪ kɔrɔbɔ
ebɔŋ ami pɽit̪ʰibir ad̪eɕ b̤ɔŋɡɔ ebɔŋ prɔt̪iɕrut̪i kɔra ut͡ɕit̪
t̪ar bɔŋɕer s̪ɔrbɔn̪aɕ b̤ɔrɔt̪ɔ
od͡ʑan̪a pɔriɕrɔmer mɔt̪ɔো bɔোd̪̤er s̪at̪ʰe bibahit̪
t̪ai al̪োkit̪ pɔriɕrɔmɔ in̪d̪rie̯mukt̪ɔ kin̪t̪u s̪et kɔra d͡zak
biɕber mukt̪i ebɔŋ t̪ar an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ an̪t̪e
s̪ei s̪ɔhɔd͡ʑɔ bd͡zɔs̪t̪ɔ hɽid̪e̯e bɔpɔn̪ɔ kɔra n̪e̯ɔ
hɔt̪aɕar bid͡ʑ। hd͡zɔ̃ prɔt̪d͡zekke t̪ar b̤umika pal̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔrɔt̪e d̪in̪
s̪ɔbɔ kit͡ɕʰut̪ei s̪e kʰũd͡ʒe pae̯ obikɽit̪ at̪mar s̪at̪ʰe।
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪ s̪ɔrbɔt̪rɔ prɔkɽit̪i d̪bara t̪ojri kɔra he̯ɔ
ɡuner mit̪ʰɔs̪krie̯ae̯।
bɔোka n̪id͡ʑer d̪bara prɔt̪arit̪ b̤abe eta ami kɔret͡ɕʰi
ebɔŋ d͡za ami t̪ojri kɔret͡ɕʰi kin̪t̪uahɔ t̪umi ɕɔkt̪iɕal̪i s̪ɔɕɔs̪t̪rɔ d͡zubrad͡ʑ
ekti b̤al̪patʰit̪ mɔn̪ɔ n̪atɔkɔti d͡ʑen̪e
in̪d̪rie̯ d͡ʑɔɡɔt̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze d̪ɽiɕd͡zɔman̪ d͡ʑin̪is̪
ebɔŋ kib̤abe ɡunabl̪i d͡zɔোɡɔd͡zɔ hɔt̪e hɔbe
emɔn̪ɔki t̪ar kad͡ʑ t̪ʰekeo d̪ure t̪ʰake। oɕikʂit̪
t̪ad̪er s̪at̪ʰe miɕe t̪ʰakো prɔkɽit̪ir pɔt̪ʰɔ n̪a d͡ʑen̪e
on̪it͡ɕt͡ɕʰakɽit̪ d̪̤ir ebɔŋ n̪is̪t̪ed͡ʑ s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ l̪ɔkʂd͡zɔ।
d͡zara al̪ো at͡ɕʰe t̪ara t̪ɔোmar pɔd̪ɔs̪kʰɔl̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔrɔbe n̪a
kin̪t̪u t̪ɔোmar s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ paon̪a amar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
ob̤d͡zɔn̪t̪ɔrinb̤abe ken̪d̪rib̤ut̪ d̪̤d͡zan̪er s̪at̪ʰe
kɔোn̪ɔ l̪ab̤ t͡ɕai n̪a s̪ɔn̪t̪uʂtɔ n̪irmɔl̪ɔ
is̪d͡zut̪e ɡaɸil̪ɔl̪ɔɽai d͡zara rakʰbe
amar ad̪eɕ eib̤abe d͡ʑnan̪i ebɔŋ it͡ɕt͡ɕʰuk hɽid̪e̯ɔ
t̪ad̪er kɔrmer s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ s̪ɔmɔs̪d͡za t̪ʰeke pɔrit̪d͡zaɡ kɔrun̪
kin̪t̪u d͡zara amar ad̪eɕ upekʂa kɔre
ei b̤ebe d͡ze t̪ara d͡ʑan̪e kit͡ɕʰui d͡ʑan̪e n̪a ebɔŋ kʂɔt̪ir mukʰe pɔɽe
bib̤ran̪t̪ɔ ebɔŋ bɔোka s̪ut̪ʰ n̪ird̪eɕit̪ ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ
t̪ar d̪̤ɔrɔner dɔt̪ʰɔ d͡za t̪ake s̪ɔbɔt͡ɕee̯e beɕi man̪ae̯ t̪a on̪us̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔre
ebɔŋ t̪ad̪er d̪̤ɔrɔn̪er n̪imn̪ɔ prani bɽit̪ʰa
l̪ɔɽɔt͡ɕʰe ain̪ l̪ab̤er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ। pre̯ɔোd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ eta hɔt̪e hɔbe
in̪d̪rie̯er bɔs̪t̪u in̪d̪rie̯ke al̪োɽit̪ kɔrɔbe
pɔt͡ɕʰɔn̪d̪opɔt͡ɕʰɔn̪d̪ɔ t̪ɔbuo al̪োkit̪ man̪uʂ
ɕɔt̪ru d͡ʑen̪eo eɡul̪োrɔ kat͡ɕʰe har man̪t͡ɕʰe n̪a।
obɕeʂe ei b̤al̪ d͡ze ek
t̪ar n̪id͡ʑer kad͡ʑ s̪e bd͡zɔrt̪ʰɔ hɔl̪eo
t̪ar n̪id͡ʑer kad͡ʑ n̪a d͡zɔd̪io t̪ara b̤al̪ mɔn̪e he̯ɔ
d̪ae̯it̪bɔ pal̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔrɔt̪e ɡie̯e mara d͡zaoe̯a os̪us̪t̪ʰɔ n̪e̯ɔ
kin̪t̪u d͡ze on̪d͡zɔ ras̪t̪a kʰũd͡ʒəbe s̪e ekʰn̪o ̤ɡ̤ure beɽabe।
ord͡ʑun̪।
t̪ɔbuo bɔl̪un̪ ɡuru man̪uʂ ki d͡ʑɔোrɔ kɔre

kam eta
abeɡ eta on̪d̪̤ɔkarer d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ
d͡za t̪ake d̪̤akka d̪ee̯। prɔbɔl̪ɔ kʂud̪̤a
papi ebɔŋ ɕɔkt̪iɕal̪i eiman̪uʂer ɕɔt̪ru
d̪̤ɔো̃ja d͡zemɔn̪ɔ s̪ad̪a aɡun̪ t̪emn̪i d͡ʑɔŋ d̪̤ɔra mɔrit͡ɕa
mɔŋɡɔl̪ɔ ud͡ʑd͡ʑbɔl̪ɔ ae̯n̪a d͡zemɔn̪ɔ ɡɔrb̤ɔ ̤ɡ̤ire at͡ɕʰe
ɕiɕuti od͡ʑat̪ t̪ai d͡ʑin̪is̪er d͡ʑɔɡɔt̪ɔ
ban̪ n̪ɔোŋra maŋs̪er ei kamn̪ae̯ abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ।
d͡ʑnan̪i pɔt̪ɔn̪ɔ t̪at̪e d̪̤ɔra pɔɽe oɕan̪t̪ɔ ɕɔt̪ru
eti d͡ʑnan̪er oɡnit̪ rup pɔrihit̪
n̪d͡zad͡zd͡zɔ kin̪t̪u prɔt̪arɔkɔ ekti ɕikʰa his̪abe s̪ukʂmɔ
in̪d̪rie̯ mɔn̪ɔ o d͡zukt̪i he kun̪t̪ir put̪rɔ
eta d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ l̪utʰ he̯ɔ eɡul̪ো n̪ie̯e kʰel̪ae̯
eta man̪uʂke paɡɔl̪ɔ kɔre prɔt̪arna kɔre t̪ake on̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre।
ot̪eb he b̤ɔrɔt̪ɔ s̪ɔn̪t̪an̪
apn̪ar hɽid̪e̯ɔ ɕas̪ɔn̪ɔ atke rakʰa in̪d̪rie̯
mit̪ʰd͡za n̪ɔrɔmɔ papke prɔt̪ihɔt̪ɔ kɔrun̪ d͡za 
d͡ʑnan̪ o bit͡ɕar hd͡zɔ̃ pɽit̪ʰibi ɕɔkt̪iɕal̪i
kin̪t̪u ki eta ɕɔkt̪iɕal̪i bɔোd͡ʑ̤a d͡zae̯ ebɔŋ mɔn̪ɔ
ɕɔkt̪iɕal̪i ebɔŋ s̪ɔbɔ ɕas̪ɔkɔ at̪ma ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔ 
ot̪eb d͡zin̪i s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ rad͡ʑɔt̪bɔ kɔren̪ t̪ake upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤i kɔre
apn̪ar n̪id͡ʑer at̪mae̯ at̪mar purnɔ ɕɔkt̪i rakʰun̪
d͡zud̪d̪̤ɔ ɕɔt̪ru ebɔŋ s̪ɔn̪d̪ehɔ pɔrad͡ʑit̪ kɔrun̪ prie̯ n̪ae̯ɔkɔ hɔt̪d͡za
ki ɕɔৌkʰin̪ akare t̪ɔোmake t̪aɽa kɔre ar biɕbas̪ɔ̤ɡ̤at̪ɔkɔt̪a kɔrɔbe
ekʰan̪e t̪ɽit̪ie̯ od̪̤d͡zae̯ ɕeʂ kɔrun̪। b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar

kɽiʂnɔ।
ei mɽit̪d͡zuhin̪ d͡zɔোɡɔ ei ɡɔb̤ir mil̪ɔn̪ɔ
ami bib̤as̪bɔt̪ake ɕikʰie̯et͡ɕʰi al̪োrɔ prɔb̤u
mɔn̪uke bib̤as̪bɔt̪a d̪ie̯et͡ɕʰe t̪in̪i
ikʂbakuke t̪ai l̪ain̪ n̪it͡ɕe pas̪
amar s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ rad͡ʑkie̯ ɽiʂid̪er। t̪arɔpɔrɔ bɔt͡ɕʰɔrer pɔrɔ bɔt͡ɕʰɔrɔ
s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ ml̪an̪ he̯e bil̪upt̪ɔ he̯e ɡel̪ mɔhie̯an̪ d͡zubrad͡ʑ
ekʰɔn̪ɔ abar apn̪ar kat͡ɕʰe ̤ɡ̤ɔোʂɔna kɔra hɔl̪ɔো
ei prat͡ɕin̪ bid̪d͡za ei rɔhɔs̪d͡zɔ s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ
d̪ekʰei t̪ɔোmae̯ b̤ɔোtari o bɔn̪d̪̤u pai।
ord͡ʑun̪।
t̪ɔোmar d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ prie̯ prɔb̤u ei pɔrɔbɔrt̪i d̪in̪e
ebɔŋ ud͡ʑd͡ʑbɔl̪ɔ bib̤as̪t̪ar purbɔbɔrt̪i s̪ɔme̯ɔ

ɕuru t̪ʰeke amii ɕikʰie̯et͡ɕʰil̪am
kɽiʂnɔ।
amar d͡ʑɔn̪mer n̪ɔbae̯ɔn̪ɔ bɔhuɡun
he̯et͡ɕʰe ord͡ʑun̪ ebɔŋ t̪ɔোmar d͡ʑɔn̪mero
kin̪t̪u amar ami d͡ʑan̪i ar t̪umi d͡ʑan̪ো n̪a
he t̪ɔোmar ɕɔt̪rud̪er hɔt̪d͡zakari d͡zɔd̪io ami hɔbɔ
od͡ʑat̪ obin̪ɔɕbɔrɔ obin̪ɔɕbɔrɔ
d͡ʑibit̪ s̪ɔbɔ kit͡ɕʰur pal̪ɔn̪ɔkɔrt̪a kɔmɔ n̪e̯ɔ
mae̯ar d̪bara amar d͡zad̪u d̪bara d͡za ami s̪td͡zampɔ
b̤as̪man̪ prɔkɽit̪iruper upɔrɔ ad̪i biɕal̪
ami as̪i ebɔŋ d͡zai ebɔŋ as̪i। d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ n̪d͡zae̯ɔpɔrae̯ɔnɔt̪a
prɔt̪d͡zakʰd͡zan̪ he b̤ɔrɔt̪ɔ d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ d̪uʂtɔt̪a
ɕɔkt̪iɕal̪i he̯ɔ ami be̯ɔs̪ɔ t̪ʰeke be̯ɔs̪e utʰi ebɔŋ ɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔri
d̪ɽiɕd͡zɔman̪ akɽit̪i ebɔŋ puruʂd̪er s̪at̪ʰe ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ man̪uʂke s̪ɔran̪ো
b̤al̪ke s̪ahad͡zd͡zɔ kɔra mɔn̪d̪ɔke pit͡ɕʰn̪e tʰel̪e d̪eoe̯a
ebɔŋ pund͡zɔke abar t̪ar as̪n̪e bɔs̪ie̯et͡ɕʰe।
pɽit̪ʰibit̪e amar d͡ʑɔn̪mer t͡ɕʰɔো̃ja s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ ke d͡ʑan̪e
ebɔŋ amar ojɕbɔrik kad͡ʑ d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ t̪in̪i maŋs̪ɔ t̪d͡zaɡ kɔren̪
er b̤ar ar rakʰe n̪a ar n̪it͡ɕe pɔɽe n̪a
part̪ʰib d͡ʑɔn̪me s̪e amar kat͡ɕʰe as̪e prie̯ rad͡ʑkumar
on̪ekei at͡ɕʰen̪ d͡zara as̪en̪ b̤e̯ɔ t̪ʰeke mukt̪i
raɡ t̪ʰeke it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa t̪ʰeke t̪ad̪er hɽid̪e̯ɔ rakʰa
amar upɔrɔ s̪t̪ʰiramar biɕbɔs̪t̪ɔɕud̪d̪̤ɔ
d͡ʑnan̪er pɔbit̪rɔ ɕikʰa d̪bara। ei d͡zemɔn̪ɔ
miɕe d͡zao amar s̪ɔt̪t̪ar s̪at̪ʰe। d͡ze amake pud͡ʑa kɔre
ami t̪ad̪er mɔhiman̪bit̪ kɔri kin̪t̪u s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑae̯ɡae̯ s̪ɔbɔ puruʂ
amar pɔt̪ʰe pɔɽɔbe d͡zɔd̪io d͡zara at̪ma
d͡za kad͡ʑer prɔt̪id̪an̪ t͡ɕae̯ t̪d͡zaɡ s̪bikar kɔre
ekʰɔn̪ɔ n̪imn̪ɔ d̪ebt̪ad̪er kat͡ɕʰe। ami t̪ɔোmake bɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰi
ekʰan̪e t̪ad̪er purɔs̪kar at͡ɕʰe। kin̪t̪u ami t̪in̪i
t͡ɕarti d͡ʑat̪i ban̪ie̯et͡ɕʰen̪ ebɔŋ t̪ad̪er ekti d͡ʑae̯ɡa b̤aɡ kɔret͡ɕʰen̪
t̪ad̪er ɡunabl̪i ebɔŋ upɔhar pɔre hd͡zɔ̃ ami
s̪ɽiʂtɔ ɕan̪t̪ime̯ɔ ami d͡ze bas̪
omɔrɔb̤abe s̪ei s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ n̪ɔɕbɔrɔ d͡ʑɔn̪mɔɡul̪i t̪ojri kɔret͡ɕʰen̪
kad͡ʑer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ mati amar s̪arɔmɔrmɔ n̪e̯ɔ kad͡ʑ hɔt͡ɕt͡ɕʰe
d͡ʑɔɽit̪ t͡ɕʰaɽa t̪ojri kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe
kɔrmɔ d̪bara okʰɔndit̪ kɔrmɔ t̪ake abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre n̪a
ebɔŋ t̪ai upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤i puran̪ো d͡zara s̪ɔbɔ s̪ad̪̤u
pɔrit̪raner d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ t͡ɕaoe̯a kad͡ʑ t̪umi kad͡ʑ kɔrɔো
ot̪it̪er d̪in̪e d͡zemɔn̪ɔ t̪ɔোmar pit̪ɽipuruʂra kɔret͡ɕʰil̪en̪।
t̪umi hɔt̪ɔb̤ɔmbɔ he̯e bɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰɔ eta aɡeo d͡ʑid͡ʑnas̪a kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe
ɡae̯ɔkɔ ebɔŋ ɽiʂid̪er d̪bara ob̤in̪e̯ɔ ki
ar ki n̪iʂkrie̯t̪a ami t̪ɔোmake ei ɕikʂa d̪eb
ebɔŋ d͡ʑen̪e apn̪i ɕikʰben̪ kɔোn̪ɔ kad͡ʑti bɔ̃t͡ɕae̯
ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔke obɔɕd͡zi ei t̪in̪ti d̪̤d͡zan̪ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe
kɔra n̪a kɔra ebɔŋ purbabɔs̪t̪ʰae̯। ekʰan̪e
kɔ̃ta ar on̪d̪̤ɔkar pɔt̪ʰɔ d͡ze d̪ekʰe s̪e
kib̤abe kɔrmɔ biɕram hɔt̪e pare biɕram kɔrmɔ t̪in̪i
bud̪d̪̤iman̪ mid t̪ar d̪̤ɔrɔn̪er t̪ar s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ at͡ɕʰe
t̪in̪i b̤al̪ kɔren̪ ob̤in̪e̯ɔ ba biɕram। bimukt̪ɔ
akaŋkʂar kɔ̃ta t̪ʰeke t̪ar s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ kad͡ʑe
s̪ɔt̪d͡zer ɕub̤rɔ aɡun̪e kɔrme puɽe pɔriʂkar
d͡ʑnan̪ira s̪ei man̪uʂke d͡ʑnan̪i bɔl̪e ebɔŋ emɔn̪ɔ ekti
kɔrmer ɸɔl̪ɔ t̪d͡zaɡ kɔre s̪ɔrbɔd̪a s̪ɔn̪t̪uʂtɔ।
s̪ɔrbɔd̪a s̪bɔs̪ɔn̪t̪uʂtɔ d͡zɔd̪i s̪e kad͡ʑ kɔre
emɔn̪ɔ kit͡ɕʰu kɔrɔben̪ n̪a d͡za t̪ar pɽit̪ʰɔkɔ at̪make d̪aɡ d̪ebe
d͡zab̤e̯ɔ o aɕa t̪d͡zaɡ kɔreat̪mɔke bɔɕib̤ut̪ kɔre
bahd͡zik abeɡ prɔt̪d͡zakʰd͡zan̪ ap ɸɔl̪ɔn̪ɔ
d̪eher pre̯ɔোd͡ʑɔn̪e ɕɔrir t͡ɕʰaɽa kit͡ɕʰui n̪ei bas̪ kɔre
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ paper mɔd̪̤d͡ze n̪ird̪ɔোʂɔ s̪ɔman̪ ɕan̪t̪it̪e
d͡za ̤ɡ̤ɔtɔt̪e pare t̪a n̪ie̯e ɕɔোke ot͡ɕɔl̪ɔ he̯e
an̪ɔn̪d̪e oprɔs̪t̪ut̪ on̪abil̪ eki
b̤al̪ ebɔŋ mɔn̪d̪ɔ b̤aɡd͡ze ekʰɔn̪ɔ abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ
kɔrmer bɔn̪d̪̤ɔn̪e। n̪a kin̪t̪u emɔn̪ɔ ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪er
d͡zar akaŋkʂa t͡ɕɔl̪e ɡet͡ɕʰe d͡zar at̪ma mukt̪i pee̯et͡ɕʰe
d͡zar hɽid̪e̯ɔ s̪ɔt̪d͡zer upɔrɔ prɔt̪iʂtʰit̪ emɔn̪ɔ ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪er
t̪in̪i d͡ze kad͡ʑ kɔren̪ t̪a t̪d͡zaɡer kad͡ʑ
d͡za biɕud̪d̪̤ɔb̤abe t͡ɕʰai ebɔŋ d̪̤ɔো̃jaj t͡ɕɔl̪e d͡zae̯
bed̪ir upɔrɔ ɡɔras̪ t̪ahɔl̪e s̪ɔbɔ iɕbɔrɔ
d͡zɔd͡ʑnɔ hɔl̪ɔ brɔhmɔ ̤ɡ̤i o ɕɔs̪d͡zɔ
ki brɔhmɔ oɡn̪ii brɔhmɔ maŋs̪ɔ s̪e kʰae̯
brɔhmɔ ebɔŋ brɔhmer kat͡ɕʰe t̪in̪i prapt̪ɔ hɔn̪ɔ
d͡zin̪i emɔn̪ɔ pɔd̪e brɔhmer d̪̤d͡zan̪ kɔren̪।
kit͡ɕʰu b̤ɔোtar at͡ɕʰe d͡zara d̪ebt̪ad̪er s̪eba kɔre
maŋs̪ɔ o bed̪ir d̪̤ɔো̃ja d̪ie̯e kin̪t̪u on̪d͡zɔ kit͡ɕʰu
ke s̪ukʂmɔ aɡun̪ d͡ʑbal̪ae̯ biɕud̪d̪̤ɔ at͡ɕar t̪ojri kɔre
pud͡ʑar it͡ɕt͡ɕʰae̯। d͡zar mɔd̪̤d͡ze t̪ara hɔোkɔ
ke d̪̤ir s̪ad̪a ɕikʰa ɡɔras̪
in̪d̪rie̯er an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ t͡ɕɔোkʰɔ o kan̪er an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ
b̤ul̪e d͡zaoe̯a kɔোmɔl̪ɔ bɔkt̪ɽit̪a ebɔŋ ɡan̪er ɕɔbd̪ɔ
ebɔŋ d͡zara s̪ɔt̪d͡zer mɔɕal̪ d̪ie̯e aɡun̪ d͡ʑbal̪ae̯
ekti l̪ukan̪ো bed̪ipat̪ʰrer upɔrɔ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ pɔোɽa
d͡zɔৌbɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ premer s̪ukʰ t̪d͡zaɡ kɔra
ebɔŋ d͡zara s̪ekʰan̪e t̪ad̪er s̪ɔmpɔd̪ɔ ut̪ɔs̪ɔrɡɔ kɔrar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ɕue̯e t̪ʰake
t̪ad̪er t̪ɔpɔs̪d͡za d̪̤d͡zan̪ t̪akoe̯a
s̪krɔোl̪ɔɡul̪i t̪ad̪er obit͡ɕl̪it̪ pɔɽa t̪ad̪er bid̪d͡za
d̪ir̤ɡ̤ɔ t̪ɔpɔs̪d͡za s̪ɔhɔ bed̪n̪ad̪ae̯ɔkɔb̤abe ord͡ʑit̪
ebɔŋ d͡zara n̪irbe at̪mɔt̪d͡zaɡ kɔre
t͡ɕin̪t̪ar ɕikʰa kʰaoe̯an̪োrɔ d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ t̪ad̪er n̪iঃɕbas̪e ãkun
ebɔŋ hɽid̪e̯ɔke ũt͡ʃute d̤el̪e d̪it̪e ɕbas̪ t͡ɕʰaɽun̪
prɔt̪iti prɔbeɕ bat̪as̪er b̤en̪ted͡ʑ pɔrit͡ɕal̪n̪a kɔra
pat͡ɕʰe ekti d̪ir̤ɡ̤ɔɕbas̪ pas̪ d͡za at̪make s̪ahad͡zd͡zɔ kɔre n̪a
ebɔŋ d͡zara d̪in̪e d̪in̪e pre̯ɔোd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ os̪bikar kɔre
bed̪iɕikʰae̯ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ d̪an̪ kɔrun̪
ɕɔrire aɡun̪ d͡ʑbɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰe। l̪ɔো ei s̪ɔbɔ rakʰa
n̪ibed̪n̪er at͡ɕar d͡zen̪ t̪ara mere ɸel̪et͡ɕʰe
ɕikar ebɔŋ er ɸɔl̪e on̪ek pap d̪ur he̯ɔ।
hd͡zɔ̃ ebɔŋ d͡zara omɔrɔ kʰabar kʰaoe̯ae̯
emɔn̪ɔ d͡zɔd͡ʑner bam brɔhmar kat͡ɕʰe
on̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ kin̪t̪u t̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ d͡ze kɔre
kɔোn̪ɔ t̪d͡zaɡ n̪ei t̪ar n̪ei oŋɕo n̪ei
emɔn̪ɔki bɔrt̪ɔman̪ biɕbeo। kib̤abe t̪in̪i ɕee̯ar kɔra ut͡ɕit̪
arekta he t̪umi t̪ɔোmar rekʰar mɔhima
brɔhmar d̪ɽiʂtit̪e ei s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ n̪ojbed̪d͡zɔ
t͡ɕʰɔɽie̯e at͡ɕʰe ebɔŋ ɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔra he̯ɔ bɔোd͡ʑ̤a
d͡ze s̪ɔbɔ ain̪ d̪bara eɡie̯e eta d͡ʑan̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
apn̪i s̪ɔn̪d̪ehɔ t̪d͡zaɡ kɔra hɔbe ut̪ɔs̪ɔrɡɔ
d͡ze d͡ʑnan̪ prɔd̪an̪ kɔre t̪a mɔhan̪ upɔharer t͡ɕee̯e ut̪t̪ɔmɔ
s̪ɔmpɔd̪er d̪bara d̪eoe̯a upɔharer mul̪d͡zɔhe amar rad͡ʑkumar
mɔn̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze mit̪ʰd͡za d͡za d̪ee̯ it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa d͡ze kad͡ʑ kɔre
ebɔŋ eɡul̪i ɕrɔd̪d̪̤ar d̪bara d̪ɽiɽ̤ on̪us̪ɔn̪d̪̤an̪er d̪bara ord͡ʑit̪ he̯ɔ
d͡zara s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ d̪ekʰe t̪ad̪er prɔt̪i bin̪it̪ mɔn̪ɔোd͡zɔোɡer d̪bara
ebɔŋ eta ɕekʰan̪ s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ d͡ʑen̪e t̪ɔোmar hɽid̪e̯ɔ ar n̪ei
b̤ul̪er s̪at̪ʰe kɔʂtɔ pabe karɔnɔ s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ d̪ekʰabe
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪ t̪ɔোmar bɔɕib̤ut̪ d͡zemɔn̪ɔ t̪umi amar kat͡ɕʰe।
t̪at͡ɕʰaɽa pandur put̪rɔ t̪umi ki s̪ɔbɔt͡ɕee̯e kʰarap t͡ɕʰil̪e
s̪ɔkɔl̪ɔ on̪d͡zae̯er s̪ɔt̪d͡zer ei n̪d͡zad͡zd͡zɔ d͡ʑahad͡ʑ
s̪ɔmud̪rer opare t̪ɔোmake n̪irapɔd̪ɔ ebɔŋ ɕukɔn̪ɔো bɔhɔn̪ɔ kɔra ut͡ɕit̪
t̪ɔোmar s̪imal̪ɔŋ̤ɡ̤ɔn̪ɔ prɔd͡ʑbɔl̪it̪ ɕikʰa his̪abe
t͡ɕʰaie̯e dube d͡zaoe̯a pɔrd͡zɔn̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑbal̪an̪i kʰae̯
t̪ai t͡ɕʰai ord͡ʑun̪ kit͡ɕʰui n̪a
d͡ʑnan̪er ɕikʰa bɔrd͡ʑd͡zɔ kɔrmer me̯ɔl̪a d̪ur kɔre
er mɔt̪ɔ kɔোn̪ɔ pɔriɕোd̪̤ɔkɔ n̪ei
ei s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ pɽit̪ʰibit̪e ebɔŋ d͡ze eti kʰũd͡ʒət͡ʃʰe
eti kʰũd͡ʒe pabe n̪ikʰũtə beɽe utʰt͡ɕʰe n̪id͡ʑer mɔd̪̤d͡ze।
biɕbas̪ kɔre at̪ma pel̪ei s̪e pae̯
n̪id͡ʑeke ae̯ɔt̪t̪ɔ kɔre ebɔŋ s̪ɔt̪d͡zer s̪at̪ʰe l̪eɡe t̪ʰake ebɔŋ as̪e
d͡ʑnan̪er od̪̤ikari ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔ ɕan̪t̪ir d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
pɔrɔmɔ biɕram kin̪t̪u d͡zara oɕikʂit̪
ebɔŋ d͡zara purnɔ iman̪ɔhin̪ ebɔŋ d͡zara b̤e̯ɔ kɔre
ɕen̪tɔ he̯ɔ ekʰan̪e ba on̪d͡zɔ kɔোt̪ʰao ɕan̪t̪i n̪ei
d͡ze s̪ɔn̪d̪ehɔ kɔre t̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kɔোn̪ɔ aɕa n̪ei s̪ukʰo n̪ei।
d͡ze s̪be̯ɔŋs̪ɔmpurnɔ he̯e s̪ɔn̪d̪ehɔke pɔrad͡ʑit̪ kɔret͡ɕʰe
s̪eba t̪ʰeke n̪id͡ʑeke kɔrmɔ t̪ʰeke at̪make bit͡ɕt͡ɕʰin̪n̪ɔ kɔra
al̪োkit̪ ebɔŋ mukt̪i amar d͡zubrad͡ʑ
kad͡ʑ t̪ake ar bẽd̤e rakʰe n̪a kata t̪arɔpɔrɔ 
bud̪d̪̤ir t̪ɔrɔbari n̪ie̯e b̤ɔrɔt̪ɔput̪rɔ
ei s̪ɔn̪d̪ehɔ d͡ze t̪ɔোmar hɽid̪ɔs̪pɔn̪d̪ɔn̪ɔke bẽd̤e rakʰe bɔn̪d̪̤ɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕʰin̪n̪ɔ
t̪ɔোmar od͡ʑnɔt̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ s̪ahɔs̪i ebɔŋ d͡ʑnan̪i hɔt̪e
amar s̪at̪ʰe matʰe n̪ao utʰi
ekʰan̪e t͡ɕɔt̪urt̪ʰɔ od̪̤d͡zae̯ ɕeʂ kɔrun̪। b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar
ɕirোn̪am d͡ʑnan̪ d͡zɔোɡɔ

od̪̤d͡zae̯ 
ord͡ʑun̪।
t̪ɔbu kɽiʂnɔ ek s̪ɔme̯ɔ t̪umi prɔɕɔŋs̪a kɔrɔbe
kad͡ʑer s̪arɔs̪ɔ ebɔŋ on̪d͡zɔ s̪ɔme̯e
kad͡ʑer mad̪̤d͡zɔme s̪eba। er mɔd̪̤d͡ze d̪ud͡ʑɔn̪ɔ s̪pɔʂtɔb̤abe bɔl̪un̪
kɔোn̪ɔti b̤al̪ upae̯
kɽiʂnɔ।
kad͡ʑ t̪ʰeke birɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰaka
b̤al̪ ebɔŋ pɔbit̪rɔt̪a kad͡ʑ kɔrɔt̪e
b̤al̪ো ebɔŋ ub̤e̯ɔ at͡ɕar pɔrɔmɔ s̪ukʰ
kin̪t̪u ei d̪ud͡ʑn̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze ut̪t̪ɔmɔ pɔt̪ʰɔ t̪ar
d͡zara d̪̤armikb̤abe kad͡ʑ kɔre n̪a।
t̪in̪ii prɔkɽit̪ t̪d͡zaɡkari d̪ɽiɽ̤ o s̪t̪ʰir
kekit͡ɕʰu t͡ɕaoe̯a kit͡ɕʰui prɔt̪d͡zakʰd͡zan̪ɔprɔman t̪ʰake
birud̪d̪̤ɔ he bir d͡zubrad͡ʑ
kɔrar s̪ɔme̯ɔ ei d̪̤ɔrɔn̪er s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ kad͡ʑ t̪ʰeke hal̪kab̤abe birt̪i
ei n̪ɔt̪un̪ pɔndit̪ kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰen̪ t̪ara d̪ud͡ʑɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕʰil̪en̪
ei s̪aŋkʰd͡zɔ ebɔŋ ei d͡zɔোɡɔ d͡ʑnan̪ira d͡ʑan̪en̪
ke s̪bami ek t͡ɕʰĩɽe s̪ɔোn̪ar ɸɔl̪ɔ d̪ud͡ʑn̪er
ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔ biɕramer ont͡ɕɔl̪ɔ d͡zekʰan̪e s̪aŋkʰd͡zɔra pɔৌ̃t͡ʃʰaj
d͡zɔোɡira ord͡ʑɔn̪ɔ kɔre। ke ei d̪uid͡ʑɔn̪ɔke ek his̪abe d̪ekʰe
pɔriʂkar t͡ɕɔোkʰe d̪ekʰe t̪ɔbuo emɔn̪ɔ bimurt̪ɔt̪a prɔd̪̤an̪
on̪ek pɔbit̪rɔt̪a t͡ɕʰaɽa d͡ʑe̯ɔ kɔra kɔtʰin̪।
d͡zin̪i pɔbit̪rɔt̪ae̯ s̪t̪ʰir s̪bɔɕas̪it̪
ɕud̪d̪̤ɔ t͡ɕit̪t̪ɔ in̪d̪rie̯ o at̪mar prɔb̤u
harie̯e d͡zai s̪ɔkɔl̪er s̪ad̪̤arɔnɔ d͡ʑibn̪e
ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ d͡zɔোɡɔd͡zukt̪ɔt̪in̪i ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ s̪ad̪̤u d͡zin̪i oe̯en̪dɔ kɔren̪
s̪ɔোd͡ʑa brɔhmer kat͡ɕʰe। emɔn̪ɔ ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔke s̪pɔrɕɔ kɔra he̯ɔ n̪a
kad͡ʑer kɔl̪ɔŋkɔ d̪bara। ami n̪id͡ʑer kit͡ɕʰui kɔri n̪a
eb̤abe s̪e b̤abbe d͡ze s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔke d̪̤arɔnɔ kɔre
d̪ekʰar ɕrɔbɔne s̪pɔrɕe ɡɔn̪d̪̤e kɔkʰɔn̪ɔ
s̪e kʰae̯ ba d͡zae̯ ba ɕbas̪ n̪ee̯ ̤ɡ̤um ba kɔt̪ʰabart̪a
d̪rut̪ d̪̤ɔre rakʰe ba al̪ɡa kɔre t͡ɕɔোkʰɔ kʰul̪e d̪ee̯ ba bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre d̪ee̯
s̪ɔrbɔd̪a aɕbɔs̪t̪ɔ eti in̪d̪rie̯ɔd͡ʑɔɡɔt̪er n̪atɔkɔ
in̪d̪rie̯ d̪ie̯e। d͡ze brɔhmer t͡ɕin̪t̪ae̯ kad͡ʑ kɔre

eti on̪d͡zɔ kɔোn̪ɔ d̪̤ɔn̪ɔ t̪ul̪n̪ie̯ bɔl̪e mɔn̪e kɔre n̪a
kin̪t̪u s̪ekʰan̪e aɕre̯ɔ d̪eoe̯a al̪োɽɔn̪ɔ ba d͡ʑ̤ɔ̃kun̪i d̪eoe̯a d͡zabe n̪a
d͡ze kɔোn̪ɔ t͡ɕɔrɔmɔ d̪uঃkʰer d̪bara s̪ei raʂtrɔtike ɕan̪t̪i bɔl̪un̪।
d͡ze s̪ukʰi bit͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ d͡zɔোɡɔ s̪ei l̪ɔোkɔtike dakো
n̪ikʰũtə d͡zɔোɡin̪
otɔl̪ɔ it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa
pɔriɕrɔmɔ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe d͡zɔt̪ɔkʂɔnɔ n̪a prɔt͡ɕeʂta s̪bat͡ɕt͡ɕʰɔn̪d̪d͡ze ɕeʂ n̪a he̯ɔ
ar t͡ɕin̪t̪a b̤abn̪a t̪ʰeke t͡ɕɔl̪e ɡet͡ɕʰe। d͡ʑ̤eɽe
kʰd͡zat̪i ebɔŋ l̪ab̤er s̪bɔpn̪ɔ d̪bara d͡ʑɔn̪man̪ো s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ akaŋkʂa
in̪d̪rie̯er d̪ɔrɔd͡ʑa bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ
s̪ɔt̪ɔrkɔ oe̯ardɔ s̪ɔhɔ t̪ai d̪̤ape d̪̤ape eti as̪e
n̪iɕt͡ɕit̪ ɕan̪t̪i ebɔŋ hɽid̪e̯ɔ prɔɕan̪t̪ir upɔhar d̪it̪e
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ mɔn̪ɔ bas̪ kɔre at̪mɔmɔোɽan̪ো ebɔŋ at̪ma ud̪bel̪it̪ he̯ɔ
kɔʂtɔhin̪। kin̪t̪u d͡zɔt̪ɔbar hɽid̪e̯ɔ
birt̪i bɔn̪d͡zɔ ebɔŋ d̪ɔোd̪ul̪d͡zɔman̪ n̪ie̯ɔn̪t̪rɔnɔ t̪ʰeke t̪ai prae̯i
t̪ake etike pun̪rud̪d̪̤ar kɔrɔt̪e d̪in̪ t̪ake etike pun̪rae̯ l̪aɡam d̪in̪
at̪mar ɕas̪n̪er kat͡ɕʰe n̪ikʰũtə s̪ukʰer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
prɔɕan̪t̪it̪e kebɔl̪ɔ buke beɽe otʰe
abeɡɔhin̪ at̪ma oprad̪̤ t̪ʰeke ɕud̪d̪̤ɔ
os̪imer kat͡ɕʰe prɔt̪id͡ʑna kɔret͡ɕʰen̪। d͡ze eib̤abe man̪ɔt̪ɔ kɔre
pɔrɔmat̪mar kat͡ɕʰe t̪ar at̪ma pap t̪d͡zaɡ
on̪t̪ɔhin̪ an̪ɔn̪d̪e bin̪a bad̪̤ae̯ t͡ɕɔl̪e d͡zae̯
brɔhmar s̪at̪ʰe ojkd͡zer। s̪e t̪ai ɕɔpɔt̪ʰɔ kɔret͡ɕʰil̪
t̪ai miɕrit̪ d̪ekʰe d͡ʑibn̪at̪mar bas̪in̪d̪a
d͡ʑibit̪ s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪ ebɔŋ s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪
s̪ei d͡ʑibn̪at̪ma n̪ihit̪। ebɔŋ d͡zara eib̤abe
amake s̪ɔkɔl̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze ebɔŋ s̪ɔkɔl̪ɔke amar mɔd̪̤d͡ze upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤i kɔre
ami t̪ake kɔkʰɔn̪ɔো d͡zet̪e d̪iin̪i ba t̪ake ɕit̪ʰil̪ kɔre n̪a
amake d̪̤ɔre rakʰো kin̪t̪u s̪e d͡zekʰan̪e pare s̪ekʰan̪e bas̪ kɔrɔ
t̪ar d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ d͡zai hɔোkɔ s̪e amar mɔd̪̤d͡zei bas̪ kɔre
karɔnɔ t̪in̪i amake d͡ʑan̪en̪ ebɔŋ upas̪n̪a kɔren̪ d͡zin̪i bas̪ kɔren̪
s̪ɔbɔ kit͡ɕʰur mɔd̪̤d͡ze d͡za bẽt͡ʃe at͡ɕʰe ebɔŋ s̪ɔbɔ kit͡ɕʰut̪ei amar s̪at̪ʰe l̪eɡe at͡ɕʰe।
ord͡ʑun̪ d͡zɔd̪i ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ man̪uʂ s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑae̯ɡae̯ d̪ekʰe
t̪ar n̪id͡ʑer upma d̪bara ɕekʰan̪ো ekti d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ

ord͡ʑun̪।
mɔd̪̤ur hɔt̪d͡zakari abaro ei d͡zɔোɡɔ
ei ɕan̪t̪i s̪ɔmɔt̪a t̪ʰeke ud̪b̤ut̪
apn̪ar d̪bara pɔrit͡ɕit̪ ami kɔোn̪ɔ s̪t̪ʰirt̪a d̪ekʰt̪e n̪a
s̪ekʰan̪e kɔোn̪ɔ biɕram karɔnɔ puruʂd̪er hɽid̪e̯ɔ
on̪ird̪iʂtɔ kɽiʂnɔ ɸus̪kuɽi ɡɔোl̪ɔmal̪
it͡ɕt͡ɕʰakɽit̪ ebɔŋ ɕɔkt̪iɕal̪i। eta s̪ɔbɔ ek t͡ɕʰil̪ ami mɔn̪e kɔri
bipɔt̪ʰɔɡami bat̪as̪ d̪̤ɔre rakʰa man̪uʂer hɽid̪e̯er mɔt̪ɔো।
kɽiʂnɔ।
d̪ir̤ɡ̤ɔ s̪ɔɕɔs̪t̪rɔ bir os̪bikarer baire kɔtʰin̪
man̪uʂer hɽid̪e̯ɔ s̪ɔŋd͡zɔt̪ɔ kɔra ebɔŋ d̪ɔোd̪ul̪d͡zɔman̪
t̪ɔbuo ob̤d͡zas̪e s̪ɔŋd͡zɔt̪ɔ beɽe utʰuk rad͡ʑkumar
s̪bad̪eɕer ob̤d͡zas̪ d̪bara। ei d͡zɔোɡɔ ami bɔl̪i
on̪ie̯ɔn̪t̪rit̪d̪er kat͡ɕʰe hal̪kab̤abe as̪e n̪a
kin̪t̪u d͡ze n̪id͡ʑei hɔbe os̪t̪ad̪
eta d͡ʑit̪t̪e hɔbe d͡zɔd̪i s̪e d̪ɽiɽ̤b̤abe s̪ekʰan̪e s̪ɔŋɡɔram kɔre।
ord͡ʑun̪।
ar kɔোn̪ɔ pɔt̪ʰe d͡zabe s̪e d͡zar biɕbas̪ at͡ɕʰe
bd͡zɔrt̪ʰɔ kɽiʂnɔ pit͡ɕʰat͡ɕt͡ɕʰe
pɔbit̪rɔt̪a t̪ʰeke n̪ikʰũtə n̪ie̯ɔmɔ on̪upɔs̪t̪ʰit̪
s̪e ki harie̯e d͡zae̯ n̪a brɔhmar al̪ো t̪ʰeke bipɔt̪ʰɔɡami
n̪irɔrt̪ʰɔkɔ me̤ɡ̤er mɔt̪ɔো d͡za b̤es̪e beɽae̯ pɽit̪ʰibi o s̪bɔrɡɔ
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ bɔd͡ʑrɔpat̪ t̪a bid̪irnɔ kɔre ebɔŋ t̪a od̪ɽiɕd͡zɔ he̯e d͡zae̯
ami ki ɕun̪t̪e pabো t̪umi amake ekʰan̪e ut̪t̪ɔrɔ d̪ebe
d͡zehet̪u kɽiʂnɔ apn̪i t͡ɕʰaɽa keu s̪ɔn̪d̪ehɔ d̪ur kɔrɔt̪e paren̪
kɽiʂnɔ।
s̪e harie̯e d͡zae̯ n̪i he pɽit̪ʰar put̪rɔ n̪a
t̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ pɽit̪ʰibi ba s̪bɔrɡo harae̯ n̪a
karɔnɔ kɔোn̪ɔ hɽid̪e̯ɔ d͡ze ekti s̪ɔtʰik it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa rakʰe
l̪ɔোkɔs̪an̪er pɔt̪ʰe hɔ̃tɔt͡ɕʰe d͡zar bd͡zɔrt̪ʰɔ hoe̯a ut͡ɕit̪
d̪̤armikt̪a kamn̪a kɔre mɽit̪d͡zu as̪e
n̪d͡zae̯er ont͡ɕɔl̪er d̪ike s̪ekʰan̪e bas̪ kɔre
pɔrimapɔhin̪ bɔt͡ɕʰɔrɔ ebɔŋ n̪ɔt̪un̪ kɔre d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ n̪eoe̯a
abar d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ ɕuru he̯ɔ kɔোn̪ɔো mel̪a baɽit̪e
mɽid̪u o kʰuɕir mad͡ʑ̤e। eta s̪ud͡zোɡɔ hɔt̪e pare
t̪in̪i d͡zɔোɡin̪ ɡɽihe obɔt̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔren̪
pund͡zer s̪t̪ɔn̪e kin̪t̪u eta birɔl̪ɔ emɔn̪ɔ d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ
ei pɽit̪ʰibit̪e paoe̯a kɔtʰin̪ prɔd̪̤an̪
t̪ai t̪in̪i abar hɽid̪e̯er ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪a ki ɸire at͡ɕʰe
t̪in̪i ord͡ʑɔn̪ɔ kɔret͡ɕʰen̪ ebɔŋ t̪ai t̪in̪i n̪ɔt̪un̪ kɔre t͡ɕeʂta kɔret͡ɕʰen̪
n̪ikʰũtətar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ aro b̤al̪ aɕa s̪ɔhɔ prie̯ d͡zubrad͡ʑ
karɔnɔ puran̪ো it͡ɕt͡ɕʰar d̪bara s̪e akɽiʂtɔ he̯ɔ

d͡zɔোɡer biɕud̪d̪̤ɔt̪a pas̪ kɔra
ɕɔbd̪ɔbrɔhmer baire kɔt̪ʰd͡zɔ bed̪।
kin̪t̪u d͡zɔোɡi he̯e ɕɔkt̪iɕal̪i ebɔŋ d̪ir̤ɡ̤ɔ prɔt͡ɕeʂta
s̪imal̪ɔŋ̤ɡ̤ɔn̪ɔ t̪ʰeke ɕud̪d̪̤ɔ d͡ʑɔn̪mer d̪bara s̪id̪d̪̤ɔ
d͡ʑɔn̪mer pɔrɔ s̪e ɕeʂ pɔrd͡zɔn̪t̪ɔ pa rɔোpɔnɔ kɔre
d̪urer pɔt̪ʰe। d͡zemɔn̪ɔ ek pɔd̪ɔ
t̪ɔpɔs̪bid̪er upre d͡ʑnan̪id̪er t͡ɕee̯e ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪ɔrɔ
bis̪t̪ɔrɔ kɔrmer kɽit̪it̪ber baire t̪umi ho
d͡zɔোɡi ord͡ʑun̪ ebɔŋ ei d̪̤ɔrɔn̪er biɕbas̪
d͡zin̪i amar ibad̪ɔt̪ɔ kɔren̪ t̪in̪ii prɔkɽit̪ o ɕreʂtʰɔ

ɕirোn̪am at̪mɔs̪ɔŋd͡zɔmɔd͡zɔোɡɔ

kɽiʂnɔ।
ekʰɔn̪ɔ ɕikʰun̪ prie̯ d͡zubrad͡ʑ kib̤abe d͡zɔd̪i apn̪ar at̪ma s̪et kɔra he̯ɔ
kɔkʰɔn̪o amar upɔrɔ ekʰn̪o d͡zɔোɡɔ bd͡zae̯am

n̪ikʰũtəb̤abe amake d̪̤ɔre rakʰt̪e hɔbe।
ami t̪ɔোmake s̪ei t͡ɕɔrɔmɔ bid̪d͡za ̤ɡ̤ɔোʂɔna kɔrɔbɔ
s̪ɔmpurnɔ ebɔŋ biɕeʂ d͡za d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ apn̪i d͡ʑan̪en̪
ei pɽit̪ʰibit̪e ar kit͡ɕʰu d͡ʑan̪ar baki n̪ei।
had͡ʑar had͡ʑar man̪uʂer mɔd̪̤d͡ze ek s̪ɔmb̤abn̪a
s̪ɔt̪d͡zer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ s̪ɔŋɡɔram ebɔŋ d͡zara t͡ɕeʂta kɔre t̪ad̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze
n̪a ebɔŋ upre utʰun̪ekmat̪rekʰan̪e ebɔŋ s̪ekʰan̪e
amake d͡ʑan̪e ami d͡zemɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔt̪d͡zi।
pɽit̪ʰibi d͡ʑɔl̪ɔ ɕikʰa bae̯u it̪ʰar d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ mɔn̪ɔ
ebɔŋ bd͡zɔkt̪it̪bɔ d͡zara at
amar md͡zan̪iɸes̪tɔ d̪ekʰan̪ো ap kɔrun̪
eɡul̪ো amar n̪imn̪ɔ prɔkɽit̪ir hɔbe ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪ɔrɔ ɕikʰun̪
d͡zar d̪bara t̪umi bir ei mɔhabiɕbɔ
d͡ʑibn̪er n̪it̪i d̪bara ut̪pad̪it̪ he̯ɔ
d͡zar d̪bara d̪ɽiɕd͡zɔman̪ d͡ʑin̪is̪er d͡ʑɔɡɔt̪er d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ he̯ɔ
ekti t̪ʰeke his̪abe d͡ʑan̪i ami s̪ei ɡɔrb̤ɔ
ami ei mɔhabiɕbɔ t̪ojri kɔri ebɔŋ ami ei mɔhabiɕbɔke t̪ojri kɔri
ami t͡ɕʰaɽa ar keu n̪ei rad͡ʑkumar

t̪ar s̪triŋ upɔrɔ mukt̪ɔো ekti s̪ari d͡ʑ̤ul̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ his̪abe
ami d͡ʑɔl̪er t̪ad͡ʑa s̪bad̪ ami
t͡ɕɔ̃d̪er rupa s̪urd͡zer s̪ɔোn̪a
bed̪e pud͡ʑar kɔt̪ʰa rɔোmant͡ɕɔ
d͡za it̪ʰare ebɔŋ ɕɔkt̪it̪e t͡ɕɔl̪e d͡zae̯

obɔhit̪ er mɔhan̪er mɔhima।
d͡ʑɔ̃kɔd͡ʑɔmɔkɔ er d͡ʑɔ̃kɔd͡ʑɔmɔkɔ। kun̪t̪ir t͡ɕʰel̪e
ei ami abeɡ ebɔŋ it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa t̪ʰeke mukt̪ɔ
t̪ɔbuo ki ami s̪ɔtʰik kamn̪a kɔri d͡zara akaŋkʂa kɔre
b̤ɔrɔt̪ɔd̪er prɔd̪̤an̪ ei s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ med͡ʑad͡ʑer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
prɔɕan̪t̪ɔ ba abeɡɔprɔbɔnɔ ba od͡ʑnɔ
d͡za prɔkɽit̪i ɸrem amar t̪ʰeke on̪uman̪ kin̪t̪u s̪ɔbɔ
miɕe at͡ɕʰe amar mɔd̪̤d͡ze ami t̪ad̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze n̪ei biɕbɔ
s̪ɔt̪t̪ar oj t̪in̪ti ɡuner d̪bara prɔt̪arit̪
t̪ad̪er s̪ɔkɔl̪er baire ke at͡ɕʰe amake t͡ɕin̪e n̪a
t̪ad̪er s̪ɔbar upre t͡ɕirɔn̪t̪ɔn̪ɔ eta kɔtʰin̪
s̪ei ̤ɡ̤ɔোmɔta t͡ɕʰid̪rɔ kɔrɔt̪e bib̤in̪n̪ɔ on̪uʂtʰan̪er d̪ibd͡zi
d͡za amake l̪ukie̯e rakʰe t̪ɔbuo d͡zara amar upas̪n̪a kɔre
etike bid̪d̪̤ɔ kɔrun̪ ebɔŋ ot̪ikrɔmɔ kɔrun̪।
ami pɔrit͡ɕit̪ n̪a
d̪uʂtɔd̪er kat͡ɕʰe n̪a bɔোkad̪er kat͡ɕʰe
ba bes̪ ebɔŋ d͡zao n̪a t̪ad̪er kat͡ɕʰe
d͡ʑin̪is̪er prɔd̪ɔrɕɔn̪e d͡zar mɔn̪ɔ prɔt̪arit̪ he̯ɔ
n̪a d͡zara os̪urd̪er pɔt̪ʰɔ d̪̤ɔre।#
t͡ɕar prɔkarer man̪uʂ amake d͡ʑan̪e d͡ze kɔ̃d̪e
ord͡ʑun̪ ebɔŋ d͡ze bd͡zɔkt̪i d͡ʑan̪t̪e t͡ɕae̯
ebɔŋ d͡ze s̪ahad͡zd͡zɔ kɔrɔt̪e pɔriɕrɔmɔ kɔre ebɔŋ d͡ze bɔs̪e
amar kit͡ɕʰu al̪োkit̪
ei t͡ɕartir mɔd̪̤d͡ze

d͡ze ɕeʂ d̪̤ɔrmɔpran at̪ma d͡ʑnan̪i ob̤iprae̯

t̪ake ebɔŋ t̪in̪i amar kat͡ɕʰe s̪ɔbɔt͡ɕee̯e prie̯
t͡ɕartii b̤al̪ ebɔŋ amake kʰɔো̃d͡ʒe kin̪t̪u amar n̪id͡ʑer
hɽid̪e̯er s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ biɕbɔs̪t̪ɔ amar upɔrɔ s̪t̪ʰir
amake t̪ad̪er pɔrɔmɔ aɕirbad̪ his̪abe ɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔre
t̪ara amar n̪e̯ɔ amiemɔn̪ɔki ami n̪id͡ʑeo
bɔhu d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ ɕeʂe amar kat͡ɕʰe t̪ara as̪e
t̪ɔbuo d͡ʑnan̪i mɔhat̪ma kʰũd͡ʒe paoe̯a kɔtʰin̪
d͡ze bd͡zɔkt̪i bɔl̪e s̪ɔbi bas̪ud̪eb#
s̪ekʰan̪eo at͡ɕʰe d͡zad̪er d͡ʑnan̪ s̪ɔre ɡet͡ɕʰe
ei it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa ba d͡ze t̪ad̪er s̪eba d̪ee̯
kit͡ɕʰu n̪imn̪ɔ d̪ebt̪a bib̤in̪n̪ɔ at͡ɕar s̪ɔhɔ s̪imabɔd̪d̪̤ɔ
d͡za t̪ad̪er ɡɔtʰɔn̪ɔ kɔre। erɔkɔmɔ s̪ɔkɔl̪er kat͡ɕʰe
t̪ara kɔোn̪ɔ mɔn̪d̪ire pud͡ʑa kɔrɔbe ki akar d̪ebe biɕbas̪e
ami t̪ad̪er biɕbas̪ d̪ei ami s̪ɔn̪t̪uʂtɔ
eib̤abe hɽid̪e̯ɔ t̪ar iɕbɔrer kat͡ɕʰe on̪uɡɔrɔhɔ prart̪ʰɔn̪a kɔre
on̪d̪̤ɔkar kin̪t̪u prɔkʰɔrɔ t̪ar ɕeʂ akaŋkʂa at͡ɕʰe
kɔmɔ aɕirbad̪ kin̪t̪u eti ami d͡zara d̪it̪e
t̪ɔbuo ɕi̤ɡ̤ri ɕukie̯e d͡zae̯ t̪ara ki t͡ɕʰɔোtɔ ɸɔl̪ɔ kate
ol̪pɔ mɔn̪er man̪uʂ d͡zara emɔn̪ɔ pud͡ʑa kɔre
d͡zekʰan̪e t̪ara upas̪n̪a kɔre s̪ekʰan̪e d͡zan̪ t̪ad̪er d̪ebt̪ad̪er s̪at̪ʰe t͡ɕɔl̪e d͡zan̪।
kin̪t̪u amar amar kat͡ɕʰe as̪a t͡ɕɔোkʰɔ on̪d̪̤ɔ
d͡za oprɔkaɕit̪ prɔkaɕ bɔl̪e mɔn̪e kɔre
amar prɔkɽit̪ at̪mar mɔd̪̤d͡ze amake upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤i n̪a
obin̪ɔɕbɔrɔ d̪ɽiʂtihin̪ o̤ɡ̤ɔোʂit̪
amar on̪uʂtʰan̪er d͡ʑad̪ur pɔrd̪ar aɽal̪e l̪ukie̯e at͡ɕʰe
ami s̪ɔkɔl̪e d̪ekʰi n̪a ami d͡ʑan̪i n̪a
od͡ʑɔn̪mɔ ebɔŋ pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪ɔhin̪ n̪iʂkrie̯ d͡ʑɔɡɔt̪e।
kin̪t̪u ami ord͡ʑun̪ d͡za t͡ɕʰil̪ s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑan̪i
ebɔŋ d͡za at͡ɕʰe ebɔŋ d͡za kit͡ɕʰu hɔt̪e hɔbe
d͡zɔd̪io t̪ad̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze keu amake t͡ɕen̪e n̪a
biprit̪ d͡ʑɔোɽar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ abeɡ d̪bara
pɔt͡ɕʰɔn̪d̪ɔ ebɔŋ opɔt͡ɕʰɔn̪d̪er oj d̪ui ɸɔ̃d̪ɔ d̪bara d͡zubrad͡ʑ
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ prani bihbɔl̪ɔ he̯e bas̪ kɔre ke̯ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔke bɔ̃t͡ɕan̪
ke pap t̪d͡zaɡ kɔrme pɔbit̪rɔ obɔhit̪
biprit̪ t̪ʰeke mukt̪ɔ ebɔŋ biɕbas̪e s̪t̪ʰir
amar kat͡ɕʰe ãkəɽe d̪̤ɔrɔ।
d͡zara t͡ɕʰĩɽe d͡zae̯ d͡zara amake kʰɔো̃d͡ʒe
d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ t̪ʰeke aɕre̯ɔ ebɔŋ mɽit̪d͡zu d͡zara s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ
d͡zara amake brɔhmɔ d͡ʑan̪e amake d͡ʑan̪un̪ at̪mar at̪ma
od̪̤d͡zat̪man̪ kɔrmɔ amar kad͡ʑ d͡ʑan̪i
d͡ʑan̪ ami od̪̤ib̤ut̪a d͡ʑibn̪er prɔb̤u
ebɔŋ od̪̤id̪aib̤a s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d̪ebt̪ar prɔb̤u
ebɔŋ od̪̤ie̯ad͡ʑna bɔl̪id̪an̪er prɔb̤u
prem o biɕbas̪er hɽid̪e̯e amake b̤al̪b̤abe upas̪n̪a kɔrɔ
ebɔŋ mɽit̪d͡zur s̪ɔme̯ɔ amake kʰũd͡ʒe pet̪e ebɔŋ d̪̤ɔre rakʰun̪।
ekʰan̪e od̪̤d͡zae̯ s̪ɔpt̪ɔmɔ ɕeʂ kɔrun̪। b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar
ɕirোn̪am bid͡ʑnan̪ɔd͡zɔোɡɔ
ot̪ʰba bibet͡ɕn̪a d̪bara d̪̤ɔrmer bi।
oʂtɔmɔ od̪̤d͡zae̯
ord͡ʑun̪।
ke s̪ei brɔhma ki d͡ze at̪mar at̪ma
od̪̤d͡zat̪man̪ ki apn̪i s̪ɔrbɔোt̪t̪ɔmɔ
t̪ɔোmar kad͡ʑ kɔrmɔɸɔl̪ɔ eta ki amake bɔl̪un̪
t̪umi ad̪̤ib̤ut̪a n̪am rakʰো ki abar
 man̪e hd͡zɔ̃ ebɔŋ eta kib̤abe as̪e
t̪umi ki t̪ɔোmar d̪ehe od̪̤id͡ʑnan̪ hɔt̪e parbe
mɔd̪̤ur hɔt̪d͡zakari aro amake d͡ʑan̪at̪e
mɽit̪d͡zur s̪ɔme̯ɔ kɔt̪ɔ b̤al̪ো man̪uʂ t̪ɔোmake kʰũd͡ʒe pae̯
kɽiʂnɔ।
ami brɔhmɔ ek on̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ iɕbɔrɔ
ar od̪̤d͡zat̪man̪ amar s̪ɔt̪t̪ar n̪am
at̪mar at̪ma amar t̪ʰeke d͡za as̪e
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔke d͡ʑibit̪ kɔre kɔrmɔke bɔl̪a he̯ɔ
ebɔŋ bib̤ɔkt̪ɔ akare ud̪b̤as̪it̪
ami od̪̤ib̤ut̪a d͡ʑibn̪er prɔb̤u
ebɔŋ od̪̤id̪aib̤a s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d̪ebt̪ar prɔb̤u
karɔnɔ ami puruʂ d͡zin̪i d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ d̪en̪।
ebɔŋ od̪̤ie̯ad͡ʑna bɔl̪id̪an̪er prɔb̤u
amiei ɕɔrire t̪ɔোmar s̪at̪ʰe kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰi
ami apn̪i ekti murt̪ɔ s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ mad͡ʑarer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
amar kat͡ɕʰe ɕikʰa ebɔŋ mɽit̪d͡zur s̪ɔme̯ɔ
d͡ze amake eka d̪̤d͡zan̪ kɔret͡ɕʰe
t̪ar maŋs̪ɔ bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre amar kat͡ɕʰe as̪e
amar s̪ɔt̪t̪bar mɔd̪̤d͡ze prɔbeɕ kɔre t̪umi s̪ɔn̪d̪ehɔ kɔrɔো n̪a
kin̪t̪u t̪in̪i d͡zɔd̪i on̪d͡zɔb̤abe d̪̤d͡zan̪ kɔren̪
mɽit̪d͡zur s̪ɔme̯ɔ maŋs̪ɔ bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ kɔrar mɔd̪̤d͡ze
s̪e d͡za kʰũd͡ʒət͡ʃʰil t̪ar kat͡ɕʰe d͡zae̯ kun̪t̪ir t͡ɕʰel̪e
karɔnɔ at̪ma t̪ar mɔt̪ɔো kɔre t̪ojri।
t̪ahɔl̪e amake s̪ɔbɔs̪ɔme̯ɔ t̪ɔোmar hɽid̪e̯e rakʰো ebɔŋ d͡zud̪d̪̤ɔ
t̪umio d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ hɽid̪e̯ɔ o mɔn̪ɔ amar upɔrɔ s̪t̪ʰir he̯ɔ
n̪iɕt͡ɕe̯ɔ amar kat͡ɕʰe as̪be s̪ɔbai as̪e d͡zara ɸatɔl̪ɔ
d̪ɽiɽ̤ biɕbas̪er obit͡ɕɔl̪ɔ it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa n̪ie̯e
on̪d͡zɔ kɔোn̪ɔ iɕbɔrer mal̪ik n̪e̯ɔ s̪ɔbai amar kat͡ɕʰe as̪e
pɔrɔmɔ puruʂ pɔbit̪rɔt̪ɔmɔ
d͡ze amake t͡ɕin̪et͡ɕʰe ɽiʂi o ɡae̯ker prɔb̤u
prat͡ɕin̪kal̪er s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ t̪in̪ biɕber t̪ʰakar
s̪imahin̪ kin̪t̪u prɔt̪iti pɔrɔmanu an̪e̯ɔn̪ɔkarir kat͡ɕʰe
d͡zeti etike d̪rut̪ kɔre ami bɔl̪i
amar rupke d͡ʑen̪et͡ɕʰe d͡za mɔrɔnɔɕil̪ d͡ʑnan̪ke ot̪ikrɔmɔ kɔre
d̪ekʰet͡ɕʰi amar d̪ipt̪i d͡za kɔোn̪ɔো t͡ɕɔোkʰɔ d̪ekʰen̪i 
s̪urd͡zer d͡ʑbɔl̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ s̪ɔোn̪ar t͡ɕee̯eo beɕi ud͡ʑd͡ʑbɔl̪ɔ
on̪d̪̤ɔkar bit͡ɕt͡ɕʰurɔnɔ t̪ar kat͡ɕʰe he̯et͡ɕʰe
s̪ɔtʰik d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ ɕeʂ hɔt͡ɕt͡ɕʰe
mɔn̪er s̪at̪ʰe d̪rut̪ ebɔŋ biɕbɔs̪t̪ɔ t̪akoe̯a n̪ie̯e
ɕan̪t̪ɔ b̤rur n̪it͡ɕe s̪t̪ʰir n̪iঃɕbas̪ ãkət͡ʃʰi
s̪ukʰi ɕan̪t̪it̪e d͡ze biɕbɔs̪t̪ɔ ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ mara d͡zae̯
an̪ɔn̪d̪e ɕan̪t̪i puruʂer s̪bɔrɡe t͡ɕɔl̪e d͡zae̯।
d͡ze s̪t̪ʰan̪er n̪am t̪ara bed̪ patʰ kɔre
okʂɔram t͡ɕuɽan̪t̪ɔ d͡zekʰan̪e t͡ɕeʂta kɔret͡ɕʰen̪
s̪ad̪̤u ebɔŋ t̪ɔpɔs̪bi t̪ad̪er ras̪t̪a eki।
d͡ze pɔt̪ʰɔs̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ pɔt̪ʰɔs̪e d͡zae̯ d͡ze bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre
t̪ar s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ in̪d̪rie̯er d̪ɔrɔd͡ʑa bas̪n̪a t̪al̪a
t̪ar hɽid̪e̯e n̪irapɔd̪ɔ ɡurut̪bɔpurnɔ bae̯uke ken̪d̪rɔ kɔre
t̪ar bit͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ t͡ɕin̪t̪ar upɔrɔ otɔl̪ɔb̤abe s̪et
ebɔŋ om pɔbit̪rɔ ɕɔbd̪aŋɕɔ
brɔhmer prɔt̪ikmɽit̪d͡zu amake d̪̤d͡zan̪ kɔre।
d͡zar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ on̪d͡zɔ kɔোn̪ɔ iɕbɔrɔ s̪ɔmpɔrke t̪akan̪
kɔkʰɔn̪o amar kat͡ɕʰe s̪ɔhɔd͡ʑe ami l̪ab̤ kɔri
emɔn̪ɔ d͡zɔোɡir d̪bara ebɔŋ amake ord͡ʑɔn̪ɔ kɔra
t̪ara pɔɽe n̪a s̪ei mɔhat̪mara d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ t̪ʰeke ɸire
d͡ʑibn̪er kat͡ɕʰe d͡za bd͡zɔt̪ʰar d͡ʑae̯ɡa d͡za ɕeʂ he̯ɔ
t̪ɔbe pɔrɔmɔ aɕirbad̪er pɔt̪ʰɔ obɔl̪ɔmbɔn̪ɔ kɔrun̪।
d͡ʑɔɡɔt̪ɔ ord͡ʑun̪emɔn̪ɔki brɔhmar d͡ʑɔɡɔt̪ɔ
mɽit̪d͡zu t̪ʰeke d͡ʑibn̪er os̪t̪ʰirt̪ae̯ abar ɸire as̪a
kin̪t̪u ora he kun̪t̪ir put̪rɔ d͡ze amar kat͡ɕʰe pɔৌ̃t͡ʃʰaj
d͡ʑɔn̪mer s̪bad̪ ar n̪ei। apn̪i d͡zɔd̪i brɔhmar d̪ibɔs̪ɔ d͡ʑan̪en̪
d͡za s̪ɔhɔs̪rɔ d͡zuɡ d͡zɔd̪i apn̪i d͡ʑan̪en̪
had͡ʑar d͡zuɡ brɔhmar rat̪ t̪ojri kɔre
ot̪ɔঃpɔrɔ t̪ɔোmɔra d̪in̪ o rat̪ke d͡ʑan̪ d͡zemɔn̪ɔ t̪in̪i d͡ʑan̪en̪।
s̪ei s̪ubiɕal̪ b̤ɔোrɔ d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ b̤aŋbe t̪ɔkʰɔn̪ɔ od̪ɽiɕd͡zɔ
d̪ɽiɕd͡zɔman̪ mɔd̪̤d͡ze n̪ɔt̪un̪ kɔre an̪a he̯ɔ
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ s̪ei ɡɔb̤ir rat̪ri on̪d̪̤ɔkar he̯e d͡zae̯ t̪ɔkʰɔn̪ɔ d͡za he̯ɔ
abar ml̪an̪ he̯e d͡zae̯ t̪ɔ̃rɔ kat͡ɕʰe d͡zin̪i eti patʰie̯et͡ɕʰen̪
hd͡zɔ̃ d͡ʑibit̪ d͡ʑin̪is̪er ei biɕal̪ s̪ɔŋs̪t̪ʰa
abar ebɔŋ ekʰn̪o abar ut̪pad̪it̪ mee̯ad̪ ɕeʂ he̯ɔ
brɔhmar rat̪er bel̪ae̯ ebɔŋ brɔhmar b̤ɔোre
ut̪t̪ʰit̪ he̯ɔ t̪ar it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa t͡ɕʰaɽai n̪ɔbɔd͡ʑat̪ker d͡ʑibn̪e।
kin̪t̪u ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪ɔrɔ ɡɔb̤irɔt̪ɔrɔ on̪t̪ɔrɔt̪ɔmɔ men̪e t͡ɕɔl̪e
on̪d͡zɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ in̪d̪rie̯ d͡ʑibn̪er mɔt̪ɔ n̪e̯ɔ
eɽie̯e d͡zaoe̯a d̪ɽiʂti opribɔrt̪it̪। ei s̪ɔhd͡zɔ he̯ɔ
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ s̪ɽiʂtɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪ ɕeʂ he̯e d͡zae̯
ei s̪ei d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ d͡zar n̪am obd͡zɔkt̪ɔ
os̪im s̪ɔbai t͡ɕɔrɔmɔt̪ɔmɔ
s̪ekʰan̪e es̪e keu ɸire as̪e n̪a। oj d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ
amar ebɔŋ ami s̪ekʰan̪e ar rad͡ʑkumar biɕbas̪ d̪bara
d͡za ̤ɡ̤ure beɽae̯ n̪a as̪ar pɔt̪ʰɔ at͡ɕʰe
s̪ekʰan̪e ami puruʂ ami d͡ze t͡ɕʰɔɽie̯et͡ɕʰi
amar t͡ɕarpaɕe mɔhabiɕbɔ d͡zar mɔd̪̤d͡ze bas̪ kɔre
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪ t̪ai pɔৌ̃t͡ʃʰanো ebɔŋ d̪ekʰa d͡zet̪e pare
 eɸen̪#১৪
bed̪e krɔmɔbɔrd̪̤ɔman̪ pɔbit̪rɔ ɸɔl̪er t͡ɕee̯eo s̪ɔmɽid̪d̪̤ɔ
upɔharer t͡ɕee̯e bɔɽɔ prart̪ʰɔn̪a ba rɔোd͡ʑar t͡ɕee̯eo b̤al̪
emɔn̪ɔ bud̪d̪̤i d͡zɔোɡi eib̤abe d͡ʑen̪e
ɕeʂ pɔrd͡zɔn̪t̪ɔ pɔrɔmɔ n̪ikʰũtə ɕan̪t̪it̪e as̪e।
ekʰan̪e oʂtɔmɔ od̪̤d͡zae̯ ɕeʂ kɔrun̪। b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar
ɕirোn̪am okʂɔrɔpɔrɔbrɔhmɔd͡zɔোɡɔ
ot̪ʰba ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ iɕbɔrer prɔt̪i b̤ɔkt̪i d̪bara d̪̤ɔrmer bi।




od̪̤d͡zae̯ 
kɽiʂnɔ।
ekʰɔn̪ɔ ami t̪ɔোmar kat͡ɕʰe kʰul̪e d̪eb d͡zar hɽid̪e̯ɔ
prɔt̪d͡zakʰd͡zan̪ kɔre n̪a d͡ze ɕeʂ bid̪d͡za ɡɔb̤irɔt̪ɔmɔɡɔোpɔn̪ɔ
amar s̪bɔrɡɔ ebɔŋ pɽit̪ʰibir s̪ei d̪urɔt̪ɔmɔ ɡɔোpɔn̪ɔ
d͡za d͡ʑan̪a apn̪ake os̪us̪t̪ʰɔt̪a t̪ʰeke mukt̪ɔ kɔrɔbe
ekti rad͡ʑkie̯ bid̪d͡za ekti rad͡ʑkie̯ rɔhɔs̪d͡zɔ
hd͡zɔ̃ at̪mar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ d͡zemɔn̪ɔ al̪ো t̪a ɕud̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre
prɔt̪iti pap t̪ʰeke pɔbit̪rɔt̪ar al̪ো
s̪ɔbɔt͡ɕee̯e d͡ʑɔ̃kɔd͡ʑɔmɔkɔ t͡ɕɔkɔt͡ɕɔke s̪ɔŋɡe d̪ekʰt̪e s̪ɔrɔl̪ɔ
hẽte d͡zaoe̯a s̪ɔhɔd͡ʑɔ okʂe̯ɔ
d͡zara eti ɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔre n̪a t̪ara biɕbas̪e bd͡zɔrt̪ʰɔ he̯ɔ৷
bɽihɔt̪t̪ɔrɔ d͡ʑnan̪ke upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤i kɔrɔt̪e amar kat͡ɕʰe n̪a pɔৌ̃t͡ʃʰao
t̪ɔোmar ɕɔt̪rud̪er d̪̤bɔŋs̪ɔkari t̪ara n̪ɔt̪un̪ kɔre dube d͡zae̯
maŋs̪er rad͡ʑd͡ze d͡zekʰan̪e s̪ɔbɔkit͡ɕʰu bɔd̪ɔl̪e d͡zae̯
amar d̪bara d͡ʑin̪is̪er s̪ɔmɔɡɔrɔ biɕal̪ mɔhabiɕbɔ
t͡ɕʰɔɽie̯e at͡ɕʰe d̪eɕbid̪eɕeamar d̪bara obd͡zɔkt̪ɔ
amar mɔd̪̤d͡ze s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ os̪t̪it̪bɔ re̯et͡ɕʰe
ami t̪ad̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze n̪a
t̪ɔbuo t̪ara d̪̤arɔnɔ kɔren̪i
oj d̪ɽiɕd͡zɔman̪ d͡ʑin̪is̪ ɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔrun̪ ebɔŋ al̪iŋɡɔn̪ɔ kɔrar t͡ɕeʂta kɔrun̪
rad͡ʑkie̯ rɔhɔs̪d͡zɔ amar s̪ɔt̪t̪a
s̪ɔbɔ s̪ɽiʂti kɔra s̪ɔbɔ tikie̯e rakʰaekʰn̪o bas̪ kɔre
s̪ɔbar baire
d̪ekʰa t̪irbihin̪ bat̪as̪er mɔt̪ɔো
pɔrimapɔhin̪ s̪t̪ʰan̪e s̪ɔran̪ kin̪t̪u s̪t̪ʰan̪ n̪e̯ɔ
ebɔŋ s̪t̪ʰan̪ t͡ɕɔl̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ bae̯u t͡ɕʰaɽa s̪t̪ʰan̪ t͡ɕʰil̪
t̪ai s̪ɔbɔ kit͡ɕʰui amar mɔd̪̤d͡ze at͡ɕʰe kin̪t̪u ami n̪i।
prɔt̪iti kɔl̪per s̪ɔmapn̪it̪e b̤art̪ie̯ d͡zubrad͡ʑ
amar s̪ɔt̪t̪ae̯ ɸire as̪a s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪ as̪e
prɔt̪iti kɔl̪per ɕurut̪e s̪ɔbɔ
amar t̪ʰeke n̪ɔbɔd͡ʑat̪ɔkɔ is̪d͡zu
ɕɔkt̪i d̪bara
ebɔŋ prɔkɽit̪ir s̪ahad͡zd͡zɔ amar bahd͡zik at̪ma
abar ebɔŋ ekʰn̪o abar ami eɡie̯e d͡zet̪e
d̪ɽiɕd͡zɔman̪ d͡ʑin̪is̪er rad͡ʑd͡zɔt̪ad̪er it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa t͡ɕʰaɽa
era s̪ɔbai prɔkɽit̪ir ɕɔkt̪it̪e।
t̪ɔbuo ei mɔhan̪ s̪ɽiʂti d͡zubrad͡ʑ amake d͡ʑɔɽaben̪ n̪a
amake mɔোhit̪ n̪a ami t̪ad̪er t̪ʰeke al̪ad̪a bɔs̪e t̪ʰaki
on̪d͡zan̪d͡zɔ ebɔŋ ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪ɔrɔ ebɔŋ bin̪amul̪d͡ze on̪d͡zɔt̪ʰae̯ s̪ɔŋd͡zukt̪ɔ
eib̤abe biɕber d͡ʑin̪is̪ɔpɔt̪rɔ amar d̪bara d̤al̪ai
t͡ɕɔl̪ɔman̪ ba s̪t̪ʰir d͡za kit͡ɕʰu at͡ɕʰe t̪a n̪ie̯e as̪un̪
d͡ʑibit̪ n̪aki pranɔhin̪ eb̤abei pɽit̪ʰibi t͡ɕɔl̪ɔt̪e t̪ʰake
mɔn̪er oɕikʂit̪ b̤ul̪ amake rupe abɽit̪
kit͡ɕʰui t̪ara amar ɡɔোpɔn̪ɔ upɔs̪t̪ʰit̪i d̪ekʰt̪e kit͡ɕʰui n̪a
amar l̪ukan̪ো prɔkɽit̪ir d͡za d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔke ɕas̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔre।
bɽit̪ʰa aɕa s̪ad̪̤n̪a bɽit̪ʰa kɔrmɔ kɔra kʰaoe̯an̪ো
n̪irɔrt̪ʰɔkɔ d͡ʑnan̪er upɔrɔ t̪ara n̪irbɔোd̪̤ɔb̤abe on̪us̪ɔn̪d̪̤an̪ kɔre
ekti mɔn̪d̪ɔ pɔt̪ʰɔ paɕbik ebɔŋ ɕe̯ɔt̪an̪er pɔt̪ʰɔ।
kin̪t̪u amar mɔhat̪mara d͡zara mɔhɔt̪ɔ at̪mar
d͡zara s̪bɔrɡie̯ pɔt̪ʰe t͡ɕɔl̪e amar pud͡ʑa kɔrɔ
ob̤ran̪t̪ɔ hɽid̪e̯e amake ut̪ɔs̪ɔ d͡ʑen̪e
d͡ʑibn̪er t͡ɕirɔn̪t̪ɔn̪ɔ ut̪ɔs̪ɔ। obiram
t̪ara amar mɔhiman̪bit̪ amake s̪ɔn̪d̪̤an̪ kɔrun̪ t̪ad̪er prɔt̪id͡ʑna rakʰa
ɕrɔd̪d̪̤a ebɔŋ b̤al̪bas̪ar pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪ɔhin̪ biɕbas̪er s̪at̪ʰe
amake ad̪ɔrɔ kɔrɔt͡ɕʰe। hd͡zɔ̃ ebɔŋ d͡zara kʰub pɔt͡ɕʰɔn̪d̪ɔ kɔre
ke d͡ʑaɡɔrɔt̪ɔ hɽid̪e̯er bɔl̪id̪an̪
ekti bis̪t̪ɽit̪ at̪mar t͡ɕap on̪ub̤ɔbɔ kɔrun̪
bɔhuɡun hɔl̪eo s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑae̯ɡae̯ ek ɕɔkt̪i
ami t̪d͡zaɡi ami prart̪ʰɔn̪akari
ami mɽit̪d̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ɸiun̪arel̪kek s̪et
ami n̪irame̯ɔ owʂd̪̤i ami ̤ɡ̤i
mɔn̪t̪rɔ ebɔŋ ɕikʰa ebɔŋ d͡za d͡ʑbɔl̪e
amiei s̪imahin̪ mɔhabiɕber
pit̪a mat̪a purbɔpuruʂ ebɔŋ prɔhɔri
ɕekʰar ɕeʂ d͡za ɕud̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre
b̤as̪man̪ d͡ʑɔl̪e ami om ami
ɽiɡbed̪ s̪ambed̪ d͡zɔd͡ʑurbed̪
pɔt̪ʰɔ pal̪ɔn̪ɔkɔrt̪a prɔb̤u bit͡ɕarɔkɔ
s̪akʂi bas̪ɔs̪t̪ʰan̪ aɕre̯ɔɡɽihɔ
bɔn̪d̪̤u d͡ʑ̤ɔrna ebɔŋ d͡ʑibn̪er s̪aɡɔrɔ
d͡za patʰae̯ ebɔŋ ɡil̪e kʰae̯ biɕber d̪̤ɔn̪ɔ
ar tred͡ʑart͡ɕembar bid͡ʑ ebɔŋ bid͡ʑ bɔpɔn̪ɔkari
kɔোt̪ʰa t̪ʰeke on̪t̪ɔhin̪ ɸɔs̪ɔl̪ɔ bɔs̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ s̪urd͡zer t̪ap amar
s̪bɔrɡer bɽiʂti amar d̪eoe̯a ba atkan̪ো
mɽit̪d͡zu ami ar omɔrɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ ami
ord͡ʑun̪ ebɔŋ d̪ɽiɕd͡zɔman̪ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ
ebɔŋ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ od̪ɽiɕd͡zɔ
hd͡zɔ̃ d͡zara ɕekʰe
t̪ribid̪̤ bed̪ d͡zara s̪ɔোmɔmɔd̪ɔ pan̪ kɔren̪
pap mɔোt͡ɕɔn̪ɔ kɔrun̪ bɔl̪id̪an̪ kɔrun̪ amar kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke t̪ara upard͡ʑɔn̪ɔ kɔre
s̪bɔrɡe d͡zat̪ae̯at̪ d͡zekʰan̪e maŋs̪ɔ ojɕbɔrik
mɔhan̪ d̪ebt̪a ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔ in̪d̪rer s̪bɔrɡe t̪ad̪er kʰaoe̯an̪।
t̪ɔbu t̪ara d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ s̪ei os̪ad̪̤arɔn̪ɔ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ aro beɽe d͡zae̯
d͡ʑan̪n̪at̪ bd͡ze̯ɔ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe ebɔŋ d͡zɔোɡɔd͡zɔt̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ mɔd͡ʑuri d̪eoe̯a he̯et͡ɕʰe
mɽit̪d͡zur d͡ʑɔɡɔt̪e es̪e aro ekbar bɔd̪ɔl̪e d͡zao।
t̪ad̪er prɔt̪id̪an̪ t͡ɕʰil̪ t̪ara t̪ad̪er d̪̤ɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔnt͡ɕe̯ɔ kɔret͡ɕʰe
t̪ribid̪̤ ɕas̪t̪rɔ ebɔŋ t̪ar rit on̪us̪ɔrɔnɔ
d͡ze ei d̪̤ɔrɔn̪er s̪ɔn̪d̪̤an̪ kɔre kʂɔnɔs̪t̪ʰae̯i an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ l̪ab̤ kɔre
an̪ɔn̪d̪er d͡za as̪e ebɔŋ d͡zae̯ ami t̪ad̪er eta mɔnd͡ʑur
kin̪t̪u d͡zara amar upas̪n̪a kɔre t̪ad̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
on̪d͡zɔ d̪ike ̤ɡ̤uri n̪a d̪rut̪ mɔn̪ɔ n̪ie̯e
ami pɔrɔl̪ɔোkɔ purnɔ s̪ukʰer n̪iɕt͡ɕe̯ɔt̪a an̪t̪e
n̪a ebɔŋ hɽid̪e̯ɔ d͡zara on̪d͡zan̪d͡zɔ upas̪d͡zɔ on̪us̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔre
s̪ɔrɔl̪ɔ biɕbas̪e t̪ad̪er prart̪ʰɔn̪a amar kat͡ɕʰe d͡ʑaɡe
he kun̪t̪ir put̪rɔ d͡zɔd̪io t̪ara on̪d͡zae̯b̤abe prart̪ʰɔn̪a kɔre
karɔnɔ amii ɡɔrɔhit̪a o prɔb̤u
prɔt̪iti kɔোrɔban̪i d͡za t̪ara d͡ʑan̪e n̪a
d͡zɔt̪ʰart̪ʰɔb̤abe t̪ai t̪ara abar pɽit̪ʰibit̪e pɔɽe
d͡zara d̪ebt̪ad̪er on̪us̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔre t̪ad̪er d̪ebt̪ar kat͡ɕʰe d͡zae̯ d͡zara brɔt̪ɔ
pitris̪er kat͡ɕʰe t̪ad̪er at̪ma pitris̪e d͡zae̯ mɔn̪ɔ
d̪uʂtɔ b̤utd̪er kat͡ɕʰe b̤utd̪er dube d͡zaoe̯a
ebɔŋ d͡ze amake b̤al̪bas̪e s̪e amar kat͡ɕʰe as̪e।
d͡ze amake biɕbas̪ o b̤al̪োbas̪ae̯ orpɔnɔ kɔrɔbe
ekti pat̪a ekti ɸul̪ ekti ɸɔl̪ɔ d͡ʑɔl̪ɔ d̤el̪e
s̪ei prɔs̪t̪ab ami ɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔri b̤al̪োbes̪e t̪ojri
d̪̤armik it͡ɕt͡ɕʰar s̪at̪ʰe। t̪umi ki kɔrɔ rad͡ʑkumar
kʰaoe̯a ba bɔl̪id̪an̪ upɔhar d̪eoe̯a
n̪amad͡ʑ ba rɔোd͡ʑa s̪ɔbi hɔোkɔ
amar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ amar his̪abe t̪ai t̪umi n̪id͡ʑeke mukt̪ɔ kɔrɔbe
kɔrmɔbɔn̪d̪̤ɔ t̪ʰeke ɕɽiŋkʰɔl̪ɔ d͡za puruʂke d̪̤ɔre rakʰe
b̤al̪োmɔn̪d̪ɔ is̪d͡zut̪e t̪ai as̪t̪e hɔbe
amar kat͡ɕʰe n̪irapɔd̪ɔd͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ t̪umi d̪ehɔt̪d͡zaɡ kɔrɔbe
biɕbas̪ ebɔŋ t̪d͡zaɡ amar s̪at̪ʰe d͡zɔোɡɔd̪an̪ kɔre
ami s̪ɔbar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ s̪ɔman̪ d͡ʑan̪i ̤ɡ̤ɽina n̪e̯ɔ
ami on̪uɡɔrɔhɔ d͡ʑan̪i n̪a d͡za t̪ojri he̯ɔ t̪a amar
kin̪t̪u d͡zara premer s̪at̪ʰe amar upas̪n̪a kɔre ami t̪ad̪er b̤al̪bas̪i
t̪ara amar mɔd̪̤d͡ze ebɔŋ ami t̪ad̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze
n̪a rad͡ʑkumar
d̪uʂtɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ d͡zɔd̪i t̪ar t͡ɕin̪t̪ae̯ ̤ɡ̤urie̯e d̪ee̯
s̪ɔোd͡ʑa amar kat͡ɕʰe t̪ake b̤al̪োrɔ mɔd̪̤d͡ze ɡɔnɔn̪a kɔrɔ
t̪in̪i ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔ pɔt̪ʰɔ bet͡ɕʰe n̪ie̯et͡ɕʰen̪ s̪e bɔɽɔ hɔbe
d̪̤armik aɡe d̪ir̤ɡ̤ɔ s̪e s̪ei ɕan̪t̪i l̪ab̤ kɔrɔbe
d͡za bɔd̪ɔl̪ae̯ n̪a। he b̤art̪er d͡zubrad͡ʑ
n̪iɕt͡ɕit̪ ho d͡ze keu bin̪ɔʂtɔ hɔt̪e pare n̪a amake biɕbas̪ kɔre
he pɽit̪ʰar put̪rɔ d͡ze amar d̪ike ɸirbe
d͡zɔd̪io t̪ara paper ɡɔrb̤ɔ t̪ʰeke d͡ʑɔn̪mɔɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔret͡ɕʰe
n̪ari ba puruʂ bojɕd͡zɔ bɔrner d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ
ba n̪ɔmrɔb̤abe obɔhel̪it̪ ɕud̪rɔ s̪ɔkɔl̪ɔ
s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ pɔt̪ʰer upɔrɔ pa l̪aɡan̪ t̪ahɔl̪e kib̤abe
pɔbit̪rɔ brahmɔnɔ ebɔŋ amar rad͡ʑkie̯ s̪ad̪̤ura
ahɔ t̪ɔোmɔra d͡zara ei os̪us̪t̪ʰɔ pɽit̪ʰibit̪e es̪et͡ɕʰ
kʂɔnɔs̪t̪ʰae̯i ebɔŋ mit̪ʰd͡za amar upɔrɔ apn̪ar biɕbas̪ d̪rut̪ s̪et kɔrun̪
amar upɔrɔ hɽid̪e̯ɔ ebɔŋ t͡ɕin̪t̪a tʰik kɔrun̪ amake ad̪ɔrɔ kɔrɔো an̪un̪
amar kat͡ɕʰe oɸar amake s̪id͡ʑd̪a kɔrɔ t̪ojri kɔrun̪
ami t̪ɔোmar s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ ebɔŋ obib̤ɔkt̪ɔ
amar biɕramer kat͡ɕʰe apn̪ar at̪ma pɔrit͡ɕal̪it̪ hɔbe।
ekʰan̪e n̪ɔbɔmɔ od̪̤d͡zae̯ ɕeʂ he̯ɔ। b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar

od̪̤d͡zae̯ 
kɽiʂna #
aro d̪ure ɕɔোn̪ɔ he s̪ud̪ir̤ɡ̤ɔ s̪ɔɕɔs̪t̪rɔ prɔb̤u ei s̪ɔrbɔɕeʂ kɔt̪ʰaɡul̪ো ami bɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰi
apn̪ake s̪ukʰ ebɔŋ ɕan̪t̪i an̪t̪e ut͡ɕt͡ɕarɔnɔ kɔret͡ɕʰen̪ d͡zin̪i amake s̪ɔrbɔd̪a b̤al̪োbas̪en̪
d̪ebt̪ad̪er mɔhɔt̪ɔ s̪ɔŋɡɔ ba rad͡ʑa ɽiʂira d͡ʑan̪en̪ n̪a
amar prɔkɽit̪i d͡zara d̪ebt̪a o ɽiʂid̪er on̪ek aɡei ban̪ie̯et͡ɕʰen̪
t̪in̪i kebɔl̪ɔ d͡ʑan̪en̪ kebɔl̪ɔ t̪in̪ii papmukt̪ɔ ebɔŋ d͡ʑnan̪i
d͡zin̪i amake biɕbɔd͡ʑɔɡɔt̪er prɔb̤u biɕbas̪al̪োkit̪ t͡ɕɔোkʰɔ d̪ie̯e d̪ekʰen̪
od͡ʑat̪ omɽit̪ on̪aɡɔt̪ɔ। prɔkɽit̪i d͡zai hɔোkɔ n̪a ken̪
n̪ɔɕbɔrɔ man̪uʂer kat͡ɕʰe bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔra he̯ɔ s̪ei prɔkɽit̪iɡul̪i amar kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke as̪e
bud̪d̪̤i d̪ɔkʂɔt̪a d͡ʑnan̪ s̪ɔhɔn̪ɔɕil̪t̪a at̪mɔn̪ie̯ɔn̪t̪rɔnɔ
s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔbad̪it̪a s̪amd͡zɔt̪a ebɔŋ d̪uঃkʰɔ ba at̪mar an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ
ebɔŋ d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ ebɔŋ mɽit̪d͡zu ebɔŋ b̤e̯ɔ ebɔŋ n̪irb̤ikt̪a ebɔŋ l̪ɔd͡ʑd͡ʑa
ebɔŋ s̪ɔmman̪ ebɔŋ mɔd̪̤ur kʂɔt̪ihin̪t̪a ebɔŋ ɕan̪t̪i d͡za
eki
d͡za kit͡ɕʰu ̤ɡ̤ɔte ebɔŋ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ ebɔŋ oɕru ebɔŋ d̪̤armikt̪a ebɔŋ s̪aɕre̯i
ebɔŋ d̪it̪e t͡ɕan̪ ebɔŋ s̪ahad͡zd͡zɔ kɔrɔt̪e t͡ɕan̪ s̪ɔbɔ amar upɔhar as̪e
s̪at̪ti prɔd̪̤an̪ s̪ad̪̤u prɔbin t͡ɕar prɔb̤ur man̪us̪ s̪et
amar kad͡ʑ b̤aɡab̤aɡi kɔre biɕbɔ ɕas̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔrar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ eiɡul̪io ami d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ d̪ie̯et͡ɕʰil̪am
ebɔŋ ɽiʂi pit̪ri man̪us̪ s̪ɔbai amar mɔn̪er ek b̤abn̪ae̯
s̪ekʰan̪ t̪ʰeke ud̪b̤ut̪ he̯et͡ɕʰil̪ ei biɕbɔke purnɔ kɔrar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ man̪ɔbɔd͡ʑat̪ir d͡ʑat̪i
kɔোt̪ʰa t̪ʰeke ke bud͡ʑ̤t̪e pare amar ot̪in̪d̪rie̯ mɔhiman̪bit̪ rad͡ʑɔt̪bɔ
s̪ɔt̪d͡zer s̪ei s̪ɔt̪d͡zekʰɔn̪ɔ t̪ʰeke amar s̪at̪ʰe t̪rutihin̪ biɕbas̪er s̪at̪ʰe d͡zukt̪ɔ he̯et͡ɕʰe
hd͡zɔ̃ amake s̪ɔkɔl̪er ut̪ɔs̪ɔ d͡ʑen̪e amar d̪barai s̪ɔkɔl̪ɔ s̪ɽiʂtir s̪ɽiʂti
at̪mae̯ d͡ʑnan̪ira amar s̪at̪ʰe s̪ɔŋd͡zukt̪ɔ t̪ʰake amar s̪ɔt̪t̪ae̯ n̪ie̯e as̪e
hɽid̪e̯ɔ amar upɔrɔ s̪t̪ʰir ɕbas̪ amar kat͡ɕʰe n̪iঃɕbas̪ prɔt̪d͡zeke amar prɔɕɔŋs̪a kɔre

ebɔŋ t̪ad̪er b̤al̪bas̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ami t̪ad̪er on̪d̪̤ɔkar at̪mar mɔd̪̤d͡ze bas̪ kɔri

ord͡ʑun̪।

t̪ɔোmar os̪ɔŋkʰd͡zɔ rup ki ruper n̪it͡ɕe

ord͡ʑun̪।

oɡnit̪ mukʰ t̪ʰeke ad̪eɕ
oɡnit̪ rɔhɔs̪d͡zɔme̯ɔ ɸɔrmɔ 
ek ɸɔrme s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔb̤abe d̪ɔ̃ɽie̯e
oɡnit̪ d̪ipt̪ime̯ɔ mɔhima pɔra
oɡnit̪ s̪bɔrɡie̯ os̪t̪rɔ bɔhɔn̪ɔ kɔre
t̪araɡut͡ɕt͡ɕʰer mal̪a d̪ie̯e mukut pɔran̪ো
bɔোn̪a l̪ɔোb̤er s̪ad͡ʑe

s̪ɔbɔ s̪bɔrɡie̯ ɡɔn̪d̪̤ɔ ɕediŋ
on̪d̪̤ɔ t̪ed͡ʑ ot̪imat̪rae̯
s̪imahin̪ s̪un̪d̪ɔrɔ s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ s̪t̪ʰan̪

t̪ai t̪in̪i d̪ekʰal̪en̪ d͡zɔd̪i otʰa ut͡ɕit̪
hɔtʰat̪ akaɕer mɔd̪̤d͡ze
had͡ʑar s̪urd͡zer s̪urd͡zɔোd̪e̯ɔ
bimer s̪at̪ʰe pl̪abit̪ pɽit̪ʰibi
t̪ahɔl̪e hɔt̪e pare d͡ze pɔbit̪rɔ ek

pandur put̪ro t̪ai d̪ekʰet͡ɕʰil̪en̪
ei s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ mɔhabiɕbɔ bis̪t̪ɽit̪

ekti biɕal̪ akare ebɔŋ hɔt̪e

d̪ebt̪a 
kin̪t̪u kʰub obak hɔl̪am
rɔোmant͡ɕit̪ muɡɔd̪̤ɔ muɡɔd̪̤ɔ ebɔŋ bis̪mit̪
ord͡ʑun̪ n̪ɔt̪ɔd͡ʑan̪u ebɔŋ mat̪ʰa n̪ɔt̪ɔ kɔrɔl̪ɔ
ebɔŋ t̪ar hat̪er t̪al̪u ãkəɽe d̪̤ɔrɔl̪ɔ ebɔŋ kɔ̃d̪ɔl̪en̪ ebɔŋ bɔl̪ɔl̪en̪
ord͡ʑun̪।
hd͡zɔ̃ ami d̪ekʰet͡ɕʰi ami d̪ekʰi
prɔb̤u s̪ɔbɔ t̪ɔোmar mɔd̪̤d͡ze abɽit̪
d̪ebt̪ara t̪ɔোmar mɔhiman̪bit̪ ɸreme d͡ʑib
pɽit̪ʰibi s̪bɔrɡɔ ebɔŋ n̪ɔrɔker
t̪ɔোmar ojɕbɔrik rupe bas̪ kɔrɔো
ebɔŋ t̪ɔোmar t͡ɕeharae̯ s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ bojɕiʂtd͡zɔ ud͡ʑd͡ʑbɔl̪ɔ
brɔhmar eka bɔs̪e
t̪ɔ̃rɔ pɔd̪mɔs̪iŋhas̪n̪e

hd͡zɔ̃ s̪ɔrbɔɕɔkt̪iman̪ prɔb̤u ami d̪ekʰi
t̪ɔোmar had͡ʑar had͡ʑar bahu s̪t̪ɔn̪ɔ o mukʰ
ebɔŋ t͡ɕɔোkʰɔ s̪ɔbɔ d̪ike

at̪mar d̪ɽiʂti d͡zed̪ike t̪akae̯
t̪ɔোmar ken̪d̪rie̯ s̪be̯ɔŋ s̪ɔrbɔɕɔkt̪iman̪ ebɔŋ s̪ɔrbɔd͡ʑe̯i
os̪im rad͡ʑa ami d̪ekʰi
t̪ɔোmar upɔrɔ an̪ad̪em

os̪ɔhd͡zɔ rɔɕmit̪e
al̪োkit̪ pɽit̪ʰibi s̪bɔrɡɔ ebɔŋ n̪ɔrɔkɔ

tred͡ʑarɔpras̪ad̪ t̪ojri kɔret͡ɕʰe

pund͡zer ain̪ke aɕre̯ɔ d̪it̪e

ek od͡ʑat̪ obiram
opribɔrt̪ɔn̪ie̯ ebɔŋ opribɔrt̪it̪

s̪urd͡zer ɡɔৌrɔbɔ ̤ɡ̤urnit̪ he̯ɔ

t̪ara ebɔŋ akaɕ d͡ʑuɽe
uʂnɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ bis̪me̯ɔ dɔt̪ʰɔ

t̪ɔোmar pɔripurnɔt̪a s̪t̪ʰan̪
t̪arkat͡ɕʰitie̯e ebɔŋ okard͡zɔkɔrɔ d͡ʑae̯ɡa

t̪umi t̪umi d͡zekʰan̪e t̪umi n̪ei
he pɔbit̪rɔ opurbɔ rup kɔোt̪ʰao paoe̯a d͡zae̯ n̪a
he rɔhɔs̪d͡zɔme̯i b̤e̯ɔŋkɔrɔ
t̪ɔোmar d̪ekʰad̪ekʰi d͡ʑan̪a ɡel̪
t̪in̪ biɕber b̤umikɔmpɔ n̪it͡ɕer d̪ebt̪ara t̪ɔোmar kat͡ɕʰe as̪e

ɕɔrir ebɔŋ s̪t̪ɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ b̤ru

ɽiʂi o s̪id̪d̪̤ɔra kɔ̃d̪e
hae̯ s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ mɔhima

t̪ɔোmar prɔɕɔŋs̪a d̪̤bɔn̪i
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ os̪ɔŋkʰd͡zɔ kɔোmpan̪i ɡɔl̪pɔti ɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔre
rud̪rɔra d͡zara d͡ʑ̤ɔɽe t͡ɕɔɽe
ad̪it̪d͡zɔd̪er ud͡ʑd͡ʑbɔl̪ɔ rup

he iɕbɔrer t͡ɕɔোkʰɔ he mat̪ʰa

kɽiʂnɔ।
t̪umi amake s̪ɔme̯ɔ his̪abe d̪ekʰো d͡ze hɔt̪d͡za kɔre
s̪ɔme̯ɔ d͡ze s̪ɔkɔl̪ɔke s̪ɔrbɔn̪aɕer d̪ike n̪ie̯e as̪e
d̪d͡zɔ s̪l̪ee̯ar taim o্d͡zan̪s̪ie̯en̪tɔ oɸ ded͡ʑ ɡɔras̪ kɔrɔt̪e ekʰan̪e as̪a
t̪ɔোmake bad̪ d̪ie̯e ei s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ ɕɔt̪ru prɔd̪̤an̪d̪er s̪ɔd͡ʑd͡ʑit̪ s̪ojn̪d͡zɔd̪ɔl̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze
d͡zud̪d̪̤er me̯ɔd̪an̪e kauke d͡ʑibit̪ t͡ɕʰeɽe d͡zabe n̪a hɔt̪aɕ
ar t̪ʰakbe n̪a utʰi kʰd͡zat̪i ord͡ʑɔn̪ɔ t̪ɔোmar ɕɔt̪rud̪er d̪̤bɔŋs̪ɔ kɔrɔ
s̪ei rad͡ʑd͡zer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ d͡zud̪d̪̤ɔ kɔrɔ d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ t̪umi t̪ad̪er pɔrad͡ʑit̪ kɔret͡ɕʰ।
amar d̪bara t̪ara pɔɽe apn̪i n̪a mɽit̪d͡zur s̪trɔোkɔ ekʰɔn̪ɔ t̪ad̪er mɔোkabel̪a kɔra he̯ɔ
emɔn̪ɔki t̪ara d͡zemɔn̪ɔ s̪ahɔs̪ib̤abe d̪ekʰae̯ amar d͡zɔn̪t̪rɔ t̪umi
a̤ɡ̤at̪ kɔrɔ bɔl̪ɔban̪ s̪ɔɕɔs̪t̪rɔ d͡zubrad͡ʑ d̪rɔোne b̤iʂmɔ d̪̤ɔrmɔ̤ɡ̤ɔte mɽit̪d͡zu mɔোkabel̪a
kɔrnɔ d͡ʑe̯ɔd̪rɔt̪ʰer upɔrɔ t̪ad̪er s̪ɔbɔ d͡zud̪d̪̤er n̪iঃɕbas̪ t̪ʰakun̪

hd͡zɔ̃ eta bis̪me̯ɔkɔrɔ ebɔŋ b̤e̯an̪ɔkɔ t͡ɕʰil̪

ord͡ʑun̪।
prɔb̤u d͡zara apn̪ar s̪eba kɔre t̪ad̪er mɔd̪̤d͡zes̪ɔt̪d͡zikar on̪t̪ɔre
d͡zemɔn̪ɔ iɕbɔrɔ prɔkaɕ kɔret͡ɕʰen̪ ebɔŋ d͡zara s̪eba kɔre
oprɔkaɕit̪ oɕriri d̪ur t̪ɔোmar upas̪n̪a
kɔোn̪ɔti iman̪ o d͡ʑibn̪er ut̪t̪ɔmɔ pɔt̪ʰɔ ɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔre
kɽiʂnɔ।
d͡ze amake s̪eba kɔrid͡zemɔn̪ɔ ami n̪id͡ʑeke d̪ekʰai

d͡zara amake kʰub pɔbit̪rɔ mɔn̪e kɔre। kin̪t̪u d͡zara pɔribeɕɔn̪ɔ kɔren̪
amake upas̪n̪a kɔra ek od̪ɽiɕd͡zɔ
oprɔkaɕit̪ n̪amɔhin̪ ot͡ɕin̪t̪ɔn̪ie̯
s̪ɔrbɔোt̪t̪ɔmɔ s̪ɔrbɔbd͡zapi s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ n̪iɕt͡ɕit̪
d͡zara eib̤abe amake upas̪n̪a kɔre t̪ad̪er bɔোd̪̤ɔke ae̯ɔt̪t̪ɔ kɔre
s̪ɔkɔl̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ek mɔn̪e s̪ɔkɔl̪ɔ b̤al̪োt̪e an̪ɔn̪d̪it̪
ei d̪̤ɔn̪d͡zɔ at̪ma amar kat͡ɕʰe as̪e।
t̪ɔbuo kɔtʰin̪

obd͡zɔkt̪ɔ s̪ei d̪ɽiʂtihin̪ pɔt̪ʰe pɔৌ̃t͡ʃʰəte

ɕud̪̤umat̪rɔ s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ rat̪ d̪in̪ s̪eba kɔrɔt̪e
amar upɔrɔ t͡ɕit̪kar kɔra t̪ake ami d̪rut̪ t̪ul̪ɔbɔ
d͡ʑibn̪er d̪urd̪ɔɕa o mɽit̪d͡zur s̪aɡɔrɔ t̪ʰeke berie̯e
d͡zar at̪ma amake ãkəɽe d̪̤ɔre। amake ãkəɽe d̪̤ɔrɔ
hɽid̪e̯ɔ ebɔŋ mɔn̪ɔ d̪ie̯e amake al̪iŋɡɔn̪ɔ kɔrun̪ t̪ai t̪umi bas̪ kɔrɔbe
obɔɕd͡zi amar s̪at̪ʰe ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪ae̯। kin̪t̪u d͡zɔd̪i apn̪ar t͡ɕin̪t̪a
d͡zemɔn̪ɔ ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪a t̪ʰeke d͡zɔd̪i apn̪i s̪et kɔrɔt̪e d̪urbɔl̪ɔ hɔn̪ɔ
ɕɔrir ebɔŋ at̪ma amar upɔrɔ krɔmaɡɔt̪ɔ
hɔt̪aɕa n̪a amake n̪imn̪ɔ s̪eba d̪in̪ t͡ɕaoe̯a
amar kat͡ɕʰe pɔৌ̃t͡ʃʰanোrɔ d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ otɔl̪ɔ it͡ɕt͡ɕʰar s̪at̪ʰe upas̪n̪a kɔra
ebɔŋ d͡zɔd̪i apn̪i obit͡ɕɔl̪ɔb̤abe ibad̪ɔt̪ɔ kɔrɔt̪e n̪a paren̪
amar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kad͡ʑ amar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔd̪ae̯ɔkɔ kad͡ʑ pɔriɕrɔmɔ

amar aɕre̯ɔ pɔriɕrɔmer ɸɔl̪ɔ d͡zet̪e d̪in̪
amar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ aɕa t̪d͡zaɡ kɔre n̪it͡ɕu hɽid̪e̯e
t̪ai t̪umi as̪be d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ d͡zɔd̪io d͡ʑan̪a aro beɕi

t̪d͡zaɡer kat͡ɕʰakat͡ɕʰikʰub kat͡ɕʰakat͡ɕʰi

d͡zar mɔd̪̤d͡ze bẽt͡ʃe t̪ʰaka n̪id͡ʑeke s̪ɔৌmd͡zɔ kɔre
s̪ɔhan̪ub̤ut̪iɕil̪ ohɔŋkar t̪ʰeke mukt̪ɔ

biɕbas̪e n̪id͡ʑeke ae̯ɔt̪t̪ɔ kɔre t̪ar kɔt̪ʰae̯ s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ
amake hɽid̪e̯ɔ ebɔŋ at̪ma kʰũd͡ʒət͡ʃʰen amar kat͡ɕʰe prɔt̪id͡ʑna kɔret͡ɕʰil̪en̪
d͡ze man̪uʂtake ami b̤al̪োbas̪i d͡ze t̪ar prɔkarke kɔʂtɔ d̪ee̯ n̪a

an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ ɕɔোkɔ ba b̤e̯er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kʰub beɕi bẽt͡ʃe t̪ʰaka
d͡ze man̪uʂtake ami b̤al̪োbas̪i ke ɕan̪t̪ɔ t͡ɕɔোkʰe bas̪ kɔre#

karো upɔrɔ t̪irɔs̪kar kɔre n̪a kauke opman̪ kɔre n̪a an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ kɔre n̪a

t̪ap ebɔŋ tʰan̪da l̪aɡe an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ ebɔŋ bd͡zɔt̪ʰa pal̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔre
bas̪n̪a t̪d͡zaɡ kɔrun̪ prɔɕɔŋs̪a ba opbad̪ ɕɔোn̪en̪

od̪̤d͡zae̯ 
ord͡ʑun̪।
ekʰɔn̪ɔ ki ɕun̪ɔbɔ he d̪e̯ame̯ɔ keɕɔbɔ#
d͡ʑibn̪er d͡za mɔn̪e he̯ɔ ebɔŋ at̪mar baire d͡za d̪ekʰe
ebɔŋ eta ki amra d͡ʑan̪iba d͡ʑan̪ar kɔt̪ʰa b̤abi।
kɽiʂnɔ।
hd͡zɔ̃ kun̪t̪ir t͡ɕʰel̪e ei maŋs̪ɔ d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ apn̪i d̪ekʰt̪e
kʂet̪rɔ ki kʂet̪rɔ d͡zekʰan̪e d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕɔl̪e d͡zae̯
ebɔŋ d͡za d̪ekʰe ebɔŋ d͡ʑan̪e t̪a hɔl̪ɔ at̪ma
kʂet̪rɔd͡ʑnan̪। s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ kʂet̪re t̪umi b̤art̪ie̯ rad͡ʑput̪rɔ
ami kʂet̪rɔd͡ʑnɔ। ami ki d͡ʑɔrip
kebɔl̪ɔ s̪ei d͡ʑnan̪i d͡ʑan̪e d͡ze d͡ʑan̪e d͡ʑan̪e
d͡ʑan̪ar kɔs̪ɔmɔ# eta ki d͡ʑibn̪er s̪ei kʂet̪rɔ
er ki ki ɡunabl̪i re̯et͡ɕʰe ebɔŋ eti kɔোt̪ʰa t̪ʰeke
ebɔŋ ken̪ eti pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ on̪uʂɔd̪ɔ
d͡ze eta er ɕɔkt̪i
ar amar kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke ei s̪ɔbɔ kɔt̪ʰa ɕun̪t̪e kemɔn̪ɔ l̪aɡe
 eɸen̪#২৮
upad̪an̪ s̪ɔt͡ɕet̪ɔn̪ɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ mɔn̪ɔ
od̪ekʰa pranɔɕɔkt̪i n̪e̯ɔti od̪b̤ut̪ d̪ɔrɔd͡ʑa
ɕɔrirer ebɔŋ in̪d̪rie̯ pɔ̃t͡ɕɔti dɔোmen̪
it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa opɔt͡ɕʰɔn̪d̪ɔ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔbed̪n̪a ebɔŋ t͡ɕin̪t̪a
ɡɔb̤ir bɔোn̪a ebɔŋ s̪ɔt̪t̪ar od̪̤d͡zɔbɔs̪ae̯
ei s̪ɔbɔ at̪ma d̪bara md͡zatar upɔrɔ t̪ojri kɔra he̯ɔ

d̪̤ojrd͡zɔ ebɔŋ s̪ɔmman̪ d͡ʑnan̪id̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ɕrɔd̪d̪̤a।
biɕud̪d̪̤ɔt̪a s̪t̪ʰirt̪a n̪id͡ʑer n̪ie̯ɔn̪t̪rɔnɔ
in̪d̪rie̯an̪ɔn̪d̪er obɔd͡ʑna at̪mɔt̪d͡zaɡ
os̪us̪t̪ʰɔt̪ar n̪iɕt͡ɕit̪t̪ar upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤i
d͡ʑɔn̪me mɽit̪d͡zut̪e be̯ɔs̪e rɔোɡe d̪uঃkʰe pape
bit͡ɕt͡ɕʰin̪n̪ɔt̪a hal̪kab̤abe baɽit̪e d̪̤ɔre rakʰa

amake upas̪n̪a kɔrɔt̪e ɕud̪̤umat̪rɔ ami t̪ʰamt͡ɕʰe n̪a
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ n̪ird͡ʑɔn̪ɔt̪a ebɔŋ kɔোl̪ahɔl̪ɔ t̪ʰeke d̪ure t̪ʰaka
murkʰɔ d͡ʑɔn̪ɔt̪ar d̪ɽiɽ̤ pre̯as̪
pɔrɔmɔ at̪mar upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤it̪e pɔৌ̃t͡ʃʰanোrɔ d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ

ar t̪a n̪a hɔl̪e ki od͡ʑnɔt̪a
ekʰɔn̪ɔ ami s̪ɔbɔt͡ɕee̯e b̤al̪ো d͡ʑnan̪er kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪ɔbɔ
d͡ze s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ man̪uʂke pan̪ kɔrɔt̪e d̪ee̯ omɽit̪

d͡zar hat̪ s̪ɔrbɔt̪rɔ s̪ɔrbɔt̪rɔ

al̪োkit̪ ebɔŋ t̪ar d͡ʑɔɡɔt̪ɔ pɔribeʂtɔn̪ɔ

t̪ɔt̪ʰapi t̪in̪i bas̪ kɔren̪ os̪ɔŋl̪ɔɡɔn̪ɔ rup o pɔd̪d̪̤ɔt̪ir
ɡuru t̪ɔbuo t̪ɔ̃rɔ rup ba rup n̪ei
t̪in̪i s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ pranir mɔd̪̤d͡ze ebɔŋ t͡ɕʰaɽa
ɡɔt̪ihin̪ t̪ɔbuo t͡ɕɔl̪ɔman̪ n̪irne̯ɔ kɔra he̯ɔn̪i
t̪at̪kʂɔnik upɔs̪t̪ʰit̪ir s̪ukʂmɔt̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ
s̪ɔbar kat͡ɕʰe prɔt̪d͡zeker kat͡ɕʰe t̪ɔbuo pɔrimapɔhin̪b̤abe d̪ure
bɔhuɡun n̪e̯ɔ ebɔŋ ekʰn̪o tike at͡ɕʰe
d͡za s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕirkal̪ pɔrit͡ɕit̪ hoe̯ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
teks̪i his̪abe t̪ɔbuo s̪ɔme̯er ɕeʂe
t̪in̪i s̪ɔbɔkit͡ɕʰuke ɕeʂ kɔre d̪en̪ ebɔŋ pun̪rae̯ s̪ɽiʂti kɔren̪।
al̪োrɔ al̪ো t̪in̪i on̪d̪̤ɔkarer hɽid̪e̯e
on̪ɔn̪t̪ɔkal̪ d͡ʑbɔl̪ɔd͡ʑbɔl̪ɔ kɔrɔt͡ɕʰe। prɔd͡ʑna t̪in̪i
ebɔŋ prɔd͡ʑnar pɔt̪ʰɔ ebɔŋ s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑnan̪id̪er pɔt̪ʰɔprɔd̪ɔrɕɔkɔ

t̪ai bɔl̪et͡ɕʰi
d͡ʑibn̪er d͡ʑin̪is̪ɔpɔt̪rɔ ebɔŋ d̤al̪ai ebɔŋ bid̪d͡za

eta upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤i kɔre obɔɕd͡zi amar kat͡ɕʰe as̪be
t̪umi d͡ʑan̪ো d͡ze prɔkɽit̪i ebɔŋ at̪ma ub̤e̯i

bed̪n̪a ebɔŋ an̪ɔn̪d̪er on̪ub̤ut̪i। at̪ma s̪ɔŋd͡zukt̪ɔ
d̤al̪ai pɔd̪art̪ʰɔ bɔn̪dɔ mɔd̪̤d͡ze

b̤al̪ো ba mɔn̪d̪ɔ d͡zɔোn̪it̪e।#
t̪ɔbuo ei
hd͡zɔ̃ er ɕaririk karaɡare pɔbit̪rɔ at̪ma
at̪ma s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ d͡ʑɔrip ɕas̪ɔn̪ɔ
ɡardiŋ prɔb̤u ebɔŋ mas̪tar ekʰn̪o

d͡ze eib̤abe n̪id͡ʑeke d͡ʑan̪e ebɔŋ t̪ar at̪make d͡ʑan̪e
puruʂ ɡuner mad̪̤d͡zɔme kad͡ʑ kɔra
prɔkɽit̪ir mɔোdɔ n̪ie̯e t̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ al̪ো es̪et͡ɕʰe
s̪e d͡ze maŋs̪i bɔhɔn̪ɔ kɔruk n̪a ken̪ ar kɔkʰɔn̪ɔো n̪e̯ɔ
s̪e ki er b̤ar bɔhɔn̪ɔ kɔrɔbe kit͡ɕʰu kit͡ɕʰu at͡ɕʰe
d̪̤d͡zan̪er mad̪̤d͡zɔme at̪mar mɔd̪̤d͡ze at̪make s̪ɔn̪d̪̤an̪ kɔrun̪
s̪bɔbid̪d͡zal̪e̯ɔ ebɔŋ kit͡ɕʰu d̪ir̤ɡ̤ɔ d̪ɔrɕɔn̪ɔ d̪bara
ebɔŋ pɔbit̪rɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ s̪ekʰan̪e pɔৌ̃t͡ʃʰan kit͡ɕʰu kad͡ʑ d̪bara
kit͡ɕʰu kɔkʰɔn̪o t̪ai ord͡ʑɔn̪ɔ al̪ো ɕun̪t̪e

ob̤arpas̪ mɽit̪d͡zu
d͡zekʰan̪ei hɔোkɔ b̤art̪ie̯ d͡zubrad͡ʑ
d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ hɔl̪ɔt͡ɕɔl̪ɔman̪ d͡ʑin̪is̪er ba ot͡ɕɔl̪ɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪er
rɔোpɔnɔ ba ekʰn̪o bid͡ʑd͡ʑan̪ s̪ekʰan̪e ki at͡ɕʰe bɔɽɔ he̯et͡ɕʰe
bɔs̪t̪u ebɔŋ at̪mar bɔn̪d̪̤ɔn̪ɔ d̪bara d͡ʑan̪un̪
t̪in̪i as̪l̪ei d̪ekʰen̪ d͡zin̪i s̪ɔkɔl̪ɔke ekib̤abe d̪ekʰen̪
d͡ʑibɔn̪t̪ɔ prɔb̤u at̪ma at̪ma s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ
d̪̤bɔŋs̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze obin̪ɔɕbɔrɔ

prɔt̪iti rupe eki ek bẽt͡ʃe t̪ʰaka d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ
n̪id͡ʑer prɔt̪i ar kɔোn̪ɔ on̪d͡zae̯ kɔrɔben̪ n̪a
kin̪t̪u s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ ras̪t̪a d͡zae̯ d͡za an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ n̪ie̯e as̪e।
d̪ekʰe t̪in̪i d̪ekʰen̪ prɔkɽit̪ɔpɔkʂe d͡zin̪i d̪ekʰen̪ d͡ze kad͡ʑ kɔre
prɔkɽit̪ir ob̤d͡zas̪ at̪ma d̪bara on̪uɕil̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔrar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
ob̤in̪e̯ɔ t̪ɔbuo ed͡ʑen̪tɔ n̪e̯ɔ b̤ɔrɔ d̪ekʰe
pɽit̪ʰɔkɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪erɔprɔt̪d͡zekti
ek t̪ʰeke is̪d͡zu ebɔŋ abar eker s̪at̪ʰe miɕrit̪ kɔrun̪
t̪ahɔl̪e s̪e brɔhmɔ l̪ab̤ kɔre
he rad͡ʑkumar
s̪ei t͡ɕuɽan̪t̪ɔ ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔ at̪ma oprɔs̪t̪ut̪
od͡zোɡɔd͡zɔ emɔn̪ɔki d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ eti maŋs̪e prɔbeɕ kɔre
kad͡ʑer kɔোn̪ɔ d̪aɡ l̪aɡe n̪a kɔোn̪ɔ kad͡ʑ kɔre n̪a
it̪ʰarie̯ bat̪as̪er mɔt̪ɔো s̪ɔrbɔt̪rɔ bis̪t̪ɽit̪
d͡za n̪it͡ɕʰɔkɔ s̪ukʂmɔt̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kɔl̪ɔŋkɔ eɽae̯
s̪ukʂmɔ at̪ma s̪ɔrbɔt̪rɔ birad͡ʑ kɔre n̪irmɔl̪ɔ
s̪ɔbɔ b̤ed̪ kɔra s̪urd͡zer al̪োrɔ mɔt̪ɔো
d͡za kit͡ɕʰut̪ei pɔribɔrt̪it̪ he̯ɔ n̪a t̪a al̪োkit̪ kɔre
at̪mar al̪ো s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑae̯ɡae̯ biɕud̪d̪̤ɔ d͡ʑbɔl̪e
ebɔŋ d͡zara d͡ʑnan̪er emɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕɔোkʰɔ d̪ie̯e d̪ekʰe
kib̤abe bd͡zapar ebɔŋ ki eta s̪ɔŋɡe dil̪ bib̤ad͡ʑɔn̪ɔ
ebɔŋ kib̤abe at̪ma ebɔŋ maŋs̪ɔ bibad̪ at͡ɕʰe
s̪ei d͡ʑnan̪ira s̪ei pɔt̪ʰe t͡ɕɔl̪e d͡za d͡ʑibn̪er d̪ike n̪ie̯e d͡zae̯
ekʰan̪e od̪̤d͡zae̯ ɕeʂ he̯ɔ b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar
ɕirোn̪am kʂet̪rɔkʂet̪rɔd͡ʑnan̪bib̤aɡ
ot̪ʰba bɔs̪t̪u ebɔŋ at̪mar bit͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ d̪bara d̪̤ɔrmer bi।




t͡ɕɔt̪urd̪ɔɕɔ od̪̤d͡zae̯
kɽiʂnɔ।
t̪ɔbuo ami apn̪ar kat͡ɕʰe aro d̪ure kʰul̪ɔbɔ
s̪ɔkɔl̪ɔ prɔd͡ʑnar ei prɔd͡ʑna pɔrɔmɔ
d͡zar od̪̤ikari amar s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ s̪ad̪̤ɔkɔ ɡɔt̪ɔ he̯et͡ɕʰen̪
n̪ikʰũtətar d̪ike। d͡zemɔn̪ɔ ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔ s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ upɔrɔ
n̪irb̤ɔrɔɕil̪ ɸel̪োɕipe utʰt͡ɕʰe
amar s̪at̪ʰe t̪ara abar d͡ʑɔn̪me d͡ʑɔn̪mae̯ n̪a
kɔl̪per n̪a prɔl̪d͡zas̪e b̤uɡe pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪ɔ
ei mɔhabiɕber ɡɔrb̤ɔ d͡zekʰan̪e ami rɔোpɔnɔ kɔri
s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑibn̪er bid͡ʑ t̪arɔpɔrɔ b̤art̪er d͡zubrad͡ʑ as̪e
s̪ɔbɔ pranir d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ hus̪ kun̪t̪ir t͡ɕʰel̪e
mae̯era prɔt̪iti n̪ɔɕbɔrɔ rup brɔhma ɡɔrb̤ɔd̪̤arɔnɔ kɔren̪
ar amii s̪ei pit̪ɽipuruʂ bɔŋɕɔ prerɔnɔkari
s̪ɔt̪t̪ban̪ rɔd͡ʑɔs̪ɔ t̪ɔmɔs̪ɔ t̪ai n̪amɔkɔrɔnɔ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe
prɔkɽit̪ir ɡunabl̪i s̪us̪t̪ʰɔt̪a
abeɡ ebɔŋ od͡ʑnɔt̪a। ei t̪in̪ti bɔn̪d̪̤ɔn̪ɔ
pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪ɔɕil̪ ɕɔrire pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪ɔhin̪ at̪ma।
d͡zar mɔd̪̤d͡ze miʂti prɔɕan̪t̪i biɕud̪d̪̤ɔt̪a d̪bara
oɕan̪t̪ɔ ebɔŋ al̪োkit̪ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔd͡zapɔn̪ɔ abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre
s̪ukʰ ebɔŋ s̪ɔt̪d͡zer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ papɔhin̪ at̪ma
ebɔŋ pd͡zaɕɔn̪ɔ kʂud̪̤ar at̪mie̯ hoe̯a
ebɔŋ prɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔn̪ɔ abeɡ ebɔŋ prɔbɔnɔt̪a
murt̪ɔ at̪make bɔ̃d̪̤e he kun̪t̪ir put̪rɔ
kad͡ʑer tai d̪bara kin̪t̪u od͡ʑnɔt̪a d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ
on̪d̪̤ɔkarer n̪ɔɕbɔrɔ man̪uʂke on̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre bẽd̤e d̪ee̯
t̪ad̪er at̪ma s̪t̪ɔbd̪̤ɔ al̪ɔs̪d͡zɔ ebɔŋ t̪ɔn̪d̪ra
hd͡zɔ̃ b̤art̪er d͡zubrad͡ʑ prɔɕan̪t̪i at̪make abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre
in̪ ebɔŋ abeɡ abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ
pɔriɕrɔmi s̪tren̪ d̪bara kin̪t̪u od͡ʑnɔt̪a d͡za d̪aɡ
d͡ʑnan̪er rɔɕmi at̪make al̪ɔs̪d͡ze abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre।
abeɡ ebɔŋ od͡ʑnɔt̪a ekbar pɔras̪t̪ɔ
prɔɕan̪t̪i t̪d͡zaɡ kɔrɔ he b̤ɔrɔt̪ɔ d͡zekʰan̪e ei
od͡ʑnɔt̪a on̪upɔs̪t̪ʰit̪ s̪ɔŋɡe abeɡ n̪ie̯ɔmɔ
ebɔŋ on̪t̪ɔre od͡ʑnɔt̪a b̤al̪ ba d̪rut̪ n̪e̯ɔ।
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ ɕɔrirer s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ prɔbeɕɔd̪barɡul̪i d͡ʑbɔl̪ɔd͡ʑbɔl̪ɔ kɔre
d͡ʑnan̪er prɔd̪ip t̪ahɔl̪e keu b̤al̪োb̤abe d̪ekʰt̪e pabe
prɔɕan̪t̪i s̪ei ɕɔhɔre rad͡ʑɔt̪bɔ kɔre
d͡zekʰan̪e akaŋkʂa ebɔŋ akul̪t̪a ebɔŋ os̪t̪ʰirt̪a
prɔt͡ɕeʂta ebɔŋ l̪ab̤er prɔrɔোt͡ɕɔn̪a ebɔŋ l̪ɔোb̤ɔ
abeɡ t̪ʰeke d͡zara bɔs̪ɔn̪t̪ɔprin̪s̪ɔt̪ojri ebɔŋ d͡zekʰan̪e
on̪d̪̤ɔkar ebɔŋ n̪is̪t̪ed͡ʑt̪a al̪ɔs̪d͡zɔ ebɔŋ muɽ̤t̪a
t̪is̪ od͡ʑnan̪t̪a t̪ad̪er ̤ɡ̤ɔtie̯et͡ɕʰe kuru prɔd̪̤an̪
t̪ɔd̪upri d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ ekti at̪ma t͡ɕɔl̪e d͡zae̯ s̪t̪ʰir he̯ɔ
prɔɕan̪t̪it̪e eti d͡zae̯ɡae̯ d͡zae̯
n̪ikʰũtə ebɔŋ biɕud̪d̪̤ɔ d͡zara s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ d͡ʑan̪e।
eta s̪et ob̤d͡zas̪ prɔs̪t̪ʰan̪ d͡zɔd̪i
impal̪ɔs̪er eti biɕber mɔd̪̤d͡ze pas̪ hɔbe
kad͡ʑer s̪at̪ʰe abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ at̪mar ebɔŋ d͡zɔd̪i eti mara d͡zae̯
kɔtʰin̪ od͡ʑnɔt̪ae̯ s̪ei on̪d̪̤ɔ at̪ma
kɔোn̪ɔ al̪োhin̪ ɡɔrb̤e n̪ɔt̪un̪ kɔre d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ n̪ee̯।
prɔɕan̪t̪ir ɸɔl̪ɔ s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ ebɔŋ miʂti
l̪al̪s̪ar ɸɔl̪ɔ hɔl̪ɔ kɔʂtɔ o pɔriɕrɔmɔ ɸɔl̪ɔti
od͡ʑnɔt̪ar ɡɔb̤ir on̪d̪̤ɔkar। hd͡zɔ̃
karɔnɔ al̪ো al̪ো an̪e ebɔŋ abeɡ bd͡zɔt̪ʰa at͡ɕʰe
ebɔŋ hɔt̪aɕa bib̤ran̪t̪i ebɔŋ od͡ʑnɔt̪a
od͡ʑnɔt̪a t̪ʰeke beɽe utʰun̪। prɔt̪ʰɔmɔ d͡zara
kɔkʰɔn̪o ut͡ɕt͡ɕe utʰun̪ d̪bit̪ie̯ mɔোdɔ d͡zara
ekti mad͡ʑ̤kʰan̪e d͡ʑae̯ɡa n̪in̪ on̪d̪̤ɔkar at̪ma ɸire dube
n̪it͡ɕu ɡɔhɔn̪ɔ bud̪d̪̤ihin̪t̪ae̯ b̤arakran̪t̪ɔ
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ d̪ekʰe d͡ʑibit̪ man̪uʂ upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤i kɔre
ekmat̪rɔ ob̤in̪et̪ari ɡun
ebɔŋ d͡ʑan̪e ɡuner baire ki n̪ie̯ɔmɔ
t̪ahɔl̪e s̪e ki amar n̪ikɔtɔbɔrt̪i he̯ɔ
at̪ma
eib̤abe t̪in̪ti ɡun t̪ʰeke berie̯e as̪a
d͡zar d̪bara s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d̪eher ut̪t̪ʰan̪ he̯ɔ pɔras̪t̪ɔ he̯ɔ
d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ mɽit̪d͡zu d̪uঃkʰɔ ebɔŋ be̯ɔs̪ɔ ebɔŋ ɡɔb̤irb̤abe pan̪ kɔre
omɽit̪er obiram mɔd̪ɔ।
ord͡ʑun̪।
he amar pal̪ɔn̪ɔkɔrt̪a
d͡za t̪ake t͡ɕen̪ar al̪amɔt̪ɔ d͡ze t͡ɕɔl̪e ɡet͡ɕʰe
t̪in̪ti mɔোdɔ ot̪it̪ s̪e kib̤abe bɔ̃t͡ɕe ki upae̯
t̪ake t̪riɡun mɔোder baire n̪irapd̪e n̪ie̯e d͡zae̯
kɽiʂnɔ।
d͡zin̪i s̪ɔmɔt̪a n̪ie̯e s̪ɔmikʂa kɔren̪
d̪̤armikt̪ar d̪ipt̪i abeɡer d͡ʑ̤ɔɡɔɽa al̪ɔs̪d͡zɔ
od͡ʑnɔt̪ar raɡ n̪a hɔl̪e ora
it͡ɕt͡ɕʰakɽit̪ n̪a d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ t̪ara n̪a d͡ze bɔs̪e
t̪ad̪er mad͡ʑ̤e ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ prɔbas̪i ebɔŋ oprit͡ɕit̪
oprɔs̪t̪ut̪ d̪ɔ̃ɽan̪ো bɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰe n̪irmɔl̪ɔ
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ d͡ʑ̤amel̪a b̤eŋɡe d͡zae̯ eɡul̪োi ɡun
t̪in̪i d͡zar kat͡ɕʰe at̪mɔken̪d̪rik d̪uঃkʰɔ ebɔŋ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ
ekti ɕɔbd̪ɔ his̪abe ɕɔbd̪ɔ d͡zar ɡɔb̤irɔd̪ɔrɕɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕɔোkʰe
kl̪ɔোdɔ marbel̪ ebɔŋ s̪ɔোn̪a ek
d͡zar s̪ɔman̪ hɽid̪e̯e eki b̤ɔd̪rɔt̪a d̪̤arɔnɔ kɔre
s̪ud̪ɽiɕd͡zɔ ebɔŋ oprit̪ikɔrɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪ɡul̪ir d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ d̪ɽiɽ̤ s̪et
prɔɕɔŋs̪a ebɔŋ opman̪e s̪ɔn̪t̪uʂtɔ s̪ɔn̪t̪uʂtɔ
s̪ɔmman̪ ba os̪ɔmman̪ s̪ɔhɔ bɔn̪d̪̤ud̪er kat͡ɕʰe
ebɔŋ ɕɔt̪rud̪er prɔt̪i s̪ɔhɔn̪ɔɕil̪t̪ae̯ s̪ɔman̪
ud̪d͡zɔোɡɔ t̪ʰeke bit͡ɕt͡ɕʰin̪n̪ɔ t̪ar n̪amɔkɔrɔnɔ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe
