od̪̤d͡zae̯ 
kɽiʂnɔ।
puruʂra bɔl̪e oɕbɔt̪t̪ʰɔ bɔtɔɡat͡ɕʰ
d͡zar n̪it͡ɕe dal̪ upre ɕikɔɽɔ
t͡ɕirɔpɔbit̪rɔ ɡat͡ɕʰ। hd͡zɔ̃ er pat̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
ki s̪ɔbud͡ʑ ar d̪ɔোl̪a s̪t̪ɔbɔkɔ d͡za ɸis̪ɸis̪ kɔre s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ
d͡zin̪i oɕbɔt̪t̪ʰɔ d͡ʑan̪en̪ bed̪ d͡ʑan̪en̪ ebɔŋ s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑan̪en̪।
er ɕakʰaɡul̪i s̪bɔrɡe ɡul̪i kɔre ebɔŋ pɽit̪ʰibit̪e dube d͡zae̯ #
emɔn̪ɔki man̪uʂer kɔrmer mɔt̪ɔো d͡za t̪ad̪er d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ n̪ee̯
ɡunabl̪i t̪ʰeke er rupal̪i s̪pre ebɔŋ prɔs̪ɸutit̪
ebɔŋ er pɔrid̪̤ir s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ ud̪ɔɡɔrib ɕɔs̪d͡zɔ
s̪urd͡zɔ o bat̪as̪er t͡ɕumbɔn̪e d̪rut̪ d͡ʑibn̪er d̪ike d͡ʑ̤ɔ̃pɔ d̪ao
puruʂd̪er d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ d͡zemɔn̪ɔ l̪ɔোb̤ɔn̪ie̯ mel̪ae̯ d̪rut̪ he̯ɔ
l̪ɔোb̤ɔn̪ie̯ ort̪ʰe er d͡ʑ̤ul̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ ɕikɔɽɔɡul̪i s̪ɔn̪d̪̤an̪ kɔre
n̪it͡ɕer mati s̪ekʰan̪e d̪̤ɔre rakʰt̪e s̪ahad͡zd͡zɔ kɔre
puruʂd̪er ei d͡ʑɔɡɔt̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze kad͡ʑɡul̪i d͡zemɔn̪ɔ he̯et͡ɕʰil̪
abar kɔkʰɔn̪o ɕɔkt̪ɔ bɔn̪d̪̤ɔn̪ɔ d̪bara t̪ad̪er abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ
apn̪i d͡zɔd̪i ɡat͡ɕʰer ɕikʂa b̤al̪b̤abe d͡ʑan̪t̪en̪
er akɽit̪i ki bɔl̪e ebɔŋ kɔোt̪ʰa t̪ʰeke eti s̪priŋ ebɔŋ t̪arɔpɔrɔ
kib̤abe eti ɕeʂ hɔt̪e hɔbe ebɔŋ er s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ mɔn̪d̪ɔ
d̪̤aral̪ো bit͡ɕt͡ɕʰin̪n̪ɔt̪ar kutʰar t̪umi t͡ɕaibe
ebɔŋ ãkəɽe t̪ʰaka s̪aper ɕikɔɽɔɡul̪ike t͡ɕʰĩɽe ɸel̪un̪ ebɔŋ ɕue̯e pɔɽun̪
in̪d̪rie̯d͡ʑibɔn̪er ei oɕbɔt̪t̪ʰɔ n̪imn̪ɔ s̪et kɔra
s̪ei s̪ukʰer akaɕe n̪ɔt̪un̪ prɔbɽid̪d̪̤i
d͡zɔ̃ra pɔৌ̃t͡ʃʰaj t̪ad̪er mɔrar kɔোn̪ɔো d̪in̪ n̪ei
ml̪an̪o n̪a pɔɽeo n̪at̪ar kat͡ɕʰe man̪e
pit̪a ebɔŋ prɔt̪ʰɔmɔ ke rɔhɔs̪d͡zɔ t̪ojri kɔret͡ɕʰe
purat̪ɔn̪ɔ s̪ɽiʂtir karɔnɔ t̪ara t̪ɔ̃rɔ kat͡ɕʰe as̪e
abeɡ ebɔŋ s̪bɔpn̪ɔ t̪ʰeke d͡zara d̪ure b̤eŋɡe
d͡zara bɔn̪d̪̤ɔn̪ɔ bit͡ɕt͡ɕʰin̪n̪ɔ kɔre t̪ad̪er maŋs̪e abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ kɔre
ebɔŋt̪ɔ̃ke s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ s̪ɔrbɔd̪a upas̪n̪a kɔre
ki haoe̯ar d̪e̯ae̯ ar baɽe n̪a
ɡɔriʂmer an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ ̤ɡ̤umɔn̪t̪ɔ ɡat͡ɕʰke al̪োɽit̪ kɔre
d͡ʑ̤ɔɽer ki bis̪ɸɔোrɔnɔ t̪ad̪er kẽde ɸel̪e dal̪pal̪a o kan̪dɔ
t͡ɕirɔn̪t̪ɔn̪ɔ d͡ʑɔɡɔt̪er kat͡ɕʰe eirɔkɔmɔ pas̪
s̪ekʰan̪e arekti s̪urd͡zɔ d͡ʑbɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰe arekti t͡ɕɔ̃d̪ɔ
arekti al̪ো s̪ɔn̪d̪̤d͡za n̪e̯ɔ b̤ɔোrɔ n̪e̯ɔ d̪upuro n̪e̯ɔ
d͡za ekbar d̪ekʰe t̪ara ar ɸire as̪e n̪a
t̪ara amar biɕram d͡ʑibn̪er pɔrɔmɔ bɔrɔ ord͡ʑɔn̪ɔ kɔret͡ɕʰe
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ ei ud̪b̤as̪it̪ d͡ʑibn̪er pɽit̪ʰibit̪e
obin̪ɔɕbɔrɔ at̪ma amar kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke ut̪t̪ʰapit̪
rup n̪ee̯ n̪id͡ʑer kat͡ɕʰe tan̪e
bie̯iŋ er b̤andar t̪ʰeke d͡zat̪e s̪ɔbɔ at͡ɕʰe
in̪d̪rie̯ o bud̪d̪̤i। s̪arbɔb̤ɔৌmɔ at̪ma
eib̤abe maŋs̪e prɔbeɕ kɔra ba eti t̪d͡zaɡ kɔra
eɡul̪ike d͡ʑɔɽɔো kɔre d͡zemɔn̪ɔ bat̪as̪ ɡɔn̪d̪̤ɔ s̪ɔŋɡɔrɔhɔ kɔre
ɸul̪ɔɕɔd͡zd͡za upre ɸũ kan̪ ebɔŋ t͡ɕɔোkʰɔ
ebɔŋ s̪pɔrɕɔ ebɔŋ s̪bad̪ ebɔŋ ɡɔn̪d̪̤ɔ eɡul̪ো l̪aɡe
hd͡zɔ̃ ebɔŋ ekti s̪ɔŋbed̪ɔn̪ɔɕil̪ mɔn̪ɔn̪id͡ʑeke s̪ɔŋd͡zukt̪ɔ kɔra
s̪en̪s̪ɔd͡ʑin̪is̪ t̪ai
od͡ʑnat̪d̪er
s̪ei at̪ma d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ d͡zae̯ ba as̪e t̪ɔkʰɔn̪ɔ t̪ake t͡ɕihn̪it̪ kɔrɔো n̪a
kiŋba d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ s̪e rup n̪ie̯e an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ pae̯
ɡunabl̪ir s̪at̪ʰe s̪ɔŋd͡zukt̪ɔ kin̪t̪u d͡zara s̪ɔrɔl̪ɔ d̪ekʰt̪e
d͡zad̪er d̪ekʰar t͡ɕɔোkʰɔ at͡ɕʰe। pɔbit̪rɔ at̪ma d̪ekʰun̪
d͡za s̪ed̪ike s̪ɔt͡ɕeʂtɔ। al̪োkit̪ t̪ara upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤i kɔre
n̪id͡ʑed̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze s̪ei at̪ma kin̪t̪u bɔোkara
d͡zɔd̪io t̪ara t͡ɕeʂta kɔre t̪ara bud͡ʑ̤t̪e pare n̪a hɽid̪e̯ɔ at͡ɕʰe
n̪irl̪ipt̪ɔ od͡ʑnat̪
amar kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰekeo d͡ʑen̪e n̪in̪
s̪urd͡zer s̪ɔŋɡɽihit̪ mɔhimake ud͡ʑd͡ʑbɔl̪ɔ kɔre
d͡za s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ biɕbɔke al̪োkit̪ kɔre amar kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke t͡ɕɔ̃d̪ɔ
rupal̪i ãkun ebɔŋ aɡun̪ uɡɔrɔ premme̯ɔt̪a
ami kad̪amati b̤ed̪ kɔri ebɔŋ s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ akar d̪̤ar d̪ii
t̪ad̪er d͡ʑibɔn̪t̪ɔ ɕɔkt̪i ami ɡat͡ɕʰe t͡ɕɔɽe d͡zai
mul̪ pat̪a ebɔŋ prɔs̪ɸutit̪ bɔn̪ɔb̤umike s̪ɔbud͡ʑ kɔrɔt̪e
s̪ɔŋɡe bɔs̪ɔn̪t̪er rɔs̪ɔ। ot̪d͡zabɔɕd͡zɔkɔ uʂnɔt̪a he̯e utʰt͡ɕʰe
ami an̪ɔn̪d̪e d͡ʑbɔl̪e utʰi ɕbas̪ɔprɔɕbas̪er ɸremɡul̪i ebɔŋ pas̪ kɔri
bahd͡zik ebɔŋ ob̤d͡zɔn̪t̪ɔrin ɕbas̪ s̪ɔhɔ kʰaoe̯an̪োrɔ d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ maŋs̪ɔ d̪bara ɕɔrir।#
ei pɽit̪ʰibit̪e d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
s̪ɔt̪t̪a d̪biɡun bib̤ɔkt̪ɔ ek
obib̤ɔkt̪ɔ ek s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪ d͡ze bas̪
bib̤ɔkt̪ɔ। d͡za al̪ad̪a kɔre bɔs̪e
obib̤ɔkt̪ɔ।
t̪in̪i ekʰn̪o ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪ɔrɔ
s̪ɔrbɔোt̪t̪ɔmɔ s̪ɔkɔl̪ɔke d̪̤arɔnɔ kɔre d͡zɔ̃rɔ n̪am prɔb̤u
t͡ɕirɔn̪t̪ɔn̪ɔ s̪arbɔb̤ɔৌmɔ prɔt̪ʰɔmɔ d͡zin̪i s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ biɕbɔke purnɔ kɔren̪
t̪ad̪er tikie̯e rakʰa। ebɔŋ eib̤abe pɔrɔl̪ɔোkɔ bɔs̪ɔbas̪
bib̤ɔkt̪ɔ s̪ɔt̪t̪a ebɔŋ obib̤ɔkt̪ɔ 
amake bɔl̪a he̯ɔ puruʂ o bed̪ d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ
puruʂোt̪t̪ɔmɔ।
ke amake eb̤abe t͡ɕen̪e
me̤ɡ̤ɔhin̪ mɔn̪ɔ n̪ie̯e s̪ɔbɔ d͡ʑan̪e prie̯ rad͡ʑkumar
ebɔŋ t̪ar s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ at̪ma d̪ie̯e s̪ɔrbɔd̪a amar upas̪n̪a kɔre।
ekʰɔn̪ɔ pɔbit̪rɔ ɡɔোpɔn̪ɔ rɔhɔs̪d͡zɔ
t̪ɔোmar kat͡ɕʰe ̤ɡ̤ɔোʂɔna ke eta bud͡ʑ̤t̪e pare
bud̪d̪̤i at͡ɕʰe s̪e t̪ɔো an̪ɔn̪d̪e kad͡ʑ t͡ɕʰaɽt͡ɕʰe
ekʰan̪e od̪̤d͡zae̯ ɕeʂ he̯ɔ। b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar
ɕirোn̪am puruʂোt̪t̪ɔmɔprɔt̪id͡zোɡɔ
ot̪ʰba pɔrɔmɔke l̪ab̤ kɔre d̪̤ɔrmɔ ɡɔrɔn̪t̪ʰɔ।




ʂɔোɽɔɕɔ od̪̤d͡zae̯
kɽiʂnɔ।
n̪irb̤ikt̪a at̪mar ekɔkɔt̪a it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa
s̪ɔrbɔd̪a d͡ʑnan̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ prɔt͡ɕeʂta kɔra kʰɔোl̪a hat̪
ebɔŋ kʂud̪̤a n̪ie̯ɔn̪t̪rit̪ ebɔŋ t̪akoe̯a
ebɔŋ ekaki pɔɽaɕun̪a prem n̪ɔmrɔt̪a
n̪d͡zae̯ɔpɔrae̯ɔnɔt̪a kɔোn̪ɔ kit͡ɕʰuke a̤ɡ̤at̪ kɔrar d̪ike mɔn̪ɔোd͡zɔোɡɔ d̪in̪ d͡za bẽt͡ʃe t̪ʰake
s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔbad̪it̪a krɔোd̪̤er prɔt̪i mɔn̪t̪ʰɔrɔt̪a ekti mɔn̪ɔ
d͡ze hal̪kab̤abe on̪d͡zɔd̪er ki purɔs̪kar d͡zet̪e 
ebɔŋ s̪ɔmɔt̪a ebɔŋ d̪at̪ɔbd͡zɔ
d͡za kɔোn̪ɔ man̪uʂer d̪ɔোʂɔ d̪ekʰe n̪a ebɔŋ kɔোmɔl̪ɔt̪a
d͡ze s̪ɔbɔ kɔʂter d̪ike t̪ɽipt̪ɔ hɽid̪e̯ɔ
kɔোn̪ɔ it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa d̪bara ekti b̤arɔbɔhɔn̪ɔ hal̪ka
bin̪e̯i ebɔŋ kɔbɔrɔ puruʂɔt̪ber s̪at̪ʰe ab̤id͡ʑat̪d͡zɔ miɕrit̪
d̪̤ojrd͡zɔ ​​d̪ɽiɽ̤t̪a ebɔŋ biɕud̪d̪̤ɔt̪ar s̪at̪ʰe
ekti prɔt̪iɕোd̪̤ɔhin̪ at̪ma d̪eoe̯a he̯ɔ n̪a
n̪id͡ʑeke kʰub beɕi ret kɔrad͡zemɔn̪ɔ l̪ɔkʂɔnɔɡul̪i
he b̤art̪ie̯ d͡zubrad͡ʑ d͡zar pa s̪t̪ʰapɔn̪ɔ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe t̪ar
s̪ei n̪d͡zad͡zd͡zɔ pɔt̪ʰe d͡za n̪ie̯e d͡zae̯ s̪bɔrɡie̯ d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ
prɔt̪arna ohɔŋkar ebɔŋ ohɔŋkar
krɔোd̪̤er d̪rut̪t̪a kɔtʰɔোrɔ ebɔŋ mɔn̪d̪ɔ kɔt̪ʰabart̪a
ebɔŋ od͡ʑnɔt̪a t̪ar n̪id͡ʑer on̪d̪̤ɔkare on̪d̪̤ɔ
ei l̪ɔkʂɔnɔ amar rad͡ʑkumar d͡zar d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ t̪ar
n̪iʂtʰur ont͡ɕɔl̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ b̤aɡɔd͡zɔ।#
s̪bɔrɡie̯ d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ mukt̪i en̪e d̪ee̯
t̪ai apn̪ar d͡ʑan̪a ut͡ɕit̪ os̪urd̪er s̪at̪ʰe d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ
bɔn̪d̪̤ɔn̪e n̪ie̯e as̪e। t̪umi an̪ɔn̪d̪it̪ ho rad͡ʑkumar
s̪bɔrɡie̯ d͡ʑɔn̪mer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ d͡zar l̪ɔtɔ al̪ad̪a kɔra at͡ɕʰe।
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑibit̪ puruʂer upɔrɔ d̪uti s̪td͡zampɔ t͡ɕihn̪it̪ kɔra at͡ɕʰe
dib̤ain̪ ebɔŋ odib̤ain̪ ami t̪ɔোmar s̪at̪ʰe kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪et͡ɕʰi
ki t͡ɕihn̪ɔ d̪bara apn̪i s̪bɔrɡie̯ man̪uʂ t͡ɕin̪t̪e hɔbe
amar kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke ekʰɔn̪ɔ os̪bɔrɡie̯ ɕun̪un̪
t̪ara bɔোd͡ʑ̤e n̪a os̪bɔrɡie̯
kib̤abe at̪ma amar t̪ʰeke berie̯e d͡zae̯ n̪a t̪ara kib̤abe as̪e
amar kat͡ɕʰe ɸire d͡zan̪ eɡul̪ir mɔd̪̤d͡ze s̪ɔt̪d͡zo n̪ei
n̪a biɕud̪d̪̤ɔt̪a n̪a d͡ʑibn̪er n̪ie̯ɔmɔ। ei pɽit̪ʰibi
kɔোn̪ɔ ain̪ n̪ei ad̪eɕ n̪ei prɔb̤u n̪ei
t̪ai t̪ara bɔl̪e karne utʰen̪i
karɔnɔ on̪us̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔre n̪ikʰũtə ud̪d̪eɕd͡ze
kin̪t̪u t̪a ar keu n̪e̯ɔ l̪al̪s̪ar ̤ɡ̤ɔrɔ।
ebɔŋ ei d͡ʑin̪is̪ti t͡ɕin̪t̪a kɔre s̪ei s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d̪̤bɔŋs̪ɔprapt̪ɔra
s̪aman̪d͡zɔ bud̪d̪̤i on̪d̪̤ɔkarɔmɔn̪ern̪id͡ʑed̪er d̪in̪
kʰarap kad͡ʑer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ t̪ad̪er d̪̤ɔrɔn̪er ob̤iɕap
ot̪ɽipt̪ɔ kamn̪ar kat͡ɕʰe at̪mɔs̪ɔmɔrpɔnɔ
prɔt̪arna murkʰɔt̪a ebɔŋ ohɔŋkare pɔripurnɔ
on̪d̪̤ɔt̪be t̪ad̪er b̤ul̪er kat͡ɕʰe d̪̤ɔra pɔɽe d͡zae̯
pappurnɔ pɔt̪ʰe t̪ara ei mit̪ʰd͡za biɕbas̪ kɔre
d͡zemɔn̪ɔti s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ t͡ɕʰil̪ei mit̪ʰd͡za d͡za mɽit̪d͡zur d̪ike n̪ie̯e d͡zae̯
an̪ɔn̪d̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze kʰũd͡ʒe paoe̯a s̪ɔbɔ b̤al̪ো d͡za
ebɔŋ kɔ̃d̪ɔt͡ɕʰe ekʰan̪ei ɕeʂ
ɸɔ̃d̪e ɸel̪a
ɕɔt̪ɔ ol̪ɔs̪ɔ aɕar ɸɔ̃d̪e
krit̪d̪as̪ t̪ad̪er abeɡ ebɔŋ t̪ad̪er krɔোd̪̤ɔ t̪ara kin̪t̪e
bes̪ did s̪ɔhɔ s̪ɔmpɔd̪ɔ ɡɔrɔmɔ kʂud̪̤a atʰa
eb̤abe ad͡ʑker d̪in̪e t̪ara bɔl̪e amra l̪ab̤ kɔret͡ɕʰi
hɽid̪e̯er omuk it͡ɕt͡ɕʰa purɔnɔ hɔbe
ebɔŋ ei amad̪er ebɔŋ on̪d͡zɔ amad̪er hɔbe
ad͡ʑ amra ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ ɕɔt̪ruke hɔt̪d͡za kɔret͡ɕʰi ebɔŋ amra hɔt̪d͡za kɔrɔbɔ
aɡamikal̪ amad̪er opɔrɔ ɕɔt̪ru d̪ekʰো
amra ki prɔb̤u n̪i amra b̤al̪b̤abe ul̪l̪as̪ n̪a
amad̪er b̤aɡɔd͡zɔ bikʰd͡zat̪ s̪ahɔs̪i ebɔŋ mɔhan̪ n̪e̯ɔ
d̪̤ɔn̪i amra ɡɔrber s̪at̪ʰe d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ ki on̪d͡zɔ puruʂd̪er
amad̪er mɔt̪ɔ bɔ̃t͡ɕɔbe t̪ahɔl̪e kurban̪ir d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ hɔt̪d͡za
bɔɽɔ ho ebɔŋ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ kɔrɔ t̪ai t̪ara kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪e
od͡ʑnɔt̪a d̪bara on̪d̪̤ɔkarat͡ɕt͡ɕʰɔn̪n̪ɔ ebɔŋ t̪ai t̪ara pɔɽe
prɔd͡ʑekter s̪at̪ʰe t͡ɕʰute d͡zaoe̯a prɔt̪arit̪ ebɔŋ abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ
kal̪ো b̤rɔmer d͡ʑal̪e l̪al̪s̪ae̯ harie̯e d͡zae̯
daun̪ tu ɸaul̪ n̪arka। ob̤iman̪i on̪uraɡi
ekɡũje ebɔŋ ɡɔrbit̪ mɔd̪er s̪at̪ʰe mɽit̪mat̪al̪
s̪ɔmpɔd̪ɔ ebɔŋ bepɔrɔোe̯a t̪ad̪er s̪ɔbɔ or̤ɡ̤ɔ
at͡ɕʰe kin̪t̪u ɕrɔd̪d̪̤a prɔd̪ɔrɕɔn̪ɔ kɔra hɔt͡ɕt͡ɕʰe n̪a
prat͡ɕin̪ biɕbas̪er d̪̤armikt̪ae̯। eb̤abe ɕɔpɔt̪ʰɔ kɔrɔl̪en̪
at̪mɔhud bɔl̪ɔpre̯ɔোɡɔ owd̪d̪̤ɔt̪d͡zɔ b̤ɔোd͡ʑɔ krɔোd̪̤ɔ
ei amar n̪in̪d̪akarira t̪ara d͡ze rupe pɔrid̪̤an̪ kɔre
ebɔŋ t̪ara d͡ze akare bɔŋɕɔbɽid̪d̪̤i kɔre amar ɕɔt̪rura
bid̪beʂpurnɔ ebɔŋ ̤ɡ̤ɽina n̪iʂtʰur mɔn̪d̪ɔ d͡ʑɔ̤ɡ̤ɔn̪d͡zɔ
s̪ɔrbɔn̪imn̪ɔ ebɔŋ s̪ɔrbɔn̪imn̪ɔ puruʂ d͡zad̪er ami n̪ikʂep kɔri
abar ebɔŋ abaro d͡ʑibn̪er ɕeʂe
kɔোn̪ɔ ɕe̯ɔt̪an̪i ɡɔrb̤e d͡zekʰan̪ t̪ʰeke d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ d͡ʑɔn̪me
ɕe̯ɔt̪an̪ ɡɔrb̤ɔ t̪ad̪er pun̪rae̯ d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ d̪ee̯ s̪ɔbai prɔt̪arit̪ he̯ɔ
ebɔŋ d͡zɔt̪ɔkʂɔnɔ n̪a t̪ara amake kʰũd͡ʒe pae̯ ebɔŋ upas̪n̪a kɔre miʂti rad͡ʑkumar
t̪ara d͡ze n̪ed̪ar rɔোdɔ pɔd̪ɔd̪ɔl̪it̪
d͡ʑahan̪n̪amer d̪ɔrɔd͡ʑa
t̪riɡun he̯ɔ d͡zar d̪bara puruʂd̪er s̪ɔrbɔn̪aɕ kɔra d͡zae̯
l̪al̪s̪ar d̪ɔrɔd͡ʑa krɔোd̪̤er d̪ɔrɔd͡ʑa d̪ɔrɔd͡ʑa
 er ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ man̪uʂ ei t̪in̪ti eɽie̯e d͡zak
d͡ze prɔbeɕ kɔra t̪ʰeke mukʰ ɸirie̯e n̪ebe
n̪ɔrɔker oi t̪in̪ti d̪ɔrɔd͡ʑai s̪ɔোd͡ʑa he̯e ɡet͡ɕʰe
t̪ar ɕan̪t̪i kʰũd͡ʒəte ebɔŋ s̪bɔrɡer d̪ɔrɔd͡ʑae̯ as̪e।

ekʰan̪e od̪̤d͡zae̯ ɕeʂ kɔrun̪। b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar
ɕirোn̪am d̪ojbs̪arɔs̪ɔৌpɔd̪bib̤aɡɔd͡zɔোɡɔ
ot̪ʰba d̪d͡zɔ buk oɸ d̪d͡zɔ s̪eparetes̪ oɸ d̪d͡zɔ dib̤ain̪ o্d͡zan̪dɔ dib̤ain̪।




od̪̤d͡zae̯ 
ord͡ʑun̪।
d͡zɔd̪i puruʂra pɔbit̪rɔ od̪̤d͡zad̪eɕ t̪d͡zaɡ kɔre
ɕas̪t̪rer omɔn̪ɔোd͡zɔোɡi t̪ɔbuo on̪t̪ɔre biɕbas̪ rakʰun̪
ar pud͡ʑa kɔrɔ ki obɔs̪t̪ʰa hɔbe t̪ad̪er
mɔhan̪ kɽiʂnɔ s̪ɔt̪t̪ban̪ rɔd͡ʑɔs̪ɔ t̪ɔmɔs̪ɔ bɔl̪e
kɽiʂnɔ।
t̪in̪ɡun biɕbas̪ man̪ɔbɔd͡ʑat̪i ebɔŋ s̪priŋs̪ɔ
ei t̪in̪ti ɡun t̪ʰeke s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ hoe̯a
ot̪ʰba abeɡd̪aɡ ba on̪d̪̤ɔkar d͡zemɔn̪ɔ apn̪i ɕun̪t̪e paben̪
prɔt̪iti mumin̪er biɕbas̪ b̤art̪ie̯ d͡zubrad͡ʑ
s̪e as̪l̪e d͡za t̪ar s̪at̪ʰe n̪id͡ʑeke man̪ie̯e n̪ee̯।
d͡zekʰan̪e apn̪i ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ upas̪ɔkɔke d̪ekʰt̪e paben̪
s̪e d͡zake upas̪n̪a kɔre d͡ʑibɔn̪ɔke at̪t̪ikɔrɔnɔ kɔre
d͡zemɔn̪ɔ mad͡ʑar t̪ai b̤ɔোtari
prɔɕan̪t̪ɔ at̪ma s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ d̪ebt̪ad̪er pud͡ʑa kɔre at̪ma
rad͡ʑd̪er an̪uɡɔt̪d͡zɔ kɔra rakʂɔs̪ɔ upas̪n̪a#
ba d͡zɔkʂɔ ebɔŋ on̪d̪̤ɔkar man̪uʂ prart̪ʰɔn̪a
pret̪as̪ ebɔŋ b̤utas̪er kat͡ɕʰe।# hd͡zɔ̃ ebɔŋ d͡zara
d͡zara t̪ikt̪ɔ t̪ɔpɔs̪d͡zar on̪uɕil̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔre ad̪eɕkɽit̪ n̪e̯ɔ
d͡zɔt̪ʰart̪ʰɔ n̪ie̯ɔmɔ d̪bara t̪ɔpɔs̪d͡za d͡zar mul̪ at͡ɕʰe
s̪be̯ɔŋs̪ɔmpurnɔ ɡɔrbit̪ kɔpɔtɔt̪ae̯
s̪ei man̪uʂɡul̪ো abeɡe at͡ɕt͡ɕʰɔn̪n̪ɔ hiŋs̪rɔ bɔn̪d͡zɔ
ot̪d͡zat͡ɕarbud̪d̪̤ihin̪raamar upad̪an̪
t̪ad̪er d̪eher mɔd̪̤d͡ze n̪d͡zad͡zd͡zɔ s̪ɔŋs̪t̪ʰae̯ bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ kɔrun̪
n̪a ami n̪id͡ʑei maŋs̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze upɔs̪t̪ʰit̪
t̪ad̪er t͡ɕen̪en̪ ɕe̯ɔt̪an̪er kat͡ɕʰe s̪bɔrɡer kat͡ɕʰe n̪e̯ɔ
karɔnɔ kʰabar d͡zemɔn̪ɔ man̪ɔbɔd͡ʑat̪ir d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ t̪in̪ɡun
puʂtit̪e t̪ai t̪riɡun upae̯ at͡ɕʰe
ibad̪ɔt̪ɔ bɔrd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ d̪an̪
amar ei kɔt̪ʰa ɕun̪un̪ ekti kʰabar at͡ɕʰe d͡za n̪ie̯e as̪e
ɕɔkt̪i pɔd̪art̪ʰɔ ɕɔkt̪i ebɔŋ s̪bas̪t̪ʰd͡zɔ ebɔŋ bẽt͡ʃe t̪ʰakar an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ
b̤al̪ paka s̪ɔৌhard̪d͡zɔpurnɔ s̪an̪t̪bɔn̪ad̪ae̯ɔkɔ hoe̯a
s̪ut̪ʰɸas̪tɔ maŋs̪ɔ। ebɔŋ an̪a d͡za kʰabar at͡ɕʰe
bd͡zɔt̪ʰa ebɔŋ oɕan̪t̪i ebɔŋ d͡ʑbɔl̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ rɔkt̪ɔ ​​ebɔŋ ɕɔোkɔ
kʰub kamɽan̪ো ɡɔrɔmɔ kɔra l̪ɔbɔnɔ ebɔŋ d̪̤aral̪ো hoe̯a
ebɔŋ t̪ai kʰub ɕɔkt̪iɕal̪i kʂud̪̤a d̪bara 
ebɔŋ s̪ekʰan̪e n̪ɔোŋra kʰabarrat̪arat̪i rakʰa he̯ɔ#
s̪bad̪ɔhin̪ n̪ɔোŋra d͡za n̪ɔোŋra kʰabe
pɔt͡ɕa ekti pɔrɔbɔ tʰɔো̃tə d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ d̪ekʰa
d͡zemɔn̪ɔ premer on̪d̪̤ɔkar।
t̪ai at͡ɕarer s̪at̪ʰe 
ekti t̪d͡zaɡ purɔs̪karer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ n̪e̯ɔ
n̪d͡zad͡zd͡zɔ bud̪d̪̤it̪e d̪eoe̯a d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ s̪e man̪ɔt̪ɔ kɔre
b̤ɔkt̪ib̤re hɽid̪e̯ɔ d̪ie̯e bɔl̪e eta amar kɔra ut͡ɕit̪
eti s̪ut̪ɸas̪tɔ at͡ɕar। kin̪t̪u l̪ab̤er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ bɔl̪id̪an̪
b̤al̪ kʰd͡zat̪ir d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ prɔs̪t̪abit̪ n̪iɕt͡ɕit̪ hɔn̪ɔ d͡ze eti
he b̤arɔt̪ɔbas̪ir ɕreʂtʰɔ rad͡ʑs̪at͡ɕar
abeɡ s̪td͡zampɔ s̪ɔhɔ। ebɔŋ ekti bɔl̪id̪an̪
ain̪er birud̪d̪̤e oɸar kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe kɔোn̪ɔো prapd͡zɔt̪a t͡ɕʰaɽai
on̪n̪ɔd̪an̪er kɔোn̪ɔ s̪ɔŋɡi t͡ɕʰaɽa
pɔbit̪rɔ s̪t̪ɔোt̪rer n̪a purোhit̪d̪er kat͡ɕʰe bɔɽɔ
obiɕbas̪i ud̪d͡zapɔn̪e eke d͡ʑɔ̤ɡ̤ɔn̪d͡zɔ bɔl̪un̪
on̪d̪̤ɔkarer kad͡ʑti harie̯e ɡet͡ɕʰe
d̪ebt̪ad̪er pud͡ʑa
med̪̤apud͡ʑa n̪imn̪ɔ ɕrɔd̪d̪̤a
d̪uibar d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ n̪eoe̯a ɕikʂɔkɔ prɔbind̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze biɕud̪d̪̤ɔt̪a
d͡zɔt̪ʰart̪ʰɔt̪a ebɔŋ brɔhmɔt͡ɕɔrd͡zer brɔt̪ɔ
ar kɔোn̪ɔো os̪ɔhae̯ d͡ʑin̪is̪ke a̤ɡ̤at̪ n̪a kɔra
eɡul̪i ain̪er prɔkɽit̪ d̪̤ɔrmie̯t̪a t̪ojri kɔre।
ɕɔbd̪ɔ kɔোn̪ɔ man̪uʂer d̪uঃkʰer karɔnɔ he̯ɔ n̪a ɕɔbd̪ɔ kɔkʰɔn̪o s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ
mɽid̪u ebɔŋ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔd̪ae̯ɔkɔ ɕɔbd̪ɔ ebɔŋ apn̪i d͡za bɔl̪en̪
ekti pɔbit̪rɔ l̪ekʰar biɽbiɽ patʰe
eɡul̪ো bɔkt̪ɽit̪ar prɔkɽit̪ d̪̤ɔrmie̯t̪a t̪ojri kɔre।
at̪mar prɔɕan̪t̪i s̪ɔৌmd͡zɔt̪a
n̪irɔbɔ at̪mar d̪ɔোl̪a d̪̤rubɔkɔ t͡ɕap
prɔkɽit̪ike pɔbit̪rɔ kɔrar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ei d͡ʑin̪is̪ɡul̪i t̪ojri kɔre
b̤al̪ at͡ɕar ebɔŋ mɔn̪er prɔkɽit̪ d̪̤ɔrmie̯t̪a
ei d̪̤ɔrɔn̪er t̪riɡun biɕbas̪ s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ d̪̤armikt̪ae̯
rɔkʂit̪ l̪ab̤er kɔোn̪ɔ aɕa t͡ɕʰaɽa b̤ɔkt̪i kɔre
s̪ɔt̪t̪ban̪er n̪ikʰũtə kad͡ʑ s̪ɔt̪d͡zikarer biɕbas̪।
ɡɔrbit̪ prɔd̪ɔrɕɔn̪er ob̤in̪e̯e d̪ekʰan̪ো d̪̤ɔrmɔ
b̤al̪ো bin̪োd̪ɔn̪ɔ pud͡ʑa kʰd͡zat̪i d͡ʑe̯ɔ kɔrɔt̪e
eirɔkɔmɔ bɔl̪un̪ ami rad͡ʑɔs̪ɔ ɸus̪kuɽi ebɔŋ bɽit̪ʰa।
bud̪d̪̤ihin̪ it͡ɕt͡ɕʰar on̪us̪ɔrɔne d̪̤ɔrmɔ
n̪id͡ʑeke n̪ird͡zat̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔrɔt̪e ba a̤ɡ̤at̪ kɔrar kʂɔmɔt̪ae̯ as̪a
arekti t̪ɔmɔs̪er t̪is̪ on̪d̪̤ɔkar ebɔŋ os̪us̪t̪ʰɔ।
b̤al̪োbas̪a d̪ie̯e d̪eoe̯a upɔhar d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ keu bɔl̪ɔbe
ekʰɔn̪ɔ ami an̪ɔn̪d̪er s̪at̪ʰe d̪it̪e hɔbe d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ s̪e n̪ee̯
kit͡ɕʰui ɸerɔt̪ɔ d̪it̪e pare n̪a d͡zɔt̪ʰas̪t̪ʰan̪e t̪ojri
n̪ird̪̤arit̪ s̪ɔme̯ɔ ebɔŋ ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ prapker s̪at̪ʰe d̪ekʰa kɔrɔt̪e
s̪ɔt̪t̪ban̪er d̪an̪ n̪d͡zad͡zd͡zɔ ebɔŋ l̪ab̤ɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ।
s̪bart̪ʰɔkɔb̤abe d̪eoe̯a upɔhar kɔোt̪ʰae̯ pab
abar aɕa kɔra he̯ɔ ot̪ʰba d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ kit͡ɕʰu ɕeʂ t͡ɕaoe̯a he̯ɔ
ot̪ʰba d͡zekʰan̪e upɔharti kʂɔোb̤er s̪at̪ʰe d̪eoe̯a he̯ɔ
iha rad͡ʑs̪er abeɡe d̪aɡ os̪us̪t̪ʰɔ।
upɔharti mɔn̪d̪ɔ s̪ɔme̯e t͡ɕʰute d͡zae̯
b̤ul̪ d͡ʑae̯ɡae̯ bes̪ prapker kat͡ɕʰe
obɔd͡ʑna ba kɔtʰɔোrɔ n̪ird̪e̯ɔt̪ae̯ t̪ojri
t̪ams̪er d̪an̪ on̪d̪̤ɔkar eta aɕirbad̪ kɔre n̪a#
ekʰan̪e od̪̤d͡zae̯ ɕeʂ kɔrun̪। b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar
ɕirোn̪am ɕrɔd̪d̪̤at̪re̯ɔbib̤aɡɔd͡zɔোɡɔ
ot̪ʰba d̪̤ɔrmer bi t̪in̪ɡun d̪̤ɔrɔner biɕbas̪er d̪bara।




od̪̤d͡zae̯ 
ord͡ʑun̪।
kʂin ami aro b̤al̪b̤abe d͡ʑan̪t̪e pari apn̪i mɔhiman̪bit̪
ekebare s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔhɽid̪e̯er prɔb̤us̪ɔn̪n̪d͡zas̪er
birɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰaka ebɔŋ ut͡ɕt͡ɕarɔnɔ prɔb̤u
t̪d͡zaɡa ebɔŋ ki ei d̪uti pɽit̪ʰɔkɔ
kɽiʂnɔ।
kɔbira tʰiki s̪ei s̪ɔn̪n̪d͡zas̪ ɕikʂa d̪en̪
s̪ɔbɔ kad͡ʑ d͡za bɔs̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ purbɔোkt̪ɔ he̯ɔ
it͡ɕt͡ɕʰar baire ebɔŋ t̪ad̪er bud̪d̪̤iman̪ bɔl̪e
t̪d͡zaɡ kɔrmer ɸɔl̪ɔ pɔrit̪d͡zaɡ kɔrɔt͡ɕʰen̪।
d̪̤armikd̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze keu keu at͡ɕʰe
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ kɔrmɔ pap ebɔŋ pɔrit̪d͡zaɡ kɔra
ebɔŋ keu keu ut̪t̪ɔrɔ d̪ee̯ n̪a ut̪t̪ɔmɔ kad͡ʑ
upas̪n̪a t̪ɔpɔs̪d͡za b̤ikʂa his̪abe kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe
ekʰɔn̪ɔ amar bakd͡zɔ ɕɔোn̪ɔ b̤arɔt̪ɔbas̪ir ɕreʂtʰɔ
t̪ɔোmar ɕɔt̪rud̪er pɔɕt͡ɕad̪d̪̤abɔn̪ɔkari eta tʰik at͡ɕʰe
t̪d͡zaɡ t̪ribid̪̤ ruper
ebɔŋ upas̪n̪a t̪ɔpɔs̪d͡za b̤ikʂa t̪ʰakt̪e hɔbe n̪a
n̪a an̪ɔn̪d̪er s̪at̪ʰe kɔra ei t̪in̪ɔd͡ʑɔn̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
prɔkɽit̪ at̪mar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ d͡ʑɔl̪ɔ biɕud̪d̪̤ɔ he̯ɔ
t̪ɔbuo s̪ei ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔ kad͡ʑɡul̪োo on̪uɕil̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe
s̪ɔŋd͡zukt̪i ap ɸɔl̪ɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ s̪ɔbɔ ɸɔl̪ɔ
kad͡ʑ d̪bara ut̪pad̪it̪ ei amar bit͡ɕar rad͡ʑkumar
eta amar od̪ɔmd͡zɔ o s̪t̪ʰir hukum
s̪ɔtʰikb̤abe n̪ird̪̤arit̪ kad͡ʑ t̪ʰeke birɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰaka
kɔkʰɔn̪ɔো d̪ekʰa he̯ɔ n̪a t̪ai bɔs̪ɔn̪t̪ɔ t̪ʰeke birɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰaka
on̪d̪̤ɔkar t̪ʰeke ebɔŋ bib̤rɔmɔ eti ɕekʰae̯।
maŋs̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kɔtʰin̪ kad͡ʑ t̪ʰeke birɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰaka
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ keu bɔl̪e eti oprit̪ikɔrɔ ei ɕun̪d͡zɔ
ei d̪̤ɔrɔn̪er ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ abeɡ t̪ʰeke kad͡ʑ kɔre l̪ab̤er kit͡ɕʰui n̪ei
d͡ʑe̯ɔ t̪ar t̪d͡zaɡ kin̪t̪u ord͡ʑun̪
kad͡ʑer prɔt̪i as̪ɔkt̪i t̪ʰeke birɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰaka
kad͡ʑe purɔs̪kar t̪ʰeke birɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰaka
d͡zɔd̪io keu eti s̪ɔmpurnɔ biɕbɔs̪t̪ɔb̤abe kɔre
bɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰe eta kɔra tʰik d͡ze s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ kad͡ʑ
ar birɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰaka ke emɔn̪ɔ d̪ae̯it̪bɔ pal̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔre
t̪ar kad͡ʑ bd͡zɔrt̪ʰɔ hɔl̪e d͡zɔd̪i eti s̪ɔɸɔl̪ɔ he̯ɔ
oprɔs̪t̪ut̪ n̪id͡ʑer hɽid̪e̯e n̪d͡zae̯ɔs̪ɔŋɡɔt̪ɔ
bit̪ɔrkɔ o s̪ɔŋɕe̯ɔ t̪d͡zaɡ kɔrun̪ t̪ɔ̃rɔ s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ kad͡ʑ
karɔnɔ ɕɔrire t̪ʰaka obɔs̪t̪ʰae̯ keu d̪ɔ̃ɽat̪e pare n̪a
kad͡ʑ t̪ʰeke s̪ɔmpurnɔb̤abe d̪ure t̪ɔbuo d͡zara birɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰake
t̪ar aml̪er l̪ab̤ t̪ʰeke birɔt̪ɔ t̪ʰake।
ɕrɔmer ɸɔl̪ɔ aɡami d͡ʑibn̪e
s̪ɔbɔ puruʂer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ t̪in̪ɡun kamd͡zɔ
ebɔŋ obant͡ɕʰit̪ ebɔŋ ub̤e̯ɔ miɕrit̪
kin̪t̪u kɔোn̪ɔ ɸɔl̪i n̪ei d͡zekʰan̪e kɔোn̪ɔ kad͡ʑ t͡ɕʰil̪ n̪a।
amar kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke ɕɔোn̪ɔ d̪ir̤ɡ̤ɔ os̪t̪rɔd̪̤ari prɔb̤u t̪ojri pɔ̃t͡ɕɔ
d͡za s̪aŋkʰd͡ze ɕikʰie̯et͡ɕʰe prɔt̪iti kɔrme
pre̯ɔোd͡ʑɔn̪ie̯ his̪abe prɔt̪ʰɔme bɔl̪ɔ ebɔŋ t̪arɔpɔrɔ
prɔt̪in̪id̪̤i pɔrɔbɔrt̪i bib̤in̪n̪ɔ d͡zɔn̪t̪rɔ
t͡ɕɔt̪urt̪ʰɔt̪ɔ biɕeʂ prɔt͡ɕeʂta pɔnt͡ɕɔmɔ iɕbɔrɔ।
ki kad͡ʑ kɔোn̪ɔ n̪ɔɕbɔrɔ 
ɕɔrir mɔn̪ɔ ba kɔt̪ʰa mɔn̪d̪ɔ ba b̤al̪
ei pɔ̃t͡ɕɔti d̪bara t̪in̪i t̪a kɔren̪। d͡za eib̤abe hɔt͡ɕt͡ɕʰe
d͡ze d͡ʑnan̪er ob̤abe n̪id͡ʑeke d̪ekʰt̪e pae̯
ekmat̪rɔ ob̤in̪et̪a his̪abe kit͡ɕʰui d͡ʑan̪en̪ n̪a
ebɔŋ kit͡ɕʰui d̪ekʰt̪e n̪a ot̪eb ami bɔl̪i d͡zɔd̪i ek
n̪id͡ʑeke t̪ʰeke d̪ure rakʰa os̪t̪ʰir mɔn̪ɔ d̪ie̯e
mere ɸel̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ bid kɔra ul̪tɔো s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ hɔোs̪tɔke hɔt̪d͡za kɔra ut͡ɕit̪
t̪in̪i hɔt̪d͡za kɔren̪ n̪a t̪in̪i t̪at̪e abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ n̪ɔn̪ɔ
d͡ʑnan̪ d͡ze d͡ʑin̪is̪ d͡ʑan̪a ebɔŋ d͡ze mɔn̪ɔ d͡ʑan̪e
eɡul̪i kard͡zer t̪in̪ɡun s̪ut͡ɕn̪as̪t̪ʰɔl̪ɔ t̪ojri kɔre।
ob̤in̪e̯ɔ ob̤in̪et̪a ebɔŋ d͡zɔn̪t̪rɔ
eɡul̪i d̪ɔl̪il̪er mɔোtɔ t̪in̪ɡun kɔre।
kin̪t̪u d͡ʑnan̪ ed͡ʑen̪tɔ kad͡ʑ part̪ʰɔkd͡zɔ at͡ɕʰe
t̪in̪ti bib̤ad͡ʑɔn̪ɔ ɡunabl̪i d̪bara। ekʰɔn̪ɔ ɕun̪un̪
d͡za t̪ad̪er bib̤ad͡ʑɔn̪ɔ ɡunabl̪i hɔt̪e
s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ d͡ʑnan̪ at͡ɕʰe। d͡ʑan̪un̪ eti hɔl̪ɔ

opurnɔ d͡ʑnan̪ at͡ɕʰe d͡za d̪ekʰe
al̪ad̪a al̪ad̪a os̪t̪it̪bɔ

mit̪ʰd͡za d͡ʑnan̪ at͡ɕʰe d͡za on̪d̪̤ɔb̤abe ãkəɽe d̪̤ɔre

al̪ো t̪ʰeke bɔnt͡ɕit̪ s̪ɔŋkirnɔ ebɔŋ n̪is̪t̪ed͡ʑ ebɔŋ on̪d̪̤ɔkar।

s̪ɔŋd͡zukt̪i t͡ɕʰaɽa abeɡɔhin̪b̤abe t̪ojri kɔra he̯ɔ
kɔrt̪ɔbd͡zer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ premer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ n̪e̯ɔ ̤ɡ̤ɽinar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ n̪e̯ɔ l̪ab̤er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ n̪e̯ɔ।
n̪irɔrt̪ʰɔkɔ krie̯a at͡ɕʰe d͡za puruʂera on̪us̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔre
akaŋkʂa metan̪োrɔ d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ d͡zɔn̪t̪rɔnad̪ae̯ɔkɔ on̪upranit̪
n̪id͡ʑer on̪ub̤ut̪i d̪bara s̪ɔrbɔɕɔোʂɔkɔ t͡ɕap s̪ɔhɔ
eti rad͡ʑs̪abeɡpurnɔ ebɔŋ n̪irɔrt̪ʰɔkɔ।
on̪d̪̤ɔkar o্d͡zakɔɕɔn̪ɔ at͡ɕʰe d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ keu kit͡ɕʰu kɔre
s̪ɔmɔs̪d͡za s̪ɔmpɔrke ɡaɸel̪ a̤ɡ̤at̪er prɔt̪i ɡaɸil̪t̪i
ot̪ʰba on̪d͡zer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ on̪d͡zae̯ ɡaɸil̪t̪i d͡zɔd̪i s̪e kʂɔt̪i kɔre
t̪ar n̪id͡ʑer at̪mat̪ɔmɔs̪er t̪is̪ kal̪ো ar kʰarap

obit͡ɕɔl̪ɔ b̤al̪ ba mɔn̪d̪ɔ eki he̯ɔ

t̪ɔোmake d͡zud̪d̪̤e ud̪bud̪d̪̤ɔ kɔrɔbe। t̪umi d͡za eɽie̯e d͡zao
n̪d͡zad͡zd͡zɔ b̤rɔmɔ d̪bara bib̤ran̪t̪ɔ t̪umi kʰũd͡ʒəbe
t̪ɔোmar it͡ɕt͡ɕʰar birud̪d̪̤e d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ kad͡ʑ t̪ɔোmar kat͡ɕʰe as̪e
t̪ɔোmar prɔkɽit̪i s̪ete prɔmpɔtiŋ d͡ʑaɡie̯e t̪ɔোl̪a।
man̪uʂer on̪t̪ɔre ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ ɡuru t̪ʰaken̪
s̪ukʂmɔ tan̪ d̪ie̯e t̪ad̪er kad͡ʑ kɔre t̪ɔোl̪e s̪triŋ
t̪in̪i ki s̪ure n̪at͡ɕben̪। apn̪ar s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ at̪ma s̪ɔŋɡe
t̪ake biɕbas̪ kɔrun̪ ebɔŋ t̪ake apn̪ar s̪ɔhae̯t̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ n̪in̪ prin̪s̪ɔ
t̪aiɕud̪̤u t̪ai ord͡ʑun̪t̪umi ki l̪ab̤ kɔrɔbe
t̪ɔ̃rɔ kɽipae̯ pɔrɔmɔ biɕram
t͡ɕirɔn̪t̪ɔn̪ɔ s̪t̪ʰan̪
eib̤abe t̪ɔোmake kʰul̪e d̪eoe̯a he̯et͡ɕʰe
ei s̪ɔt̪d͡zer s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ arো l̪ukie̯e t̪ʰaka rɔhɔs̪d͡zɔ
kɔোn̪ɔো ɡɔোpɔn̪ɔ rɔhɔs̪d͡zer t͡ɕee̯e। d̪̤d͡zan̪
ebɔŋ apn̪i d͡zemɔn̪ɔ t͡ɕan̪ t̪arɔpɔrɔ kad͡ʑ
n̪a kin̪t̪u arো ekbar
amar ɕeʂ kɔt̪ʰata d̪̤ɔrɔ amar pɔrɔmɔ ort̪ʰɔ at͡ɕʰe
t̪umi amar kat͡ɕʰe mul̪d͡zɔban̪ tʰik b̤al̪ɔpree̯s̪i
ɕɔোn̪ɔ ami t̪ɔোmar s̪bat͡ɕt͡ɕʰɔn̪d̪d͡zer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ t̪ɔোmake bɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰi।
amake t̪ɔোmar hɽid̪e̯ɔ d̪ao amake ad̪ɔrɔ kɔrɔো amar s̪eba ãkəɽe t̪ʰaka
biɕbas̪ ebɔŋ b̤al̪bas̪a ebɔŋ amar prɔt̪i ɕrɔd̪d̪̤a
t̪ahɔl̪e ki t̪umi amar kat͡ɕʰe as̪be kɔt̪ʰa d̪il̪am s̪ɔt̪d͡zi
karɔnɔ t̪umi amar kat͡ɕʰe miʂti
ar s̪eɡul̪ো t͡ɕʰeɽe d̪ao
at͡ɕar o rit kɔrt̪ɔbd͡zɔ amar kat͡ɕʰe eka uɽe
amake apn̪ar ekɔkɔ aɕre̯ɔ kɔrun̪ ami mukt̪ɔ kɔrɔbɔ
apn̪ar at̪ma t̪ar s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ pap t̪ʰeke b̤al̪ kʰaoe̯ad̪aoe̯a kɔra
aɽal̪ pɔbit̪rɔ kɽiʂnɔ bɔl̪et͡ɕʰen̪
eta t̪ar kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke d͡zar biɕbas̪ n̪ei
d͡ze t̪ar upas̪n̪a kɔre n̪a ba t͡ɕae̯ n̪a
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ s̪e kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪e t̪ɔkʰɔn̪ɔ prɔd͡ʑnar ɕikʂa
d͡zara upɔhas̪ kɔre t̪ad̪er kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke eta l̪ukan̪
kin̪t̪u d͡zekʰan̪ei mad͡ʑ̤e pal̪er
amar premikd̪er ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ ɕekʰabe
ei d̪ibd͡zɔ d͡ʑnan̪i b̤aʂɔnɔ
biɕbas̪e ɕikʂa d̪it̪e hɔbe
t̪ad̪er kat͡ɕʰe s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ ebɔŋ prɔs̪t̪ab
amar kat͡ɕʰe s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ s̪ɔmman̪er
brɔhmar kat͡ɕʰe s̪e as̪e
n̪a ebɔŋ apn̪i kɔোt̪ʰao kʰũd͡ʒe paben̪ n̪a
s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ man̪ɔbɔd͡ʑat̪ir d͡ze kɔোn̪o man̪uʂ
amar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ s̪ɔbɔt͡ɕee̯e prie̯ kad͡ʑ kɔra
kiŋba kɔোn̪ɔ prie̯ɔt̪ɔmɔ hɔbe n̪a
amar pɽit̪ʰibit̪e। hd͡zɔ̃ t̪at͡ɕʰaɽa
d͡ze ei kɔt̪ʰɔোpɔkɔt̪ʰɔn̪ɔ patʰ kɔre
s̪ɔmɔb̤umit̪e amad̪er d̪bara od̪̤iʂtʰit̪
d̪̤armikb̤abe ebɔŋ ol̪ɔs̪ɔb̤abe t͡ɕin̪t̪a kɔra
t̪in̪i amake kurban̪i d̪ie̯et͡ɕʰen̪
kɽiʂnɔ ei d͡ʑnan̪i kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪ɔt͡ɕʰen̪
hd͡zɔ̃ ebɔŋ d͡zara biɕbas̪e purnɔ
eta d͡za bɔl̪e t̪a bid͡ʑnɔt̪ar s̪at̪ʰe ɕɔোn̪e
n̪ɔmrɔb̤abe ɕun̪e d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ s̪e mara d͡zae̯
n̪iɕt͡ɕe̯i t̪ar at̪ma utʰbe
s̪ei s̪ɔbɔ ont͡ɕɔl̪e d͡zekʰan̪e bl̪es̪tɔ
maŋs̪ɔmukt̪ɔ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ biɕrame।
eta ki apn̪i ɕun̪et͡ɕʰen̪ he b̤art̪ie̯ d͡zubrad͡ʑ
mɔn̪er it͡ɕt͡ɕʰae̯ s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ od͡ʑnɔt̪a at͡ɕʰe
kɔোn̪ɔti t̪ɔোmar kɔʂter d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ d̪ie̯et͡ɕʰe od̪ɽiɕd͡zɔ he̯e ɡet͡ɕʰe amar ord͡ʑun̪
ord͡ʑun̪।
d͡ʑ̤amel̪a o od͡ʑnɔt̪a kete ɡet͡ɕʰe al̪ো
amar kat͡ɕʰe es̪et͡ɕʰe t̪ɔোmar on̪uɡɔrɔhe prɔb̤u
ekʰɔn̪ɔ ami ki s̪t̪ʰir amar s̪ɔn̪d̪ehɔ d̪ur he̯ɔ
t̪ɔোmar kɔt̪ʰamɔt̪ɔ ami t̪ai kɔrɔbɔ
s̪ɔnd͡ʑe̯ɔ।
eib̤abe ami kɽiʂner kɔruname̯ɔ bani s̪ɔŋɡɔrɔhɔ kɔrɔl̪am he amar rad͡ʑa
eib̤abe ami ei d͡ʑnan̪i ebɔŋ aɕt͡ɕɔrd͡zɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ d͡ʑin̪is̪ti hɽid̪e̯er rɔোmant͡ɕer s̪at̪ʰe bɔl̪et͡ɕʰi
mɔhan̪ bd͡zas̪er ɕikʂɔnie̯ l̪ekʰar mad̪̤d͡zɔme kib̤abe kɽiʂner at̪make d͡ʑan̪a d͡zae̯
d͡zɔোɡɔ d͡zɔোɡer prɔb̤u hɔt͡ɕt͡ɕʰe। t̪ai ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔ s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔ d̪ekʰan̪ো he̯ɔ
ebɔŋ hd͡zɔ̃ d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ ami abar s̪mɔrɔnɔ kɔri he prɔb̤u amar rad͡ʑa
al̪োt͡ɕɔn̪ae̯ ord͡ʑun̪ ebɔŋ iɕbɔrɔ ebɔŋ ei s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ pɔbit̪rɔ s̪tren̪
mɔhan̪ amar an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ ami s̪ei d͡ʑɔ̃kɔd͡ʑɔmɔkɔ pas̪iŋ bɔkt̪ɽit̪a
hɔrir d̪ɽiɕd͡zɔman̪ ebɔŋ s̪ɔrɔl̪ɔ pɔৌ̃t͡ʃʰanোrɔ mɔt̪ɔ kɔোn̪ɔ d͡ʑihba n̪ei
amar bis̪me̯ɔ ebɔŋ amar b̤al̪bas̪a ebɔŋ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ he t̪irɔn̪d̪ad͡ʑrad͡ʑɔput̪rɔ s̪ɔbɔ ɕil̪abɽiʂti
he d͡zɔোɡer prɔb̤u kɽiʂnɔ obɔɕd͡zi bd͡zɔrt̪ʰɔ hɔbe n̪a
aɕirbad̪ ebɔŋ bid͡ʑe̯ɔ ebɔŋ ɕɔkt̪i apn̪ar s̪ɔbɔt͡ɕee̯e ɕɔkt̪iɕal̪i d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
ord͡ʑun̪er ei ɡan̪ti kɔোt̪ʰae̯ es̪et͡ɕʰe ebɔŋ t̪in̪i kib̤abe iɕbɔrer s̪at̪ʰe kɔt̪ʰa bɔl̪et͡ɕʰen̪।
 od̪̤d͡zae̯ d̪ie̯e ekʰan̪e ɕeʂ he̯ɔ।
ɕirোn̪am mɔোkʂɔs̪ɔn̪d͡zas̪ɔd͡zɔোɡɔ
ot̪ʰba mukt̪i o t̪d͡zaɡ d̪bara d̪̤ɔrmer bi
b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɡit̪a।




# kit͡ɕʰu pun̪rabɽit̪t̪imul̪ɔkɔ l̪ain̪ ekʰan̪e bad̪ d̪eoe̯a he̯et͡ɕʰe।

# bojd̪ik d̪̤ɔrmer prɔd͡zukt̪iɡɔt̪ɔ bakd͡zaŋɕɔ।

# ei pd͡zas̪ed͡ʑtir purোtai ot̪d͡zɔn̪t̪ɔ d͡ʑɔɽit̪ ebɔŋ ren̪dar kɔra kɔtʰin̪।

# ami mɔn̪e kɔri s̪aŋkʰd͡zan̪ɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ d͡zɔোɡin̪an̪ke ekʰan̪e ort̪ʰe s̪t̪ʰan̪an̪t̪ɔrɔ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe।

# ami ekʰan̪e n̪irb̤ul̪t̪a n̪ie̯e s̪ɔn̪d̪ihan̪।

# s̪urd͡zer ekti n̪am।

# ɸɔl̪er akaŋkʂa t͡ɕʰaɽai।

# ort̪ʰat̪ an̪ɔn̪d̪ɔ ebɔŋ d̪uঃkʰɔ s̪aɸɔl̪d͡zɔ ebɔŋ bd͡zɔrt̪ʰɔt̪a t̪ap ebɔŋ tʰan̪da&।

# ort̪ʰat̪ ɕɔrir।

# s̪ɔŋs̪kɽit̪e at̪mɔn̪er d̪biɡun ort̪ʰɔ n̪ie̯e ei n̪atɔkɔti re̯et͡ɕʰe।

# t̪ai as̪ɔl̪ɔ।

# n̪imn̪ɔ ebɔŋ ɕe̯ɔt̪an̪ prɔkɽit̪ir prani।

# kɽiʂnɔ।

# ami ekʰan̪e d͡ʑɔn̪ɔmɔ pɔɽi d͡ʑɔn̪mɔ d͡ʑara n̪abe̯ɔs̪ɔ

# ami ekʰan̪e s̪ɔŋs̪kɽit̪ patʰer d̪ɔɕɔti l̪ain̪ bat̪il̪ kɔret͡ɕʰi kit͡ɕʰu bed̪an̪t̪ɔbad̪ir ekti n̪iঃs̪ɔn̪d̪ehe in̪tarɔpɔোl̪eɕɔn̪ɔ his̪abe

# ekʰan̪e s̪ɔŋs̪kɽit̪ kɔbit̪ati ɕojl̪i ebɔŋ pɔd̪d̪̤ɔt̪ir ekti ut͡ɕt͡ɕɔt̪ae̯ utʰe ɡet͡ɕʰe d͡za ami mitar pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪er mad̪̤d͡zɔme t͡ɕihn̪it̪ kɔrar t͡ɕeʂta kɔret͡ɕʰi।

# ohin̪s̪a।

# omɔrɔt̪ber omɽit̪।

# d̪d͡zɔ d͡ʑap bɔl̪a he̯ɔ।

# s̪ɔŋs̪kɽit̪ ɕɔbd̪er d͡zɔৌɡik rup।

# kɔmɔl̪ɔpɔt̪rakʂɔ

# eɡul̪ো s̪ɔbi hin̪d̪u pd͡zan̪t̪ʰie̯n̪er ojɕbɔrik ba d̪ebikɽit̪ ad̪eɕ।

# t̪ɔোmake ob̤in̪ɔn̪d̪ɔn̪ɔ iɕbɔrer iɕbɔrɔ d̪e̯a kɔrun̪

# bat̪as̪।

# on̪pekʂa s̪ɔmpɔrke ũki d̪it͡ɕt͡ɕʰen̪ n̪a।

# mɔhab̤art̪er kɔl̪ɔkat̪a s̪ɔŋs̪kɔrɔne ei t̪in̪ti prarɔmb̤ik l̪ain̪ re̯et͡ɕʰe।

# eti hɔl̪ɔ kʂet̪rɔkʂet̪rɔd͡ʑnan̪e̯ɔোd͡ʑɔn̪ɔn̪ɔ d͡zɔt̪ɔ t̪ɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔn̪ɔ mat̪an̪ mamer n̪ikɔtɔt̪ɔmɔ s̪ɔmb̤abd͡zɔ s̪ɔŋs̪kɔrɔnɔ।

# ami ekʰan̪e s̪ɔŋs̪kɽit̪er d̪uti pɔŋkt̪i bad̪ d̪it͡ɕt͡ɕʰi s̪pɔʂtɔt̪i kit͡ɕʰu bed̪an̪t̪ɔbad̪i d̪bara prɔt̪d͡zɔkʂɔ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe।

# ɡɔrb̤aɕe̯ɔ।

# ami ekʰan̪e s̪ɔŋs̪kɽit̪ ɕl̪ɔোkɔɡul̪i bibet͡ɕn̪a kɔri n̪a d͡zeɡul̪i kit͡ɕʰuta obad̪̤e ren̪dar kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe bed̪er kɔrt̪ɽit̪ber upɔrɔ akrɔmɔnɔ miɦ deb̤is̪er s̪at̪ʰe t̪ɔbe ekti s̪un̪d̪ɔrɔ l̪irikd͡zal̪ pɔrbɔ ekti n̪ɔt̪un̪ dumurer upma ɡat͡ɕʰ।

# ami ekʰan̪e ekti ae̯at̪ bad̪ d̪it͡ɕt͡ɕʰi s̪pɔʂtɔt̪i in̪tarɔpɔোl̪eted।

# os̪urad̪er ami miɦ deb̤is̪er s̪at̪ʰe d̪ɔɕɔti s̪ɔmapt̪i ɕl̪ɔোkɔ bad̪ d̪it͡ɕt͡ɕʰi।

# rakʂɔs̪ɔ ebɔŋ d͡zɔkʂɔra murt̪ibihin̪ kin̪t̪u mɔhan̪ ɕɔkt̪i upɔhar ebɔŋ s̪ɔৌn̪d̪ɔrd͡zer kɔৌt̪ukpurnɔ prani eki s̪ɔme̯e s̪ɔৌmd͡zɔro।

# era d̪uʂtɔ bit͡ɕɔrɔnɔkari b̤ut̪er at̪ma।

# ie̯at̪ae̯amɔn̪ɔ rat̪er prɔhɔrer pɔreo d͡ze kʰabar t̪ʰake। b̤art̪e eti s̪ɔmb̤ɔbɔt̪ɔ kʰarap he̯e d͡zabe।

# ami s̪ɔmapt̪i ɕl̪ɔোkɔɡul̪i bad̪ d̪it͡ɕt͡ɕʰi ot̪d͡zɔn̪t̪ɔ s̪ɔn̪d̪ehɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔkɔ s̪ɔt̪d͡zɔt̪a his̪abe।











ben̪ami d̪bara b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪ar prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ ibuker s̪ɔmapt̪i

*** ei prɔkɔl̪per s̪ɔmapt̪i ɡuten̪barɡɔ ibuk d̪d͡zɔ b̤ɔɡɔbɔd̪ɔɡit̪a ei ɸail̪tir n̪am ba hoe̯a ut͡ɕit̪ *****
eti ebɔŋ bib̤in̪n̪ɔ ɸɔrɔmd͡zater s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ s̪ɔŋɕl̪iʂtɔ ɸail̪ et̪e paoe̯a d͡zabe
///////

prɔd͡zɔোd͡ʑɔn̪a kɔret͡ɕʰen̪ d͡ʑes̪i bae̯ars̪ɔ। al̪ hain̪es̪er eit͡ɕtiemel̪ s̪ɔŋs̪kɔrɔnɔ।

hal̪n̪aɡad̪ kɔra s̪ɔŋs̪kɔrɔnɔɡul̪i purbɔbɔrt̪i s̪ɔŋs̪kɔrɔnɔɡul̪ike prɔt̪is̪t̪ʰapɔn̪ɔ kɔrɔbepurɔn̪ɔো s̪ɔŋs̪kɔrɔnɔɡul̪i৷
n̪am pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔra hɔbe।

pabl̪ik dɔোmein̪ mud̪rɔnɔ s̪ɔŋs̪kɔrɔnɔ t̪ʰeke kad͡ʑ t̪ojri kɔra man̪e d͡ze n̪a
ei kad͡ʑɡul̪it̪e ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ markin̪ d͡zukt̪ɔraʂtrer kɔpiraiter mal̪ik t̪ai ɸaun̪deɕɔn̪ɔ
ebɔŋ apn̪i eti markin̪ d͡zukt̪ɔraʂtre on̪ul̪ipi ebɔŋ bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔrɔt̪e paren̪
on̪umt̪i ebɔŋ kɔpirait re̯d͡zal̪ti pɔriɕোd̪̤ɔ t͡ɕʰaɽai। biɕeʂ n̪ie̯ɔmɔ
ei l̪ais̪en̪s̪er oŋɕɔ bd͡zɔbɔharer s̪ad̪̤arɔnɔ ɕɔrt̪abl̪it̪e ul̪l̪ekʰ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ abed̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔrun̪
prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑɡul̪ike on̪ul̪ipi kɔra ebɔŋ bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔra
prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem d̪̤arna ebɔŋ tredmarkɔ rɔkʂa kɔrun̪। prɔkɔl̪pɔ
ɡuten̪barɡɔ ekti n̪ibɔn̪d̪̤it̪ tredmarkɔ ebɔŋ apn̪i d͡zɔd̪i bd͡zɔbɔhar n̪ao kɔrɔt̪e paren̪
ibukɡul̪ir d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ t͡ɕard͡ʑɔ kɔrun̪ d͡zɔd̪i n̪a apn̪i n̪ird̪iʂtɔ on̪umt̪i pan̪। apn̪i d͡zɔd̪i
ei ibuker prɔt̪il̪ipir d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kit͡ɕʰu t͡ɕard͡ʑɔ kɔrɔben̪ n̪a s̪at̪ʰe men̪e
n̪ie̯ɔmɔ kʰub s̪ɔhɔd͡ʑɔ। apn̪i prae̯ kɔোn̪ɔ ud̪d̪eɕd͡ze ei ibuk bd͡zɔbɔhar kɔrɔt̪e paren̪
d͡zemɔn̪ɔ derib̤etib̤ kad͡ʑ t̪ojri ripোrtɔ kɔrmɔkʂɔmɔt̪a ebɔŋ
ɡɔbeʂna s̪eɡul̪ike s̪ɔŋɕɔোd̪̤ɔn̪ɔ kɔra d͡zet̪e pare ebɔŋ mud̪rit̪ kɔre d̪eoe̯a d͡zet̪e pareapn̪i kɔrɔt̪e paren̪
pabl̪ik dɔোmein̪ ibuk s̪ɔhɔ kard͡zɔt̪ɔ kit͡ɕʰu। pun̪ɔrbɔn̪tɔn̪ɔ hɔl̪ɔ
tredmarkɔ l̪ais̪en̪s̪ɔ s̪apekʂe biɕeʂ kɔre banid͡ʑd͡zik
pun̪ɔrbɔn̪tɔn̪ɔ



*** ɕuru s̪ɔmpurnɔ l̪ais̪en̪s̪ɔ ***

s̪ɔmpurnɔ prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ l̪ais̪en̪s̪ɔ
apn̪i ei kad͡ʑti bit̪ɔrɔnɔ ba bd͡zɔbɔhar kɔrar aɡe d̪e̯a kɔre eti pɔɽun̪

prɔোd͡ʑekter s̪urɔkʂar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem bin̪amul̪d͡ze prɔt͡ɕarer miɕɔn̪ɔ
ei kad͡ʑti bd͡zɔbɔhar kɔre ba bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔre il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑer bit̪ɔrɔnɔ
ot̪ʰba on̪d͡zɔ kɔোn̪ɔ kad͡ʑ d͡ze kɔোn̪ɔ upae̯e prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɕɔbd̪er s̪at̪ʰe d͡zukt̪ɔ
ɡuten̪barɡɔ apn̪i s̪ɔmpurnɔ prɔkɔl̪per s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ ɕɔrt̪abl̪i men̪e t͡ɕɔl̪ɔt̪e s̪ɔmmɔt̪ɔ hɔn̪ɔ
 l̪ais̪en̪s̪ɔ ei ɸail̪er s̪at̪ʰe ba on̪l̪ain̪e upɔl̪ɔbd̪̤ɔ
/


od̪̤d͡zae̯ bd͡zɔbɔharer s̪ad̪̤arɔnɔ ɕɔrt̪ad̪i ebɔŋ pun̪ɔঃbɔn̪tɔn̪ɔ prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem
il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ

 ei prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiemer d͡zekোn̪ɔো oŋɕɔ pɔɽe ba bd͡zɔbɔhar kɔre
il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ apn̪i iŋɡit̪ kɔren̪ d͡ze apn̪i pɔɽet͡ɕʰen̪ bud͡ʑ̤et͡ɕʰen̪ s̪ɔmmɔt̪ɔ he̯et͡ɕʰen̪
ebɔŋ ei l̪ais̪en̪s̪ɔ ebɔŋ bɔৌd̪d̪̤ik s̪ɔmpɔt̪t̪ir s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ ɕɔrt̪ɔ s̪bikar kɔrun̪৷
tredmarkɔ/kɔpirait t͡ɕukt̪i। rad͡ʑi n̪a hɔl̪e s̪ɔbɔ man̪t̪e hɔbe
ei t͡ɕukt̪ir ɕɔrt̪abl̪i apn̪ake obɔɕd͡zi bd͡zɔbɔhar bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe ebɔŋ ɸirie̯e d̪it̪e hɔbe ba d̪̤bɔŋs̪ɔ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe
prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑer s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ kɔpi apn̪ar d̪ɔkʰɔl̪e।
apn̪i d͡zɔd̪i ekti prɔkɔl̪per on̪ul̪ipi ba o্d͡zaks̪es̪ paoe̯ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ekti ɸi prɔd̪an̪ kɔren̪
ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ ebɔŋ apn̪i abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ hɔt̪e rad͡ʑi n̪ɔn̪ɔ
ei t͡ɕukt̪ir ɕɔrt̪abl̪i apn̪i bd͡zɔkt̪ir kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke ort̪ʰɔ ɸerɔt̪ɔ pet̪e paren̪ ba
s̪ɔt̪t̪a d͡zake apn̪i on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ e n̪ird̪̤arit̪ his̪abe ɸi prɔd̪an̪ kɔret͡ɕʰen̪।

bi prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ ekti n̪ibɔn̪d̪̤it̪ tredmarkɔ। eta ɕud̪̤umat̪rɔ hɔt̪e pare
kɔোn̪ɔো il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑer s̪at̪ʰe bd͡zɔbɔhar kɔra ba s̪ɔŋɕl̪iʂtɔ bd͡zɔkt̪id̪er d̪bara
ei t͡ɕukt̪ir ɕɔrt̪abl̪i d̪bara abɔd̪d̪̤ɔ hɔt̪e s̪ɔmmɔt̪ɔ। ekti ke̯ek at͡ɕʰe
d͡ze d͡ʑin̪is̪ɡul̪i apn̪i beɕirb̤aɡ prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑer s̪at̪ʰe kɔrɔt̪e paren̪
emɔn̪ɔki ei t͡ɕukt̪ir s̪ɔmpurnɔ ɕɔrt̪abl̪i men̪e n̪a n̪ie̯eo। d̪ekʰa
on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ n̪it͡ɕe। apn̪i prɔd͡ʑekter s̪at̪ʰe on̪ek kit͡ɕʰu kɔrɔt̪e paren̪
ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ kɔre d͡zɔd̪i apn̪i ei t͡ɕukt̪ir ɕɔrt̪abl̪i on̪us̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔren̪
ebɔŋ prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪iker bin̪amul̪d͡ze b̤ɔbiʂd͡zɔt̪er o্d͡zaks̪es̪ s̪ɔŋrɔkʂɔnɔ kɔrɔt̪e s̪ɔhae̯t̪a kɔrun̪
kad͡ʑ kɔre n̪it͡ɕe on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ d̪ekʰun̪।

 prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ s̪ahit̪d͡zɔ s̪ɔŋrɔkʂɔnaɡar ɸaun̪deɕɔn̪ɔ ɸaun̪deɕɔn̪ɔ
ot̪ʰba prɔkɔl̪per s̪ɔŋɡɔrɔhe ekti s̪ɔŋkɔl̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔpiraiter mal̪ik
ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ kɔre। prae̯ s̪ɔbɔ s̪bɔt̪ɔn̪t̪rɔ kad͡ʑ
s̪ɔŋɡɔrɔhɔ markin̪ d͡zukt̪ɔraʂtre pabl̪ik dɔোmen̪e at͡ɕʰe d͡zɔd̪i ekta
bd͡zɔkt̪iɡɔt̪ɔ kad͡ʑ markin̪ d͡zukt̪ɔraʂtre pabl̪ik dɔোmen̪e re̯et͡ɕʰe ebɔŋ apn̪i
markin̪ d͡zukt̪ɔraʂtre obɔs̪t̪ʰit̪ amra apn̪ake bad̪̤a d̪eoe̯ar od̪̤ikar d̪abi kɔri n̪a
on̪ul̪ipi kɔra bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔra s̪ɔmpad̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔra prɔd̪ɔrɕɔn̪ɔ kɔra ba derib̤etib̤ t̪ojri kɔra
d͡zɔt̪ɔkʂɔnɔ pɔrd͡zɔn̪t̪ɔ prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡer s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ reɸaren̪s̪ɔ kad͡ʑer upɔrɔ b̤it̪t̪i kɔre kad͡ʑ kɔre
ops̪arɔnɔ kɔra he̯ɔ obɔɕd͡zi amra aɕa kɔri apn̪i prɔkɔl̪pɔti s̪ɔmɔrt̪ʰɔn̪ɔ kɔrɔben̪
ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑe bin̪amul̪d͡ze prɔbeɕad̪̤ikar prɔt͡ɕarer miɕɔn̪ɔ
obad̪̤e ɕee̯ariŋ prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem er ɕɔrt̪abl̪i men̪e kad͡ʑ kɔre
prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem er s̪at̪ʰe d͡zukt̪ɔ rakʰar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ei t͡ɕukt̪i
kad͡ʑ apn̪i s̪ɔhɔd͡ʑei ei t͡ɕukt̪ir ɕɔrt̪abl̪i men̪e t͡ɕɔl̪ɔt̪e paren̪
ei kad͡ʑtike t̪ar s̪ɔŋd͡zukt̪ɔ s̪ɔmpurnɔ prɔkɔl̪per s̪at̪ʰe eki bin̪d͡zas̪e rakʰa
ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem l̪ais̪en̪s̪ɔ d͡zɔkʰɔn̪ɔ apn̪i on̪d͡zɔd̪er s̪at̪ʰe t͡ɕard͡ʑɔ t͡ɕʰaɽai ɕee̯ar kɔren̪।

 apn̪i d͡zekʰan̪e at͡ɕʰen̪ s̪ei d͡ʑae̯ɡar kɔpirait ain̪ɡul̪io n̪ie̯ɔn̪t̪rɔnɔ kɔre৷
apn̪i ei kad͡ʑ d̪ie̯e ki kɔrɔt̪e paren̪ od̪̤ikaŋɕɔ d̪eɕe kɔpirait ain̪ at͡ɕʰe
pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪er ekti d̪̤rubɔkɔ obɔs̪t̪ʰa। apn̪i d͡zɔd̪i markin̪ d͡zukt̪ɔraʂtrer baire t̪ʰaken̪ t̪ɔbe t͡ɕek kɔrun̪
ei t͡ɕukt̪ir ɕɔrt̪abl̪i t͡ɕʰaɽao apn̪ar d̪eɕer ain̪
daun̪ɔl̪ɔোdɔ kɔrar aɡe on̪ul̪ipi kɔra prɔd̪ɔrɕɔn̪ɔ kɔra s̪ɔmpad̪ɔn̪ɔ kɔra bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔra ba
ei kad͡ʑ ba on̪d͡zɔ kɔোn̪ɔ prɔkɔl̪per upɔrɔ b̤it̪t̪i kɔre derib̤etib̤ kad͡ʑ t̪ojri kɔra
ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem kad͡ʑ। ɸaun̪deɕɔn̪ɔ biʂe̯e kɔোn̪ɔ prɔt̪in̪id̪̤it̪bɔ kɔre n̪a
iun̪aiteder baire d͡zekোn̪ɔো d̪eɕe d͡zekোn̪ɔো kad͡ʑer kɔpirait s̪td͡zatas̪
rad͡ʑd͡zɔɡul̪i

i apn̪i prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡer s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ reɸaren̪s̪ɔ mut͡ɕʰe n̪a d̪il̪e

i n̪imn̪ɔl̪ikʰit̪ bakd͡zɔ s̪ɔkrie̯ l̪iŋkɔ s̪ɔhɔ ba on̪d͡zan̪d͡zɔ obil̪ɔmbe
o্d͡zaks̪es̪ s̪ɔmpurnɔ prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem l̪ais̪en̪s̪ɔti obɔɕd͡zi s̪pɔʂtɔb̤abe prɔd̪ɔrɕit̪ hɔbe
d͡zɔkʰɔn̪i kɔোn̪ɔ prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem kad͡ʑer kɔোn̪ɔ on̪ul̪ipi d͡ze kɔোn̪ɔ kad͡ʑ d͡zar upɔrɔ
bakd͡zaŋɕɔ prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ prɔd̪ɔrɕit̪ he̯ɔ ba d͡zar s̪at̪ʰe prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɕɔbd̪ɔɡut͡ɕt͡ɕʰɔ
ɡuten̪barɡɔ d͡zukt̪ɔ o্d͡zaks̪es̪ kɔra prɔd̪ɔrɕit̪ s̪ɔnt͡ɕal̪it̪ d̪ekʰa
on̪ul̪ipi ba bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔra

ei ibukti d͡zekোn̪o d͡ʑae̯ɡae̯ bin̪a kʰɔrɔt͡ɕe ebɔŋ s̪at̪ʰe d͡ze karো bd͡zɔbɔharer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ
prae̯ kɔোn̪ɔ bid̪̤in̪iʂed̪̤ n̪ei। apn̪i eti on̪ul̪ipi eti d̪ure d̪it̪e paren̪ ba
prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ l̪ais̪en̪s̪er ɕɔrt̪abl̪ir od̪̤in̪e eti pun̪rae̯ bd͡zɔbɔhar kɔrun̪ on̪t̪ɔrb̤ukt̪ɔ
ei ibuk s̪ɔhɔ ba on̪l̪ain̪ e

i। d͡zɔd̪i ekti pɽit̪ʰɔkɔ prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ ud̪b̤ut̪ he̯ɔ
pabl̪ik dɔোmein̪ t̪ʰeke eti n̪ird̪eɕ kɔre emɔn̪ɔ ekti bid͡ʑnɔpt̪i n̪ei
kɔpirait d̪̤arker on̪umt̪i n̪ie̯e pɔোs̪tɔ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe kad͡ʑti on̪ul̪ipi kɔra d͡zet̪e pare
ebɔŋ kɔোn̪ɔো ɸi prɔd̪an̪ t͡ɕʰaɽai markin̪ d͡zukt̪ɔraʂtre d͡ze kauke bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe
ba t͡ɕard͡ʑɔ। apn̪i d͡zɔd̪i ekti kad͡ʑer pun̪rae̯ bit̪ɔrɔnɔ ba o্d͡zaks̪es̪ prɔd̪an̪ kɔren̪
prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ ɕɔbd̪ɔɡut͡ɕt͡ɕʰer s̪at̪ʰe d͡zukt̪ɔ ba prɔd̪ɔrɕit̪ hɔt͡ɕt͡ɕʰe
kad͡ʑ apn̪ake obɔɕd͡zi on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ er pre̯ɔোd͡ʑɔn̪ie̯t̪aɡul̪i men̪e t͡ɕɔl̪ɔt̪e hɔbe
 er mad̪̤d͡zɔme ba kad͡ʑer bd͡zɔbɔharer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ on̪umt̪i prapt̪ɔ kɔrun̪ ebɔŋ
prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem tredmarkɔ on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ ba


i। d͡zɔd̪i ekti pɽit̪ʰɔkɔ prɔkɔl̪pɔ il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ pɔোs̪tɔ kɔra he̯ɔ
kɔpirait d̪̤arker on̪umt̪i n̪ie̯e apn̪ar bd͡zɔbɔhar ebɔŋ bit̪ɔrɔnɔ
ub̤e̯ɔ on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ t̪ʰeke ebɔŋ d͡zekোn̪ɔো ot̪irikt̪ɔ men̪e t͡ɕɔl̪ɔt̪e hɔbe
kɔpirait d̪̤arɔkɔ d̪bara arোpit̪ ɕɔrt̪abl̪i। ot̪irikt̪ɔ ɕɔrt̪abl̪i l̪iŋkɔ kɔra hɔbe
er s̪at̪ʰe pɔোs̪tɔ kɔra s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ kad͡ʑer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem l̪ais̪en̪s̪e
ei kad͡ʑer ɕurut̪e paoe̯a kɔpirait d̪̤arker on̪umt̪i।

 s̪ɔmpurnɔ prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem an̪l̪iŋkɔ ba bit͡ɕt͡ɕʰin̪n̪ɔ ba ops̪arɔnɔ kɔrɔben̪ n̪a
ei kad͡ʑ t̪ʰeke l̪ais̪en̪s̪er ɕɔrt̪abl̪i ba er ekti oŋɕɔ s̪ɔmbɔl̪it̪ kɔোn̪ɔো ɸail̪
kad͡ʑ ba prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem er s̪at̪ʰe d͡zukt̪ɔ on̪d͡zɔ kɔোn̪ɔ kad͡ʑ।

i। eti on̪ul̪ipi prɔd̪ɔrɕɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔmpad̪ɔn̪ɔ bit̪ɔrɔnɔ ba pun̪rae̯ bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔrɔben̪ n̪a
il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ ba ei il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑer kɔোn̪ɔো oŋɕɔ t͡ɕʰaɽa
er s̪at̪ʰe on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ e ul̪l̪ikʰit̪ bakd͡zɔti biɕiʂtɔb̤abe prɔd̪ɔrɕɔn̪ɔ kɔra
s̪ɔkrie̯ l̪iŋkɔ ba prɔkɔl̪per s̪ɔmpurnɔ ɕɔrt̪abl̪i obil̪ɔmbe o্d͡zaks̪es̪
ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem l̪ais̪en̪s̪ɔ।

i apn̪i ei kad͡ʑtike d͡zekোn̪ɔো bain̪arit̪e rupan̪t̪ɔrɔ ebɔŋ bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔrɔt̪e paren̪
s̪ɔŋkut͡ɕit̪ markɔ ap mal̪ikan̪ahin̪ ba mal̪ikan̪ad̪̤in̪ ɸɔrmɔ d͡ze kɔোn̪o s̪ɔhɔ
ɕɔbd̪ɔ prɔkrie̯akɔrɔnɔ ba haiparteks̪ɔtɔ ɸɔrmɔ। d͡zaihɔোkɔ d͡zɔd̪i apn̪i o্d͡zaks̪es̪ prɔd̪an̪ kɔren̪ ba
ekti prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem kad͡ʑer on̪ul̪ipi on̪d͡zɔ ekti ɸɔrɔmd͡zate bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔrun̪
 ba oɸis̪ie̯al̪ s̪ɔŋs̪kɔrɔne bd͡zɔbɔhɽit̪ on̪d͡zɔ bin̪d͡zas̪
oɸis̪ie̯al̪ prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem oe̯eb s̪aite pɔোs̪tɔ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe 
bd͡zɔbɔharkarike kɔোn̪ɔো ot̪irikt̪ɔ kʰɔrɔt͡ɕɔ ɸi ba kʰɔrɔt͡ɕɔ t͡ɕʰaɽai apn̪ake obɔɕd͡zi ekti prɔd̪an̪ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe
on̪ul̪ipi ekti on̪ul̪ipi rɔpt̪an̪i kɔrar ekti upae̯ ba ekti on̪ul̪ipi paoe̯ar ekti upae̯
er as̪ɔl̪ɔ pl̪ein̪ b̤d͡zan̪il̪a ba on̪d͡zɔ kad͡ʑer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ on̪urোd̪̤ɔ
ɸɔrmɔ d͡zekোn̪ɔো bikɔl̪pɔ bin̪d͡zas̪e obɔɕd͡zi s̪ɔmpurnɔ on̪t̪ɔrb̤ukt̪ɔ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe
on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ e ul̪l̪ekʰit̪ l̪ais̪en̪s̪ɔ।

 o্d͡zaks̪es̪ d̪ekʰar prɔd̪ɔrɕɔn̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kɔোn̪o ɸi t͡ɕard͡ʑɔ kɔrɔben̪ n̪a
ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem prɔkɔl̪per kad͡ʑ s̪ɔmpad̪ɔn̪ɔ on̪ul̪ipi ba bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔra
d͡zɔd̪i n̪a apn̪i on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ ba men̪e t͡ɕɔl̪en̪।

 apn̪i on̪ul̪ipi ba prɔd̪an̪er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ekti d͡zukt̪is̪ɔŋɡɔt̪ɔ ɸi t͡ɕard͡ʑɔ kɔrɔt̪e paren̪
prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑɡul̪it̪e o্d͡zaks̪es̪ ba bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔra
d͡ze

 apn̪i prapt̪ɔ mɔোtɔ l̪ab̤er re̯d͡zal̪ti ɸi prɔd̪an̪ kɔren̪
prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem kad͡ʑer bd͡zɔbɔhar pɔd̪d̪̤ɔt̪i bd͡zɔbɔhar kɔre ɡɔnɔn̪a kɔra he̯ɔ
apn̪i it̪imɔd̪̤d͡zei apn̪ar prɔd͡zɔোd͡ʑd͡zɔ kɔrɔ ɡɔnɔn̪a kɔrɔt̪e bd͡zɔbɔhar kɔrɔt͡ɕʰen̪। ɸi hɔl̪ɔ
prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem tredmarker mal̪iker kat͡ɕʰe ɽini kin̪t̪u t̪in̪i
ei on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪er od̪̤in̪e re̯d͡zal̪ti d̪an̪ kɔrɔt̪e s̪ɔmmɔt̪ɔ he̯et͡ɕʰe৷
prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ s̪ahit̪d͡zɔ s̪ɔŋrɔkʂɔnaɡar ɸaun̪deɕɔn̪ɔ। re̯d͡zal̪ti pemen̪tɔ
prɔt̪iti t̪arikʰer d̪in̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze ort̪ʰɔ prɔd̪an̪ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe d͡ze t̪arikʰe apn̪i
apn̪ar pɔrd͡zae̯ɔkrɔmik td͡zaks̪ɔ prɔs̪t̪ut̪ kɔrun̪ ba ain̪ib̤abe prɔs̪t̪ut̪ kɔrɔt̪e hɔbe
ritarn̪ɔ re̯d͡zal̪ti pemen̪tɔ s̪pɔʂtɔb̤abe t͡ɕihn̪it̪ kɔra ut͡ɕit̪ d͡zemɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ
prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ l̪itarari arkaib̤ ɸaun̪deɕn̪e patʰan̪ো he̯et͡ɕʰe
d̪̤ara e ul̪l̪ekʰit̪ tʰikan̪a on̪ud̪an̪ s̪ɔmpɔrke t̪ɔt̪ʰd͡zɔ
prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ s̪ahit̪d͡zɔ s̪ɔŋrɔkʂɔnaɡar ɸaun̪deɕɔn̪ɔ।

 apn̪i ekɔd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ bd͡zɔbɔharkarir d̪bara prɔd̪ɔt̪t̪ɔ d͡zekোn̪ɔ ort̪ʰer s̪ɔmpurnɔ ɸerɔt̪ɔ prɔd̪an̪ kɔren̪ d͡zin̪i bid͡ʑnɔpt̪i d̪en̪
apn̪i prapt̪ir d̪in̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze l̪ikʰit̪b̤abe ba imeil̪er mad̪̤d͡zɔme
s̪ɔmpurnɔ prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiemer ɕɔrt̪e s̪ɔmmɔt̪ɔ n̪e̯ɔ
l̪ais̪en̪s̪ɔ apn̪i ei d̪̤ɔrɔn̪er ekti bd͡zɔbɔharkarir pre̯ɔোd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ hɔbe ɸerɔt̪ɔ ba
ekti b̤ɔৌt̪ɔ ​​mad̪̤d͡zɔme abiʂtɔ kad͡ʑer s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ kɔpi d̪̤bɔŋs̪ɔ
ebɔŋ er on̪d͡zan̪d͡zɔ on̪ul̪ipiɡul̪ir s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ bd͡zɔbɔhar ebɔŋ s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ o্d͡zaks̪es̪ bɔn̪d̪̤ɔ kɔrun̪৷
prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem kad͡ʑ kɔre।

 apn̪i on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ on̪ud͡zae̯i d͡ze kɔোn̪ɔো ekti s̪ɔmpurnɔ ɸerɔt̪ɔ prɔd̪an̪ kɔren̪
ekti kad͡ʑ ba ekti prɔt̪is̪t̪ʰapɔn̪ɔ kɔpi d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ort̪ʰɔ prɔd̪an̪ d͡zɔd̪i ekti t̪ruti
il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ abiʂkɽit̪ he̯ɔ ebɔŋ d̪in̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze apn̪ake ripোrtɔ kɔra he̯ɔ
kad͡ʑer prapt̪i।

 apn̪i bin̪amul̪d͡ze ei t͡ɕukt̪ir on̪d͡zan̪d͡zɔ ɕɔrt̪abl̪i men̪e t͡ɕɔl̪en̪
prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem kad͡ʑer bit̪ɔrɔnɔ।

 apn̪i d͡zɔd̪i ekti ɸi t͡ɕard͡ʑɔ kɔrɔt̪e t͡ɕan̪ ba ekti prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔrɔt̪e t͡ɕan̪
il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ ba kad͡ʑer ɡɔrup s̪et kɔra t̪ʰeke b̤in̪n̪ɔ pɔd̪e
ei t͡ɕukt̪it̪e apn̪ake obɔɕd͡zi l̪ikʰit̪b̤abe on̪umt̪i n̪it̪e hɔbe
prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ l̪itarari arkaib̤ ɸaun̪deɕɔn̪ɔ ebɔŋ maikel̪ ub̤e̯i
hartɔ prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem tredmarker mal̪ik। d͡zɔোɡad͡zোɡɔ
n̪it͡ɕer od̪̤d͡zae̯ e ul̪l̪ikʰit̪ b̤it̪t̪i।

eɸ

 prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔ s̪bet͡ɕt͡ɕʰas̪ebɔkɔ ebɔŋ kɔrmɔt͡ɕarira d͡zɔt̪ʰeʂtɔ bd͡ze̯ɔ kɔre
s̪ɔn̪akt̪ɔkɔrɔnɔ kɔpirait ɡɔbeʂna prɔt̪il̪ipi ebɔŋ pruɸrid kɔrar prɔt͡ɕeʂta
pabl̪ik dɔোmein̪ prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem t̪ojrit̪e kad͡ʑ kɔre
s̪ɔŋɡɔrɔhɔ ei prɔt͡ɕeʂta s̪ɔt̪t̪beo prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik
kad͡ʑ kɔre ebɔŋ d͡ze mad̪̤d͡zɔmɔtit̪e s̪eɡul̪i s̪ɔŋrɔkʂɔnɔ kɔra d͡zet̪e pare t̪at̪e t̪ʰakt̪e pare
t̪ruti d͡zemɔn̪ɔ kin̪t̪u s̪imabɔd̪d̪̤ɔ n̪e̯ɔ os̪ɔmpurnɔ b̤ul̪ ba
d̪uʂit̪ deta tran̪s̪ɔkripɔɕɔn̪ɔ t̪ruti ekti kɔpirait ba on̪d͡zan̪d͡zɔ bud̪d̪̤id͡ʑibi
s̪ɔmpɔt̪t̪i l̪ɔŋ̤ɡ̤ɔn̪ɔ ekti t̪rutipurnɔ ba kʂɔt̪iɡɔrɔs̪t̪ɔ dis̪kɔ ba on̪d͡zan̪d͡zɔ mad̪̤d͡zɔmɔ kɔ
kɔmpiutar b̤airas̪ ba kɔmpiutar kɔোdɔ d͡za kʂɔt̪i kɔre ba pɔɽɔt̪e pare n̪a
apn̪ar s̪ɔrɔnd͡ʑam।

। s̪imit̪ oe̯d͡zaren̪ti kʂɔt̪ir os̪bikɽit̪i od̪̤ikar bd͡zɔt̪it̪
prɔt̪is̪t̪ʰapɔn̪ɔ ba ɸerɔt̪ɔ on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ prɔkɔl̪pe bɔrnit̪
ɡuten̪barɡɔ l̪itarari arkaib̤ ɸaun̪deɕɔn̪ɔ prɔkɔl̪per mal̪ik
 tredmarkɔ ebɔŋ on̪d͡zɔ kɔোn̪ɔো pɔkʂɔ ekti prɔkɔl̪pɔ bit̪ɔrɔnɔ kɔrɔt͡ɕʰe
ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem ei t͡ɕukt̪ir od̪̤in̪e il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑ s̪ɔbɔ os̪bikar
ain̪i s̪ɔhɔ kʂɔt̪i kʰɔrɔt͡ɕɔ ebɔŋ kʰɔrɔt͡ɕer d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ apn̪ar d̪ae̯ɔbɔd̪d̪̤ɔt̪a
ɸi apn̪i s̪ɔmmɔt̪ɔ d͡ze apn̪ar obɔhel̪ar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ kɔোn̪ɔ prɔt̪ikar n̪ei kɔtʰɔোrɔ
d̪ae̯ɔbɔd̪d̪̤ɔt̪a oe̯d͡zaren̪ti l̪ɔŋ̤ɡ̤ɔn̪ɔ ba t͡ɕukt̪i l̪ɔŋ̤ɡ̤ɔn̪ɔ eɡul̪i bd͡zɔt̪it̪
 e prɔd̪an̪ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe। apn̪i d͡ze ɸaun̪deɕɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔmmɔt̪ɔ hɔn̪ɔ
tredmarker mal̪ik ebɔŋ ei t͡ɕukt̪ir od̪̤in̪e kɔোn̪ɔো bit̪ɔrɔnɔkari hɔbe n̪a
prɔkɽit̪ prɔt̪d͡zɔkʂɔ pɔrɔোkʂɔ ɸɔl̪ɔs̪bɔrup ɕas̪t̪imul̪ɔkɔ ba er d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ apn̪ar kat͡ɕʰe d̪ae̯ɔbɔd̪d̪̤ɔ
apn̪i ei d̪̤ɔrɔn̪er s̪ɔmb̤abn̪ar n̪ɔোtiɕ d̪il̪eo an̪uʂɔŋɡik kʂe̯ɔkʂɔt̪i
kʂɔt̪i।

 prɔt̪is̪t̪ʰapɔn̪ɔ ba ɸert̪er s̪imit̪ od̪̤ikar d͡zɔd̪i apn̪i ekti abiʂkar kɔren̪
ei il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑer t̪ruti prapt̪ir d̪in̪er mɔd̪̤d͡ze apn̪i kɔrɔt̪e paren̪
ekti patʰan̪োrɔ mad̪̤d͡zɔme apn̪i etir d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ ort̪ʰɔ prɔd̪an̪ kɔret͡ɕʰen̪ d͡zɔd̪i t̪ʰake ɸerɔt̪ɔ pan̪
apn̪i d͡zar kat͡ɕʰ t̪ʰeke kad͡ʑ pee̯et͡ɕʰen̪ t̪ar kat͡ɕʰe l̪ikʰit̪ bd͡zakʰd͡za। apn̪i d͡zɔd̪i
ekti b̤ɔৌt̪ɔ ​​mad̪̤d͡zɔme kad͡ʑ prapt̪ɔ apn̪i mad̪̤d͡zɔmɔ s̪ɔŋɡe ɸerɔt̪ɔ d̪it̪e hɔbe
apn̪ar l̪ikʰit̪ bd͡zakʰd͡za। d͡ze bd͡zɔkt̪i ba s̪ɔt̪t̪a apn̪ake prɔd̪an̪ kɔret͡ɕʰe৷
t̪rutipurnɔ kad͡ʑ ekti pɔribɔrt̪e ekti prɔt̪is̪t̪ʰapɔn̪ɔ on̪ul̪ipi prɔd̪an̪ n̪irbat͡ɕɔn̪ɔ kɔrɔt̪e pare
ɸerɔt̪ɔ apn̪i d͡zɔd̪i il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ikb̤abe kad͡ʑti pee̯e t̪ʰaken̪ t̪ahɔl̪e s̪ei bd͡zɔkt̪i ba s̪ɔt̪t̪a
apn̪ake eti prɔd̪an̪ kɔrar d͡ʑɔn̪d͡zɔ apn̪ake d̪bit̪ie̯ s̪ud͡zোɡɔ d̪it̪e bet͡ɕʰe n̪it̪e pare
ort̪ʰɔ ɸert̪er pɔribɔrt̪e bojd̪d͡zut̪in̪b̤abe kad͡ʑ ɡɔrɔhɔnɔ kɔrun̪। d̪bit̪ie̯ kɔpi hɔl̪e
et͡ɕʰaɽao t̪rutipurnɔ apn̪i aro n̪a kɔre l̪ikʰit̪b̤abe ɸerɔt̪ɔ d̪abi kɔrɔt̪e paren̪
s̪ɔmɔs̪d͡za s̪ɔmad̪̤an̪er s̪ud͡zোɡɔ।

 prɔt̪is̪t̪ʰapɔn̪ɔ ba ɸerɔt̪ɔ d̪eoe̯ar s̪imit̪ od̪̤ikar bd͡zɔt̪it̪
on̪ut͡ɕt͡ɕʰed̪ e ei kad͡ʑti apn̪ake d͡zemn̪i at͡ɕʰe prɔd̪an̪ kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe on̪d͡zɔ kɔোn̪ɔো t͡ɕʰaɽai
d͡ze kɔোn̪ɔো d̪̤ɔrɔn̪er oe̯d͡zaren̪ti prɔkaɕ ba uhd͡zɔ s̪ɔhɔ kin̪t̪u s̪imabɔd̪d̪̤ɔ n̪e̯ɔ
d͡ze kɔোn̪ɔ ud̪d̪eɕd͡ze bɔnikt̪a ba upd͡zukt̪ɔt̪ar oe̯d͡zaren̪ti।

। kit͡ɕʰu rad͡ʑd͡zɔ kit͡ɕʰu uhd͡zɔ d̪abi os̪bikar kɔrar on̪umt̪i d̪ee̯ n̪a
oe̯d͡zaren̪ti ba n̪ird̪iʂtɔ d̪̤ɔrɔner kʂɔt̪ir bɔrd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ ba s̪imabɔd̪d̪̤ɔt̪a।
d͡zɔd̪i ei t͡ɕukt̪it̪e ul̪l̪ekʰ kɔra kɔোn̪ɔো d̪abit̪d͡zaɡ ba s̪imabɔd̪d̪̤ɔt̪a l̪ɔŋ̤ɡ̤ɔn̪ɔ kɔre
ei t͡ɕukt̪ir kʂet̪re raʂtrer ain̪ prɔd͡zɔোd͡ʑd͡zɔ t͡ɕukt̪i hɔbe
d̪bara on̪umোd̪it̪ s̪ɔrbɔোt͡ɕt͡ɕɔ d̪abit̪d͡zaɡ ba s̪imabɔd̪d̪̤ɔt̪a kɔrɔt̪e bd͡zakʰd͡za kɔra he̯et͡ɕʰe
prɔd͡zɔোd͡ʑd͡zɔ raʂtrɔ ain̪। kɔোn̪ɔtir obojd̪̤t̪a ba opre̯ɔোɡɔd͡zɔোɡɔd͡zɔt̪a
ei t͡ɕukt̪ir bid̪̤an̪ obɕiʂtɔ bid̪̤an̪ bat̪il̪ hɔbe n̪a

 kʂɔt̪ipurɔnɔ apn̪i kʂɔt̪ipurɔnɔ d̪it̪e ebɔŋ ɸaun̪deɕɔn̪ɔke d̪̤ɔre rakʰt̪e s̪ɔmmɔt̪ɔ hɔn̪ɔ
tredmarkɔ mal̪ik ɸaun̪deɕn̪er kɔোn̪ɔো ed͡ʑen̪tɔ ba kɔrmɔt͡ɕari d͡ze keu
prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑer on̪ul̪ipi prɔd̪an̪ kɔra
ei t͡ɕukt̪ir s̪at̪ʰe ebɔŋ ut̪pad̪ɔn̪er s̪at̪ʰe d͡zukt̪ɔ d͡ze kɔোn̪ɔো s̪bet͡ɕt͡ɕʰas̪ebɔkɔ
prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem il̪ekɔtrɔn̪ik kad͡ʑer prɔt͡ɕar o bit̪ɔrɔnɔ
ain̪i ɸi s̪ɔhɔ s̪ɔmɔs̪t̪ɔ d̪ae̯ kʰɔrɔt͡ɕɔ ebɔŋ kʰɔrɔt͡ɕɔ t̪ʰeke n̪irihɔ
d͡za apn̪i d͡za kɔren̪ t̪a t̪ʰeke prɔt̪d͡zɔkʂɔ ba pɔrɔোkʂɔb̤abe ud̪b̤ut̪ he̯ɔ
ba ̤ɡ̤ɔtɔt̪e karɔnɔ kɔ eti ba d͡zekোn̪ɔ prɔd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem er bit̪ɔrɔnɔ
kad͡ʑ kʰɔ pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪ɔ pɔribɔrt̪ɔn̪ɔ ba s̪ɔŋd͡zɔোd͡ʑɔn̪ɔ ba mut͡ɕʰe ɸel̪a
prɔোd͡ʑektɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem kad͡ʑ ebɔŋ ɡɔ apn̪ar s̪ɽiʂtɔ kɔোn̪ɔ t̪ruti।


bib̤aɡ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem prɔkɔl̪per miɕɔn̪ɔ s̪ɔmpɔrke t̪ɔt̪ʰd͡zɔ

prɔkɔl̪pɔ ɡuten̪barɡɔtiem er bin̪amul̪d͡ze bit̪ɔrɔner s̪ɔmart̪ʰɔkɔ
kɔmpiutarer bis̪t̪ɽit̪ bojt͡ɕit̪rd͡zɔ d̪bara patʰɔd͡zɔোɡɔd͡zɔ bin̪d͡zas̪e bojd̪d͡zut̪in̪ kad͡ʑ
oprɔt͡ɕɔl̪it̪ puran̪ো mɔd̪̤d͡zɔbe̯ɔs̪i ebɔŋ n̪ɔt̪un̪ kɔmpiutar s̪ɔhɔ। eti bid̪d͡zɔman̪
karɔnɔ ɕɔt̪ɔ ɕɔt̪ɔ s̪bet͡ɕt͡ɕʰas̪ebɔkɔd̪er prɔt͡ɕeʂta ebɔŋ t̪ʰeke on̪ud̪an̪
